Section 0: Ch1-2: Introduction & Key Concepts

學習目標 Learning Objectives

  1. 了解 GAMP 5 第二版與第一版的主要差異，包括新增的 AI/ML、區塊鏈、Agile 及批判性思維指引。
  2. 掌握 GAMP 5 的目的與範圍：保護病患安全、產品品質與數據完整性，適用於全類型 GxP 電腦化系統。
  3. 理解 GAMP 5 不是標準、不是認證體系，而是實務指引；企業不能聲稱「GAMP 認證合規」。
  4. 熟悉五大核心概念：符合預期用途、生命週期方法、可縮放生命週期活動、科學化 QRM、善用供應商參與。
  5. 理解 GAMP 5 與 ICH Q9（QRM）、21 CFR Part 11、EU Annex 11 之關聯，以及在 CDMO 環境中的應用。
  6. 掌握關鍵術語定義：電腦化系統（Computerized System）、CSV、GxP、製程負責人（Process Owner）、QMS 等。

Chapter 1: Introduction — 第一章：導論

1. Introduction

GAMP guidance aims to safeguard patient safety, product quality, and data integrity in the use of GxP computerized systems. It aims to achieve computerized systems that are fit for intended use and meet current regulatory requirements by building upon existing industry good practice in an efficient and effective manner.

GAMP provides practical guidance that:

  • Facilitates the interpretation of regulatory requirements
  • Establishes a common language and terminology
  • Promotes a system life cycle approach based on good practice
  • Clarifies roles and responsibilities

It is not a prescriptive method or a standard, but rather provides pragmatic guidance, approaches, and tools for the practitioner. When applied with expertise and good judgment, this Guide offers a robust, cost-effective approach.

The approach described in this document is designed to be compatible with a wide range of other models, methods, and schemes including:

  • Quality systems standards and certification schemes, such as the ISO 9000 Series
  • ISO 14971: Medical devices – Application of risk management to medical devices
  • Schemes for assessing and improving organization capability and maturity, such as Capability Maturity Model Integration® (CMMI)
  • Software process models such as ISO 12207
  • Iterative and incremental (Agile) software development methods and models
  • Approaches to IT service management, such as ITIL

Where possible, terminology is harmonized with standard international sources such as ICH and ISO. This Guide aims to be fully compatible with the approach described in the ASTM E2500 Standard Guide for Specification, Design, and Verification of Pharmaceutical and Biopharmaceutical Manufacturing Systems and Equipment.

GAMP is an ISPE Community of Practice.

導論解析

核心使命：三重保護

GAMP 5 的存在理由是一個三角形使命：

  • 病患安全（Patient Safety）：數據決策影響治療結果
  • 產品品質（Product Quality）：系統控制製程的每個步驟
  • 數據完整性（Data Integrity）：記錄的真實性與可追溯性

這三者互相依存，缺一不可。

比喻：交通法規還是路況指南？

GAMP 5 更像「駕駛最佳實踐手冊」，而非強制性的《道路交通法》。它告訴你如何開車更安全、更有效率，但各國交通法規（21 CFR Part 11、EU Annex 11）才是你必須遵守的法律。GAMP 5 幫你詮釋這些法規，但不能取代它們。

重要：GAMP 不是標準，不能聲稱「GAMP 認證」

原文明確指出：GAMP 是指引（guides），不是標準（standards）。因此，任何公司、供應商或產品都不適合聲稱自己是「GAMP 認證（GAMP certified）」或「GAMP 合規（GAMP compliant）」。

CDMO 合規聲明應依據 21 CFR Part 11、EU GMP Annex 11 等法規要求。

CDMO 應用場景

在無菌充填 CDMO 中，GAMP 5 所說的「電腦化系統」包括：

  • 充填機的 PLC/SCADA 控制系統
  • LIMS（實驗室資訊管理系統）
  • MES（製造執行系統）
  • ERP（企業資源規劃）
  • BMS（樓宇管理系統，含溫濕度監控）
  • 電子批次記錄（eBPR）

1.1 Rationale for GAMP 5 Second Edition

This Second Edition Guide aims to protect patient safety, product quality, and data integrity by facilitating and encouraging the achievement of computerized systems that are effective, reliable, and of high quality.

While the overall approach, framework, and key concepts remain unchanged, technical content of the Guide has been updated to reflect the increased importance of IT service providers including cloud service providers, evolving approaches to software development including incremental and iterative models and methods, and increased use of software tools and automation to achieve greater control, higher quality, and lower risks throughout the life cycle.

Associated with this is the reinforcement of the message that the GAMP specification and verification approach is not inherently linear but also fully supports iterative and incremental (Agile) methods.

Guidance on the application of new and developing technological areas such as Artificial Intelligence and Machine Learning (AI/ML), blockchain, cloud computing, and Open-Source Software (OSS) has been included or updated.

The importance of critical thinking and the application of patient-centric, risk-based approaches (aimed at quality and safety) versus primarily compliance-driven approaches is further underlined. Concepts of computerized systems assurance as discussed as part of the US FDA Center for Devices and Radiological Health (CDRH) Case for Quality program are also explored and applied.

Links and references to GAMP guidance on the topic area of record and data integrity have been added.

The following ISPE initiatives and topic areas are supported:

  • Knowledge Management – focusing on how organizations create, manage, and use knowledge throughout the life cycle of a product.
  • APQ (Advancing Pharmaceutical Quality) – building industry-for-industry tools and programs to help companies assess and improve their quality operations.
  • Pharma 4.0™ – providing guidance to accelerate Pharma 4.0 transformations, enabling organizations to leverage the full potential of digitalization to provide faster innovations for the benefit of patients.

GAMP guidance adopts a patient-centric risk-based approach that enables innovation while demonstrating compliance with regulatory requirements.

1.1 第二版更新理由解析

第一版 vs 第二版：什麼沒變，什麼變了

不變的：整體框架、五大核心概念、QRM 流程（對應 ICH Q9）

新增的：

  • AI/ML 指引（Appendix D11）
  • 區塊鏈 / 分散式帳本系統（Appendix D10）
  • 雲端運算與 OSS 更新
  • Agile 敏捷開發方法（Appendix D8）
  • 軟體工具（Appendix D9）
  • IT 基礎設施（Appendix M11）
  • 批判性思維（Critical Thinking）（Appendix M12）——第二版最重要的哲學轉向

移除的：Appendix D2（功能規格）、Appendix O7（維修活動）、Appendix S5（外包 IS/IT 環境）

批判性思維（Critical Thinking）——第二版的靈魂

第二版最大的精神轉變：從「合規驅動（compliance-driven）」走向「以病患為中心的風險導向（patient-centric, risk-based）」。

以前：只要填完表格、完成文件，就算合規。
現在：要問「這樣做真的保護了病患安全嗎？」——這就是批判性思維。

Appendix M12 專門討論如何培養這種能力。對 CDMO 的意義：不要為了驗證而驗證，要問每個 CSV 活動的實質風險貢獻。

比喻：Pharma 4.0 與 GAMP 5 的關係

Pharma 4.0 是目的地（全面數位化、實時數據驅動工廠），GAMP 5 是地圖（如何在這條路上確保電腦化系統合規）。兩者不衝突，GAMP 5 第二版刻意與 Pharma 4.0 框架對齊。

AI/ML 對 CDMO 的意義

第二版新增 AI/ML 指引，直接影響 CDMO 的未來系統（如本公司研究的 SA25 相關 AI 視覺檢測）。重點：AI/ML 系統的「fit for intended use」驗證，比傳統軟體更複雜，因為模型會隨數據演化。GAMP 5 的框架提供了一個起點。

1.2 New and Revised Material

New guidance has been included on the following topics:

  • Appendix D8 – Agile
  • Appendix D9 – Software Tools
  • Appendix D10 – Distributed Ledger Systems (Blockchain)
  • Appendix D11 – Artificial Intelligence and Machine Learning (AI/ML)
  • Appendix M11 – IT Infrastructure
  • Appendix M12 – Critical Thinking

Significantly updated guidance has been included on the following topics:

  • Appendix D1 – Specifying Requirements
  • Appendix S2 – Electronic Production Records

As a result of the above additions and revisions, the following guidance included in the previous version of this Guide have been removed:

  • Appendix D2 – Functional Specifications
  • Appendix O7 – Repair Activity
  • Appendix S5 – Managing Quality within an Outsourced IS/IT Environment

The overall GAMP 5 framework, key concepts, system life cycle, specification and verification approach, and Quality Risk Management (QRM) process (aligned with ICH Q9) remains unchanged.

核心框架穩定性

重要提醒：第二版雖然更新了許多技術內容，但框架本身（Framework）、五大核心概念、QRM 流程未變。這表示如果你掌握了 GAMP 5 第一版的精神，第二版只是在新技術場景上擴充應用。

1.3 Purpose

The purpose of this Guide is to provide a cost-effective framework of good practice to ensure that computerized systems are effective and of high quality, fit for intended use, and compliant with applicable regulations. The framework aims to safeguard patient safety, product quality, and data integrity while also delivering business benefit.

This Guide also provides suppliers to the life-science industry with guidance on the development and maintenance of systems by following good practice.

Patient safety is affected by the integrity of critical records, data, and decisions, as well as those aspects affecting physical attributes of the product. The phrase "patient safety, product quality, and data integrity" is used throughout this Guide to underline this point.

This Guide is intended for use by regulated companies, suppliers, and regulators. Suppliers include providers of software, hardware, equipment, system integration services, IT service providers, and IT support services, both internal and external to the regulated company.

The Guide has been designed for use by a wide range of disciplines and responsibilities, including:

  • Management
  • Quality Unit
  • Research
  • Development
  • Manufacture
  • Laboratory
  • Engineering
  • IT
  • Support Staff
  • All associated suppliers

GAMP documents are guides and not standards. It is the responsibility of regulated companies to establish policies and procedures to meet applicable regulatory requirements. Consequently, it is inappropriate for regulated companies, suppliers, or products to claim that they are GAMP certified, approved, or compliant.

1.3 目的解析

目的的三個層次

  • 合規層：幫助解讀法規要求（21 CFR Part 11、EU Annex 11、ICH Q9 等）
  • 品質層：確保系統 fit for intended use（符合預期用途）
  • 業務層：在合規的同時帶來商業利益（減少停機、降低維護成本）

再次強調：不能聲稱 GAMP 認證

原文："it is inappropriate for regulated companies, suppliers, or products to claim that they are GAMP certified, approved, or compliant."

這是很多 CDMO 供應鏈稽核時常見的誤解。供應商說「我們是 GAMP 合規」是不正確的說法，正確的說法應是「我們的系統驗證遵循 GAMP 5 指引，並符合 EU GMP Annex 11 要求。」

比喻：廚師的食譜書 vs 食品安全法規

GAMP 5 像米其林廚師的最佳實踐食譜書，告訴你怎麼做才能出好菜。FDA 21 CFR Part 11 和 EU Annex 11 是食品安全法規，不遵守就違法。食譜書幫你符合法規，但法規才是強制要求。

適用對象對 CDMO 的意義

GAMP 5 明確指出適用對象包含：受監管公司、供應商、監管機構，以及管理層、QA、研發、製造、實驗室、工程、IT 等所有職能。

這意味著在 CDMO 中，CSV 活動不是 IT 一個部門的責任，而是跨部門協作：製程負責人（Process Owner）定義需求，IT 負責技術實施，QA 負責驗證策略，供應商提供文件支持。

1.4 Scope

This Guide applies to computerized systems used in regulated activities covered by:

  • Good Manufacturing Practice (GMP) (pharmaceutical, including Active Pharmaceutical Ingredient (API), veterinary, and blood)
  • Good Clinical Practice (GCP)
  • Good Laboratory Practice (GLP)
  • Good Distribution Practice (GDP)
  • Good Pharmacovigilance Practices (GVP)
  • Medical Device Regulations (where applicable and appropriate, e.g., for systems used as part of production or the quality system, and for some examples of Software as a Medical Device (SaMD))

These are collectively known as GxP regulations.

This Guide provides an approach that is suitable for all types of computerized systems, focusing on those based on standard and configurable products, but equally applicable to custom (bespoke) applications.

The principles described can be applied to a wide range of computerized systems. Detailed application of these principles to specific system types (e.g., IT, infrastructure, process control systems, and analytical laboratory systems) is described in supporting ISPE GAMP Good Practice Guides.

Not all the activities defined in this Guide will apply to every system. The scalable approach, with application of critical thinking, enables regulated companies to select the appropriate system life cycle activities.

This Guide is also consistent with other regulatory demands such as Sarbanes-Oxley (SOX) and those associated with data privacy. The use of this Guide, however, does not guarantee compliance with, or replace, these regulatory demands.

It is recognized that there are acceptable methods other than those described in this Guide. This Guide is not intended to place any constraints on innovation and development of new concepts and technologies.

1.4.1 Supplier Aspects

The computerized system life cycle described in this Guide for a regulated company should not be confused with the need for a defined approach or method for software development, which is the responsibility of the supplier.

This Guide defines activities and responsibilities expected of the supplier in the provision of products and services. These activities perform an important role in supporting regulated company activities. The supplier may be a third party or an internal group of the regulated company. Such internal groups should follow processes consistent with the regulated company Quality Management System (QMS).

This Guide uses various diagrams to represent the system life cycle. These diagrams often present relationships in a linear representation. This is not intended to constrain the choice of development methods and models. Suppliers should use the most appropriate methods and models, which may include iterative and incremental (Agile), evolutionary, exploratory, and prototyping techniques, or the use of DevOps approaches.

Modern systems may have a complex supply chain involving multiple suppliers. This Guide aims to meet the needs of each group.

1.4 適用範圍解析

GxP 涵蓋範圍（x = 不同製藥活動）

縮寫全名典型系統
GMP製造品質規範MES、SCADA、eBPR
GCP臨床試驗規範CTMS、EDC
GLP實驗室規範LIMS、電子實驗記錄
GDP流通規範倉儲管理、溫控追蹤
GVP藥物警戒規範不良反應報告系統

CDMO（無菌充填）主要適用：GMP（核心）、部分 GLP（若有品管實驗室）。

SaMD（Software as a Medical Device）的邊界

GAMP 5 適用部分醫療器械法規，但 SaMD 有自己的框架（ISO 13485、ISO 14971、IEC 62304），通常需要個別審批和臨床評估。兩者不能混淆：GAMP 5 管「支援 GxP 製程的內部系統」，SaMD 管「交到病患或醫護手中的軟體產品」。

供應商責任框架

受監管公司（Regulated Company）
├── 負責：合規策略、供應商評估、驗證
└── 委託 ──▶ 供應商（Supplier）
              ├── 負責：軟體開發方法、文件提供
              ├── 可使用：Agile、DevOps、原型開發
              └── 內部 IT 部門也算「供應商」角色

關鍵概念：供應商可以用 Agile 方法開發，GAMP 5 的線性圖示只是示意，不代表必須用瀑布式開發。

CDMO 供應商管理應用

GAMP 5 明確要求受監管公司評估供應商能力。在 CDMO 中，這意味著：

  • 設備供應商（如充填機製造商）提供的 IQ/OQ 文件，可以作為 CSV 證據使用，但前提是通過了供應商評估（Supplier Assessment）
  • 雲端服務提供商（AWS、Azure）的安全認證可納入系統驗證策略
  • 內部 IT 部門開發的系統，同樣需要遵循 QMS 規定

1.5 Business Benefits

Effective, reliable, and high-quality computerized systems assist in achieving the primary objectives of patient safety, product quality, and data integrity, but there are major business benefits in having a defined process that delivers systems fit for intended use, on time, and within budget. Systems that are well defined and specified are easier to support and maintain, resulting in less downtime and lower maintenance costs. Adoption of the approaches described in this Guide will assist regulated companies in managing business risk as well as quality risks.

Specific benefits to both regulated companies and suppliers include:

  • Reduction of cost and time taken to achieve and maintain compliance
  • Early defect identification and resolution leading to reduced impact on cost and schedule
  • Cost-effective operation and maintenance
  • Effective change management and continual improvement
  • Enabling of innovation and adoption of new technology
  • Providing frameworks for user/supplier cooperation
  • Assisting suppliers to produce required documentation
  • Promotion of common system life cycle, language, and terminology
  • Providing practical guidelines and examples
  • Promoting pragmatic interpretation of regulations

1.5 商業利益解析

CSV 不只是合規成本，也是競爭優勢

GAMP 5 明確指出，良好的 CSV 帶來商業價值：

  • 減少停機時間：充填線每小時停機成本極高，好的系統維護策略直接影響 OEE
  • 降低維護成本：規格清楚的系統，變更管理更容易
  • 加速新技術採用：有框架的公司可以安全地引入 AI/ML、雲端等新技術
  • 共同語言：與客戶、供應商、監管機構建立共通術語，減少溝通成本

比喻：提早發現缺陷的價值

「Early defect identification」就像工程界的「右移測試成本曲線」：在需求階段發現一個問題修改的成本是 1，在驗證階段是 10，在上線後是 100。GAMP 5 的生命週期方法就是要把問題提前發現。

對 CDMO 來說：一個在 FAT（工廠驗收測試）階段發現的 SCADA 問題，遠比在 PQ 後才發現便宜得多。

對管理層的說服邏輯

當你需要向管理層說明為什麼要投資 CSV 時，這裡提供了完整的商業案例：

  • 減少合規成本 → 降低稽查風險罰款
  • 系統可靠性提升 → OEE 提升
  • 變更管理標準化 → 上市速度加快
  • 供應商協作框架 → 採購談判有據可依

1.6 Structure

1.6.1 Overview of GAMP Documentation Structure

This Guide forms part of a family of documents that together provide a powerful and comprehensive body of knowledge covering all aspects of computerized systems' good practice and compliance (Figure 1.2: GAMP Documentation Structure).

This Guide comprises a main body and a set of supporting appendices. The main body provides principles and a life cycle framework applicable to GxP regulated computerized systems. Practical guidance on a wide range of topics is provided in the supporting appendices.

Separate ISPE GAMP Good Practice Guides cover the application of these general principles and framework to specific types of systems and platforms.

1.6.2 GAMP 5 Main Body Structure

The main body introduction covers the purpose, scope, benefits, and structure of this Guide. Subsequent sections of the main body cover the topics:

  • Key concepts
  • Life cycle approach
  • Life cycle phases:
    • Concept
    • Project
    • Operation
    • Retirement
  • QRM
  • Regulated company activities:
    • Governance for achieving compliance
    • System-specific activities
  • Supplier activities
  • Efficiency improvements

The key concepts, described in Chapter 2, are the five concepts that underpin the rest of the document and should be applied using critical thinking.

QRM is a systematic approach for the identification, assessment, control, communication, and review of risks to patient safety, product quality, and data integrity. It is an iterative process applied throughout the system life cycle. Chapter 5 describes this approach.

Chapter 4 describes the project life cycle phase in more detail, including: Planning; Specification, configuration, and coding; Verification; Reporting and release. The key supporting processes of risk management, change and configuration management, design review, traceability, and document management are also introduced.

Ensuring compliance and fitness for purpose is the responsibility of the regulated company. Governance and system-specific regulated company activities are covered in Chapter 6. An overview of typical supplier activities is given in Chapter 7. Chapter 8 covers key topics leading to efficiency improvements.

    ├── 特定系統類型（如 IT 基礎設施、實驗室系統）
    └── 特定活動類型（如資料完整性、雲端系統）

比喻：地圖 + 詳細街道指南

GAMP 5 主體就像「台灣全圖」，給你整體方向和架構。各附錄像「城市詳細地圖」，帶你深入具體場景。ISPE GAMP GPGs 則像「特定景點導覽手冊」，針對特定系統類型（如 SCADA、雲端 SaaS）提供專屬建議。

Chapter 2: Key Concepts — 第二章：核心概念

2 Key Concepts

2.1 Overview

Five key concepts are applied throughout this Guide:

  1. Product and process understanding
  2. Life cycle approach within a QMS
  3. Scalable life cycle activities
  4. Science-based QRM
  5. Leveraging supplier involvement

The relationship between these concepts is shown in Figure 2.1: Key Concepts of this Guide. These five concepts underpin the entire framework and should be applied using critical thinking.

2.1 五大核心概念總覽

五大核心概念記憶框架

  • 1. 了解製程（Product & Process Understanding）：你的系統要服務什麼製程？
  • 2. 全生命週期（Life Cycle Approach）：從搖籃到墳墓，都在 QMS 框架內管理
  • 3. 可縮放活動（Scalable Activities）：高風險系統多做，低風險系統少做
  • 4. 科學化 QRM（Science-Based QRM）：用 ICH Q9 方法識別、評估、控制風險
  • 5. 善用供應商（Leveraging Supplier）：供應商的文件、測試、經驗都是你的資源

比喻：蓋房子的五個基本原則

1=了解地基和建築用途；2=從設計到拆除都有計畫；3=豪宅和倉庫規格不同；4=用科學計算結構風險；5=充分利用建築師和承包商的專業。五個概念環環相扣，缺任何一個都會出問題。

2.1.1 Product and Process Understanding

An understanding of the supported process is fundamental to determining system requirements. Product and process understanding is the basis for making science- and risk-based decisions to ensure that the system is fit for its intended use. An understanding of the intended use of data within the process is also fundamental. Data integrity cannot be achieved without a complete understanding of the data flow.

"Product and process knowledge should be managed from development through the commercial life of the product up to and including product discontinuation… Knowledge management is a systematic approach to acquiring, analysing, storing, and disseminating information related to products, manufacturing processes and components." — ICH Q10

Efforts to ensure fitness for intended use should focus on those aspects that are critical to patient safety, product quality, and data integrity. These critical aspects should be identified, specified, and verified.

Systems within the scope of this Guide support a wide range of processes, including but not limited to clinical trials, toxicological studies, API production, formulated product production, warehousing, distribution, and pharmacovigilance.

For some manufacturing systems, process requirements depend on a thorough understanding of product characteristics. For these systems, identification of Critical Quality Attributes (CQAs) and related Critical Process Parameters (CPPs) enable process control requirements to be defined.

Specification of requirements should be focused on critical aspects. The extent and detail of requirement specification should be commensurate with associated risk, complexity, and novelty of the system. Requirements may be developed iteratively or incrementally, based upon an initial set of base requirements.

Incomplete process understanding hinders effective and efficient compliance and achievement of business benefit.

概念一：符合預期用途（Fit for Intended Use）

「符合預期用途」是整個 GAMP 5 的核心邏輯

「Fit for intended use（符合預期用途）」是 GAMP 5 最重要的一個短語。它的意思是：系統要能完成它被設計來完成的任務，同時滿足相關的法規要求。

關鍵推論：你必須先清楚知道預期用途，才能驗證系統是否符合。這就是為什麼「產品與製程理解」排在五大概念第一位。

CQA → CPP → 系統需求的鏈結

QTPP（品質目標產品檔案）
    │
    ▼
CQA（關鍵品質屬性）：如無菌性、效價、純度
    │
    ▼
CPP（關鍵製程參數）：如滅菌溫度、充填重量、環境微粒
    │
    ▼
系統控制需求（System Requirements）：SCADA 需監控 CPP
    │
    ▼
驗證重點（Verification Focus）：只驗 CPP 相關功能

這條鏈結確保 CSV 工作聚焦於真正影響品質的地方。

比喻：廚房設備的「預期用途」

一台設計用來揉麵的攪拌機（預期用途），你驗證它能不能正確揉麵。你不需要驗證它能不能榨果汁——那不是它的預期用途。GAMP 5 告訴你：把驗證精力集中在預期用途中的關鍵功能上。

數據完整性從製程理解開始

原文重點："Data integrity cannot be achieved without a complete understanding of the data flow."

在 CDMO 中，這意味著：在設計 eBPR 或 LIMS 之前，你必須先畫出數據流圖（Data Flow Diagram）——數據從哪裡產生、如何傳遞、由誰核准、保存在哪裡、保存多久。沒有這張圖，數據完整性只是空話。

2.1.2 Life Cycle Approach within a QMS

Adopting a complete computerized system life cycle entails defining activities in a systematic way from system conception to retirement. This enables management control and a consistent approach across systems.

The life cycle should form an intrinsic part of the company's QMS, which should be maintained and kept up-to-date as new ways of working are developed.

As experience is gained in system use, the QMS should enable continual process and system improvements based on periodic review and evaluation, operational and performance data, and root-cause analysis of failures. Identified improvements and corrective actions should follow change management.

A suitable life cycle, properly applied, enables the assurance of quality and fitness for intended use, and achieving and maintaining compliance with regulatory requirements. A well-managed and understood life cycle facilitates adoption of a Quality by Design (QbD) approach.

The life cycle approach is fundamental to this Guide and embodies each of the other key concepts. The life cycle is structured into phases and activities, as described in Chapter 3.

概念二：生命週期方法

系統生命週期四個階段

  • 概念階段（Concept）：確定需求、進行初步風險評估
  • 專案階段（Project）：規格、開發/採購、驗證、發布
  • 運營階段（Operation）：日常使用、變更管理、定期審查
  • 退場階段（Retirement）：數據遷移、系統停用

每個階段都在 QMS 框架內運行，並與持續改善（CAPA）連結。

比喻：車輛全生命週期管理

就像一輛公司車：採購前評估需求（概念）→ 驗車交車（專案）→ 定期保養、事故記錄（運營）→ 報廢/轉售（退場）。每個階段都有記錄，都在公司流程（QMS）內。臨時買的車、不維護、報廢也不留記錄——這就是沒有生命週期方法的系統。

QbD（品質設計）與 CSV 的連結

原文提到「well-managed life cycle facilitates QbD approach」。QbD 的核心是在設計階段就建入品質，而不是靠測試找問題。應用在 CSV：在系統規格階段就定義好 CQA/CPP 相關的系統功能，而不是系統上線後才想要測什麼。

2.1.3 Scalable Life Cycle Activities

Life cycle activities should be scaled according to:

  • System impact on patient safety, product quality, and data integrity (risk assessment)
  • System complexity and novelty (architecture and nature of system components including maturity and level of configuration or customization)
  • Outcome of supplier assessment (supplier capability)

Business impact also may influence the scaling of life cycle activities.

The strategy should be clearly defined in a plan and follow established and approved policies and procedures.

概念三：可縮放生命週期活動

可縮放（Scalable）的三個維度

  • 系統影響程度：影響 CQA/CPP 的系統 → 高度驗證；只管非 GxP 流程 → 最低驗證
  • 系統複雜度與新穎性：現成商品軟體（COTS）→ 較少驗證；客製化系統 → 更多驗證
  • 供應商能力：通過評估的成熟供應商 → 可槓桿其文件；新供應商 → 需更多自行驗證

GAMP 系統分類（Category）

Category 1：基礎設施軟體（操作系統、虛擬化）
    → 最少驗證文件

Category 3：非配置商品軟體（Word, Excel 非用於 GxP 用途）
    → 最少驗證

Category 4：可配置商品軟體（LIMS, MES, ERP）
    → 中度驗證，重點在配置驗證

Category 5：客製化軟體（內部開發 eBPR）
    → 最高驗證，需完整開發文件

（GAMP 類別在附錄中詳細定義，但此概念貫穿全書）

比喻：滅火器和核電廠的安全驗證不同

你不會用驗證核電廠的標準去驗證辦公室滅火器。同樣，一個只管行政費用報銷的 Excel 表，和一個控制無菌充填壓力的 SCADA 系統，驗證程度應該完全不同。可縮放原則就是讓你把驗證資源用在刀口上。

CDMO 系統分級實例

系統類別驗證程度
充填機 SCADACat 4高（CPP 監控）
LIMSCat 4高（GLP/GMP）
MESCat 4高（批次記錄）
ERP（庫存）Cat 4中（間接影響）
BMS（溫濕度）Cat 4高（環境監控）
HR 系統Cat 1/3低（非 GxP）

2.1.4 Science-Based Quality Risk Management

QRM is a systematic process for the identification, assessment, control, communication, mitigation, and review of risks. Application of QRM enables effort to be focused on critical aspects of a computerized system in a controlled and justified manner.

QRM should be based on clear process understanding and potential impact on patient safety, product quality, and data integrity. Combining knowledge management and QRM will facilitate achievement of QMS objectives by providing the means for science- and risk-based decisions related to product quality. For systems controlling or monitoring CPPs, these should be traceable to CQAs, and ultimately back to the Quality Target Product Profile (QTPP) and relevant regulatory submissions.

Qualitative or quantitative techniques may be used to identify and manage risks. Controls are developed to reduce risks to an acceptable level. Implemented controls are monitored during operation to ensure ongoing effectiveness.

A practical risk-management process is described in Chapter 5.

概念四：科學化品質風險管理

QRM 與 ICH Q9 的關聯

GAMP 5 的 QRM 方法直接對應 ICH Q9（品質風險管理）。ICH Q9 是製藥 QRM 的聖經，GAMP 5 將其應用到電腦化系統領域。

QRM 的六個步驟：識別（Identify）→ 評估（Assess）→ 控制（Control）→ 溝通（Communicate）→ 緩解（Mitigate）→ 審查（Review）

科學化 QRM 的鏈結

QTPP（目標產品品質檔案）
    │
    ▼
CQA（關鍵品質屬性）
    │
    ▼
CPP（關鍵製程參數）← 系統需控制/監控
    │
    ▼
系統風險評估（Risk Assessment）
    │
    ├── 高風險功能 → 深度驗證 + 持續監控
    └── 低風險功能 → 簡化驗證

關鍵：風險評估必須可追溯（traceable）回 CQA 和 QTPP，符合法規要求。

科學化 vs 合規驅動的差異

合規驅動（舊思維）：「我要驗證這個功能，因為 SOP 說要。」
科學化 QRM（新思維）：「這個功能影響無菌充填的溫度控制（CPP），進而影響產品效價（CQA），所以我要深度驗證它。」

前者是盲目填表，後者是有科學依據的決策。第二版的批判性思維就是要推動這種轉變。

定性 vs 定量風險評估

GAMP 5 允許兩種方式：

  • 定性：高/中/低風險矩陣（FMEA 式）——最常用，適合大多數 CDMO 系統
  • 定量：概率 × 後果的數值計算——較少見，適合高度複雜系統

選擇方法本身也需要批判性思維：不要為了做定量評估而做，如果定性評估已足夠支持決策，就用定性。

2.1.5 Leveraging Supplier Involvement

Regulated companies should seek to maximize supplier involvement throughout the system life cycle in order to leverage knowledge, experience, and documentation, subject to satisfactory supplier assessment.

For example, the supplier may assist with requirements gathering, risk assessments, the creation of functional and other specifications, system configuration, testing, support, and maintenance.

Planning should determine how best to use supplier documentation, including existing test documentation, to avoid wasted effort and duplication. Justification for the use of supplier documentation should be provided by the satisfactory outcome of supplier assessments, which may include supplier audits.

Documentation should be assessed for suitability, accuracy, and completeness. There should be flexibility regarding acceptable format, structure, and documentation practices.

Supplier assessment is described in Chapter 6.

概念五：善用供應商參與

供應商文件可以作為 CSV 證據

這是 GAMP 5 最具實用價值的概念之一：如果供應商通過評估，其文件（IQ/OQ 協議、測試報告、FAT 記錄）可以直接用作你的驗證包一部分，避免重複工作。

前提：必須先完成供應商評估（Supplier Assessment），確認其能力和可信度。

比喻：信任但需驗證（Trust but Verify）

就像買車時，你信任原廠的品質測試報告，但你仍然要試駕和檢查重要功能。GAMP 5 的供應商槓桿就是：相信有能力的供應商的工作，但你仍需評估其適用性、準確性和完整性，並在自己的文件中引用和認可。

CDMO 供應商槓桿實例

  • 充填機製造商：利用其 FAT 測試記錄作為 IQ 基礎，不需全部重測
  • LIMS 供應商（如 LABVANTAGE）：使用其標準安裝驗證協議，只補充自己的配置驗證
  • 雲端服務商（AWS/Azure）：使用其 ISO 27001、SOC 2 報告支持基礎設施驗證
  • ERP 供應商（SAP）：利用其標準化流程文件，聚焦於自己的客製化驗證

每種情況都需先完成供應商評估並記錄，才能合理使用其文件。

文件評估三個標準

GAMP 5 明確指出，使用供應商文件前需評估：

  • 適用性（Suitability）：文件是否適用於你的系統配置？
  • 準確性（Accuracy）：內容是否正確反映系統實際狀態？
  • 完整性（Completeness）：是否覆蓋所有你需要驗證的功能？

2.2 Key Terms

Computerized System

A computerized system consists of the hardware and software components, together with the controlled function or process (including procedures, people, and equipment and associated documentation).

This term covers a broad range of systems, including, but not limited to:

  • Clinical trials data management
  • Manufacturing resource planning
  • Laboratory information management
  • Automated manufacturing equipment
  • Automated laboratory equipment
  • Process control and process analysis
  • Manufacturing execution
  • Building management
  • Warehousing and distribution
  • Blood processing management
  • Adverse event reporting (vigilance)
  • Document management
  • SaMD and digital health applications

Computerized System Validation (CSV)

Achieving and maintaining compliance with applicable GxP regulations and fitness for intended use by:

  • The adoption of principles, approaches, and life cycle activities within the framework of validation plans and reports
  • The application of appropriate operational controls throughout the life of the system

GxP Compliance

Meeting all applicable pharmaceutical and associated life-science regulatory requirements.

GxP Regulated Computerized System

Computerized systems that are subject to GxP regulations. The regulated company must ensure that such systems comply with the appropriate regulations.

GxP Regulation

The underlying international pharmaceutical requirements, such as those set forth in the US FD&C Act, FDA regulations, EU Directives, UK MHRA regulations, Japanese regulations, or other applicable national legislation or regulations. These include but are not limited to: GMP, GCP, GLP, GDP, Good Quality Practice (GQP), GVP, Medical Device Regulations, Prescription Drug Marketing Act (PDMA).

Process Owner

The owner of the business process or processes being managed. The process owner is ultimately responsible for ensuring that the computerized system and its operation is in compliance and fit for intended use in accordance with applicable company SOPs. The process owner may also be the system owner. The process owner may be the de facto owner of the data residing on the system (data owner) and therefore, ultimately responsible for the integrity of the data. Process owners are typically the head of the functional unit using the system.

Quality Management System (QMS)

Management system to direct and control an organization with regard to quality. (ISO). This is equivalent to Quality System as defined in ICH Q9.

Subject Matter Expert (SME)

Those individuals with specific expertise in a particular area or field. SMEs should take the lead role in the verification of computerized systems. SME responsibilities include planning and defining verification strategies, defining acceptance criteria, selection of appropriate test methods, execution of verification tests, and reviewing results. (ASTM E2500)

System Owner

The system owner is responsible for the availability and support and maintenance of a system, and for the security of the data residing on that system. The system owner is responsible for ensuring that the computerized system is supported and maintained in accordance with applicable company SOPs. For systems supporting regulated processes and maintaining regulated data and records, the ownership of the data resides with the GxP process owner, not the system owner. The system owner acts on behalf of the users. The system owner for larger systems will typically be from IT or engineering functions. Global IT systems may have a global system owner and a local system owner to manage local implementation.

2.2 關鍵術語解析

電腦化系統（Computerized System）的廣義定義

注意 GAMP 5 的定義包含「硬體 + 軟體 + 受控功能或製程（包括程序、人員、設備和相關文件）」。

這意味著：驗證的對象不只是軟體本身，還包括 SOP、操作人員的訓練、相關設備的整合。這是為什麼 CSV 是跨部門工作的根本原因。

比喻：系統 = 硬體 + 軟體 + 人 + 流程

就像「廚房系統」不只是烤箱（硬體）和定時器控制程式（軟體），還包括廚師（人）和食譜 SOP（流程）。一個環節出問題，整個系統就出問題。

CSV 的正式定義重點

CSV 是「達成並維持合規性與符合預期用途」，關鍵詞是「達成 AND 維持」——不是一次性驗證，而是整個生命週期的持續活動。這也是為什麼「定期審查（Periodic Review）」和「變更管理」是 CSV 的核心組成部分。

製程負責人 vs 系統負責人的責任區分

製程負責人（Process Owner）
├── 業務製程合規的最終責任
├── 確保系統符合預期用途
├── 通常是使用該系統的功能單位主管
└── 數據完整性的最終責任（數據擁有者）

系統負責人（System Owner）
├── 系統可用性、支援與維護
├── 數據安全（存取控制）
├── 通常來自 IT 或工程部門
└── 代表使用者管理系統

重要：受監管製程的數據所有權 → 製程負責人
      （不是系統負責人）

CDMO 中誰是誰

系統製程負責人系統負責人
充填機 SCADA生產部門主管工程部門
LIMSQC 主管IT 部門
MES/eBPR生產部門主管IT 部門
BMS廠務/工程主管工程部門
ERP多個（財務/採購）IT 部門

SME（主題專家）的關鍵角色

GAMP 5 明確說 SME 應在系統驗證中扮演主導角色——負責規劃驗證策略、定義接受標準、選擇測試方法、執行測試、審查結果。

對 CDMO 的意義：驗證工作不應只由 QA 或 IT 執行，必須由真正懂製程的 SME（如 QC 分析師、生產工程師）主導。QA 是框架提供者和監督者，而非所有 CSV 活動的唯一執行者。

GAMP 5 與主要法規的關聯

法規適用市場GAMP 5 的角色
21 CFR Part 11美國 FDA提供實施指引
EU GMP Annex 11歐盟 EMA提供實施指引
ICH Q9國際通用QRM 方法來源
ICH Q10國際通用QMS 框架對齊
PIC/S GMP多國適用互相兼容

GAMP 5 不是法規，但它的框架設計確保遵循 GAMP 5 的公司更容易滿足上述所有法規。

章節總結 Section Summary — Chapters 1–2

  • GAMP 5 是什麼：ISPE 的實務指引，不是標準，不是認證體系。目標是幫助製藥業確保 GxP 電腦化系統符合預期用途，同時保護病患安全、產品品質與數據完整性。
  • 第二版最大亮點：新增批判性思維（M12）、AI/ML（D11）、區塊鏈（D10）、Agile（D8）、IT 基礎設施（M11）指引；強調從合規驅動走向以病患為中心的科學化風險決策。
  • 五大核心概念：①了解製程→定義需求；②全生命週期在 QMS 內管理；③根據風險/複雜度/供應商能力縮放驗證；④用 ICH Q9 科學化 QRM 聚焦關鍵功能；⑤善用供應商知識與文件（需先評估）。
  • 可縮放原則的實踐意義：LIMS 和充填 SCADA 的 CSV 策略應顯著不同；把驗證精力集中在 CPP/CQA 相關的關鍵功能，而非平均分配。
  • 關鍵術語釐清：電腦化系統 = 硬體+軟體+製程+人員；CSV 是持續活動而非一次性驗證；製程負責人擁有數據，系統負責人管理系統；SME 主導驗證工作。
  • CDMO 核心應用：建立系統清單並分類（Category 1-5），為每個 GxP 系統指定製程負責人，利用供應商 IQ/OQ 文件（通過評估後），以及數據流分析作為數據完整性的起點。
1

Section 1: Ch3-4: Life Cycle Approach & Phases

生命週期方法與各階段 | p23-p48

ISPE GAMP 5 Second Edition | p23 – p48

Learning Objectives  |  學習目標

  1. Explain the four major phases of the computerized system life cycle (Concept, Project, Operation, Retirement) and the activities within each.  ／  說明電腦化系統生命週期的四大階段及各階段核心活動。
  2. Distinguish between linear (V-model) and iterative/incremental (Agile) specification and verification approaches, and know when each is appropriate.  ／  區分線性（V-model）與迭代增量（Agile）方法，並能判斷各自的適用情境。
  3. Describe the GAMP 5 computerized system validation (CSV) framework and how it achieves GxP compliance without being tied to a fixed documentation set.  ／  描述 GAMP 5 CSV 框架如何在不拘泥於固定文件集的前提下達成 GxP 合規。
  4. Apply critical thinking to scale verification activities proportionately to risk, complexity, and novelty — not to paperwork volume.  ／  運用批判性思維，依風險、複雜度與新穎性比例調整查驗活動，而非以文件量為標準。
  5. Map traditional qualification terminology (DQ/IQ/OQ/PQ) to GAMP 5 verification activities and understand why GAMP 5 moves away from this terminology.  ／  將傳統 DQ/IQ/OQ/PQ 術語對應至 GAMP 5 查驗活動，並理解轉變的原因。
  6. Identify the key operational processes (change management, periodic review, CAPA, business continuity) that maintain compliance throughout the operation phase.  ／  識別在操作階段維持合規的關鍵運作流程，包括變更管理、定期審查、CAPA 與業務持續計畫。

Chapter 3: Life Cycle Approach  |  第3章：生命週期方法

3 Life Cycle Approach

Compliance with regulatory requirements and fitness for intended use may be achieved by adopting a life cycle approach following good practice as defined in this Guide.

A life cycle approach entails defining and performing activities in a systematic way from conception, understanding the requirements, through development, release, and operational use, to system retirement. Figure 3.1 shows a general specification, design, and verification process described in ASTM E2500.

This section of the Guide introduces the computerized system life cycle, a general approach to specification and verification, a framework for computerized system validation, and the application of critical thinking.

3.1 Computerized System Life Cycle

The computerized system life cycle encompasses all activities from initial concept to retirement. The life cycle for any system consists of four major phases:

  • Concept
  • Project
  • Operation
  • Retirement

During the concept phase, the regulated company should consider opportunities to automate one or more business processes based upon business need and benefits. Typically at this phase, initial requirements will be developed and potential solutions considered. An initial risk assessment or GxP assessment should be performed, so that GxP regulated systems are identified before the project phase commences.

The project phase involves planning, supplier assessment and selection, various levels of specification, configuration (or coding for custom applications), and verification leading to acceptance and release for operation. Risk management is applied to identify risks and to remove or reduce them to an acceptable level.

System operation is often the longest phase and is managed using defined, up-to-date, operational processes and procedures applied by personnel who have appropriate training, education, and experience. Maintaining control (including security), fitness for intended use, and compliance are key aspects. The management of changes of different impact, scope, and complexity is an important activity during this phase.

The final phase is the ultimate retirement of the system. It involves decisions about data retention, migration, or destruction, and the management of these processes.

Suppliers of products and services should be involved as appropriate throughout the life cycle. An inventory of computerized systems should be maintained. A GxP assessment should be performed by the beginning of the project stage to determine whether a system is GxP regulated, and if so, which specific regulations apply.

第3章 解析：生命週期思維

核心觀念：為什麼需要「生命週期方法」？

傳統上，許多藥廠把電腦化系統驗證（CSV）視為「上線前的一次性活動」——做完驗證文件、放行就結束了。GAMP 5 第2版明確反對這種心態。

生命週期方法（Life Cycle Approach）的核心思想是：合規不是一個時間點，而是整個系統存在期間的持續狀態。從最初的概念發想，到系統退役，每個階段都有相應的活動和控制。

CDMO 情境類比：新 LIMS 的生命旅程

假設你的 CDMO 決定導入一套新的 LIMS（實驗室資訊管理系統）：

  • 概念階段：業務需求分析、評估是否值得導入、初步 GxP 評估（LIMS 屬於 GxP 系統嗎？答：是的，因為它管理檢測結果）
  • 專案階段：選商、撰寫需求規格書（URS）、設定系統（Category 4）、執行測試、放行上線
  • 操作階段：日常使用、變更控制（例如新增一個分析方法的工作流程）、定期審查（每年確認系統仍符合法規）
  • 退役階段：當更新的 LIMS 取代舊系統時，舊系統的資料要保留多久？如何遷移？

重要實務提醒：GxP 評估要提早做

GxP 評估必須在專案階段開始前完成。這意味著在批准專案預算之前，就要確認這個系統是否受 GMP/GLP/GCP 等法規管轄，以及適用哪些條款。

若等到系統快上線才做 GxP 評估，往往會遇到需要補做大量文件的困境，甚至導致上線延遲。

3.2 Specification and Verification

The GAMP specification and verification approach is not inherently linear; it also fully supports iterative and incremental (Agile) methods.

A linear approach is particularly suitable when system requirements are fully understood and defined upfront (Figure 3.3). The specification activities have equivalent verification steps to determine whether the specification has been met. A hierarchy of specifications may be required for larger systems, while specifications may be combined for smaller, simpler, or standard systems.

As shown in Figure 3.4, the life cycle and specification and verification approach described in the Guide is not inherently linear. This Guide supports the use of Agile approaches for product development, the development of custom applications, and incremental product configuration.

Factors for the successful adoption of Agile include:

  • A robust QMS within an appropriate organizational culture
  • Well-trained and highly disciplined teams following a well-defined process supported by effective tools and automation
  • Proper customer or product owner involvement

This Guide describes the overall GxP system life cycle from the perspective of the regulated company and does not define the software development process in detail. While this section provides a suggested approach, it is recognized that other models and approaches are equally acceptable.

3.2 規格說明與查驗方法

線性 vs. 迭代：GAMP 5 的重要進化

GAMP 5 第1版主要以 V-model（V型模型） 為框架——左側從上到下寫規格（URS → FRS → CS → 程式碼），右側由下到上做測試（單元測試 → 整合測試 → OQ → PQ）。

第2版明確承認：V-model 只是眾多可接受方法之一。Agile 方法——短週期迭代、持續交付、隨時調整需求——同樣完全符合 GAMP 5 框架。

實務判斷：什麼時候用線性，什麼時候用 Agile？

情境建議方法
新 SCADA 系統（需求明確、供應商固定）線性（接近 V-model）
內部開發的資料分析工具（需求會演進）Agile（迭代+增量）
標準 ERP 模組上線（Category 4）彈性線性（可合併規格文件）
SaaS 系統（持續更新版本）Agile（CI/CD 概念）

關鍵認知：查驗不等於測試

「Verification（查驗）」是一個廣義概念，包含：

  • 設計審查（Design Review）
  • 程式碼審查（Code Review）
  • 組態設定審查（Configuration Review）
  • 各層次的測試執行

很多工程師習慣把「驗證」等同於「跑測試腳本」，但 GAMP 5 強調：在測試之前的設計審查本身就是查驗活動的一部分，甚至可以取代某些測試。

3.3 Computerized System Validation Framework

GAMP advocates a computerized system validation framework to achieve and maintain GxP compliance throughout the computerized system life cycle.

The framework is based on system-specific validation plans and reports and the application of appropriate operational controls. Validation plans and reports provide a disciplined and consistent approach to meeting regulatory requirements, leading to appropriate documentation at the right level. Such documents are valuable both in preparing for, and during, regulatory inspections.

Where a computer system is regarded as one component of a wider manufacturing process or system, particularly in an integrated QbD environment, specific and separate computerized system validation may not be necessary. This environment requires both complete product and process understanding and that the CPPs can be accurately and reliably predicted and controlled over the design space. In such a case, the fitness for intended use of the computer system within the process may be adequately demonstrated by documented engineering or project activities together with subsequent process validation or continuous quality verification of the overall process or system. The same principle applies to the adoption of Process Analytical Technology (PAT).

For automated manufacturing equipment, separate computer system validation should be avoided. Computer system specification and verification should be part of an integrated engineering approach to ensure compliance and fitness for intended use of the complete automated equipment.

3.3 CSV 框架解析

CSV 框架的核心文件：驗證計畫與報告

每個 GxP 電腦化系統都應有：

  • Validation Plan（驗證計畫）：描述「我們打算怎麼驗證」——範圍、方法、責任分工、可接受標準
  • Validation Report（驗證報告）：記錄「我們實際上做了什麼」——活動摘要、偏差、未解決事項、適用聲明（fitness for intended use statement）

這兩份文件是查驗活動的書面骨架，查驗計畫訂好游戲規則，報告確認規則有被遵守。

進階概念：何時不需要獨立的 CSV？

GAMP 5 提出一個重要例外：當電腦化系統只是更大製程系統中的一個組件（例如整合 QbD 環境），如果整體製程驗證已能涵蓋電腦系統的適用性，就不需要單獨進行 CSV。

CDMO 情境：一台凍乾機（Lyophilizer）的 PLC 控制器，如果其關鍵製程參數（CPPs）的控制能力已在製程驗證（PPQ）中充分驗證，那麼對這台 PLC 單獨做 IQ/OQ/PQ 可能是重複且不必要的。這正是 GAMP 5 與 ISPE C&Q 指引（Volume 5）整合思維的體現。

3.4 Critical Thinking Through the Life Cycle

Critical thinking promotes informed decision-making and good judgment on where and how to apply and scale quality and compliance activities for computerized systems. It relies on knowledge of the business process and on the detailed comprehension and analysis of where the business process can potentially impact patient safety, product quality, and data integrity.

The extent and depth, formality, and level of documentation formality may, and should, vary to a considerable degree between different business processes, types of systems, functions within a system, and applications. Significant efficiency improvements can be achieved by focusing on what is essential in individual situations and avoiding unnecessary work.

Critical thinking is not a one-time activity and should be applied throughout the computerized system life cycle. As such, critical thinking should become a habitual mindset based on an intellectual commitment to continual improvement.

Figure 3.5 illustrates critical thinking for computerized systems whereby proactive adoption of a risk-based approach takes into account the multiple layers of assurance provided elsewhere within the business process — combining technical, procedural, and behavioral controls applied throughout the business process.

This holistic approach requires an initial investment of time and effort to analyze the overall business process that the computerized system will support, and the associated regulated data. Business process mapping and data flow diagrams capture this knowledge and facilitate the identification and understanding of the potential risks to patient safety, product quality, and data integrity.

Regulatory authorities are adopting critical thinking to help determine whether controls are fit for intended use. Practitioners should not consider that the level of regulatory compliance achieved is directly proportionate to the amount of paperwork produced. Too much paperwork can confuse and make it harder to maintain and inspect computerized systems. Regulators look for scaled and targeted activities with well-organized information and records that have an appropriate level of detail, supported by clear and unambiguous rationales explaining the critical thinking applied.

3.4 批判性思維的實際應用

什麼是「批判性思維」在 GMP 情境中的意義？

「Critical Thinking」在 GAMP 5 中不是哲學概念，而是一個實際的決策工具：

  • 分析業務流程在哪裡可能影響病患安全、產品品質或數據完整性
  • 根據這個分析，判斷需要多嚴格的控制
  • 將控制力度與風險成比例——高風險處嚴格，低風險處精簡

多層保證（Layers of Assurance）的概念

假設你的 MES 系統有一個功能：記錄無菌灌裝操作的環境監測數據。批判性思維的問法是：

  • 如果 MES 這個功能出錯，還有什麼其他控制層可以接住？（例如：操作員人工確認、QC 實驗室複核、SCADA 系統備份數據）
  • 如果這些其他控制層很強，那麼這個 MES 功能的驗證深度就可以相應降低
  • 如果 MES 是唯一來源（single point of truth），沒有備援，那麼驗證就必須更嚴格

這就是「多層保證」思維——不孤立評估系統，而是評估整個業務流程的防護網。

監管機構的新期待：品質勝於數量

GAMP 5 明確寫道：合規程度與文件數量不成正比。這是對藥廠普遍「文件越厚越安全」心態的直接反駁。

FDA、EMA 查廠官員現在更傾向於問：

  • 「你為什麼這樣設計驗證方案？」（要看你的風險評估邏輯）
  • 「這份規格書的這個要求，你是怎麼確認它被滿足的？」（看可追溯性）

而不是：「你的 IQ/OQ/PQ 文件在哪裡？」

Chapter 4: Life Cycle Phases  |  第4章：生命週期各階段詳解

Phase 1: CONCEPT

4 Life Cycle Phases

The life cycle approach described is not inherently linear, and is designed to be compatible with a wide range of models and methods, including iterative and incremental (Agile) approaches. References to documentation and deliverables should not be interpreted as always requiring traditional documents. The maintenance of records and information in appropriate and effective software tools is encouraged.

4.1 Concept

Detailed activities in this phase will depend on company approaches to initiating and justifying project commencement. Gaining management commitment to provide appropriate resources is an important pre-project activity.

An initial risk assessment or GxP assessment should be performed so that GxP regulated systems are identified before the project phase commences.

階段一：概念期

4.1 概念階段解析

概念階段的核心任務

概念階段是整個生命週期的起點，在這個階段投入的思考品質，直接決定後續專案的順暢度。主要任務包括：

  • 定義業務需求（不是系統需求）——「我們需要什麼功能」而非「我們要買什麼軟體」
  • 初步評估可能的解決方案（外購、客製化、SaaS？）
  • 進行 GxP 評估：這個系統是否直接或間接影響 GxP 活動？
  • 取得管理層承諾與資源支持

CDMO 實例：新 SCADA 系統的概念評估

CDMO 計畫為新建無菌灌裝線安裝 SCADA 系統。概念階段要做的事：

  • GxP 評估：SCADA 控制灌裝參數（灌裝量、充氮速度、溫度）→ 直接影響產品品質 → GxP 系統，適用 GMP Annex 11
  • 評估方案：整合型工控 SCADA vs. 獨立 PLC + HMI？
  • 初步成本效益分析：是否值得進入專案階段？
Phase 2: PROJECT

4.2 Project

This section describes the following project stages in more detail:

  • Planning
  • Specification, configuration, and coding
  • Verification
  • Reporting and release

The key supporting processes of risk management, change and configuration management, design review, traceability, and document management also are described in this section. Each project stage typically involves multiple activities.

4.2.1 Planning

Planning should cover all required activities, responsibilities, procedures, and timelines. As described in Section 2.1.3, life cycle activities should be scaled according to:

  • System impact on patient safety, product quality, and data integrity (risk assessment)
  • System complexity and novelty (architecture and nature of system components, including maturity and level of configuration or customization)
  • Outcome of supplier assessment (supplier capability)

A clear and complete understanding of the process to be supported and initial user requirements facilitates effective planning. Initial requirements are often gathered during the concept phase and refined and enhanced during the planning stage.

The extent and detail of requirements gathering and specification should be sufficient to support risk assessment, further specification, development of the system, and verification. Where appropriate, e.g., for process control systems, requirements should be traceable to relevant CPPs and CQAs.

Requirements are the responsibility of the user community and should be maintained and controlled.

階段二：專案期

4.2 專案階段解析

專案階段的流程架構

專案階段是系統生命週期中活動最密集的時期，可以理解為四個主要階段的串聯：

規劃 → 規格／組態設定 → 查驗 → 報告與放行

這四個階段不是嚴格線性的——規劃期間可能已開始部分規格制定，查驗活動從規格審查就已開始。

4.2.1 規劃階段：三個決策維度

規劃階段最重要的決策是「這個系統的驗證要做到什麼程度」，GAMP 5 要求從三個維度評估：

  1. 風險程度：系統對病患安全、產品品質、數據完整性的影響有多大？影響越大，驗證越嚴格。
  2. 複雜度與新穎性：是成熟的標準軟體（低新穎性）還是全新客製化開發（高新穎性）？越新穎，越需要嚴格測試。
  3. 供應商能力：供應商有沒有通過藥廠稽核？供應商的測試文件能不能被採用？供應商能力越強，受監管公司的工作量越可以降低。

需求的歸屬：用戶社群的責任

GAMP 5 明確指出：需求的制定、維護與控制是用戶社群（user community）的責任——也就是實際使用這個系統的業務部門（生產、QC、QA 等），而不是 IT 部門或驗證部門。

實務提醒：URS（用戶需求規格書）必須由業務端主導撰寫，IT 或供應商只是協助澄清技術可行性。許多 CDMO 的問題在於讓 IT 單獨寫 URS，最後系統做出來不符合 GMP 業務邏輯。

4.2.2 Specification, Configuration, and Coding

The role of specification is to enable systems to be developed, verified, and maintained. The number and level of detail of the specifications will vary depending upon the type of system and its intended use. For example, software design specifications are not expected from the regulated company for non-custom products.

Specifications should be adequate to support subsequent activities, including risk assessment, further specification and development of the system, verification as appropriate, and system maintenance and update.

Any required configuration should be performed in accordance with a controlled and repeatable process. Any required software coding should be performed in accordance with defined standards. The need for code reviews within the organization producing the software should be considered.

Configuration management and version control are intrinsic and vital aspects of controlled configuration and coding. Specifications should be maintained and controlled.

4.2.2 規格說明、組態設定與程式撰寫

規格文件的目的：三個用途

規格文件存在的理由不是「監管機構要看」，而是：

  • 開發依據：讓供應商知道要做什麼
  • 查驗依據：讓測試人員知道要確認什麼
  • 維護依據：未來變更時，讓人知道原本的設計意圖

如果規格文件不能服務這三個目的，它就是沒有價值的文件。

URS → FRS → CS 的實務流程

以 CDMO 導入 LIMS 為例，規格文件的層次關係：

  • URS（用戶需求規格）：「QC 需要記錄每批原料的效期，並自動在效期前30天發出警告」
  • FRS（功能需求規格）：「系統應在效期 - 30 天時觸發警告通知，發送至指定的收件群組」（供應商層級）
  • CS（組態規格）：「Alert_Rule_01: Expiry_Date - 30 days, Recipient_Group: QC_Supervisors」（具體設定值）

對於 Category 3 系統（標準產品），通常只需要 URS + 測試記錄，不需要 FRS 和 CS。

版本控制是核心控制措施

GAMP 5 特別強調：組態管理與版本控制是受控組態設定的內在必要條件。在 GMP 環境中，這意味著：

  • 每一次系統設定的變更都必須有記錄可循
  • 在任何時間點都能回溯系統當時的狀態
  • 沒有經過版本控制的系統設定，在查廠時無法證明「受控狀態」

4.2.3 Verification

Verification confirms that specifications have been met. This may involve multiple stages of reviews and testing depending on the type of system, the development method applied, and its use.

While verification is shown as a single box on Figure 4.1, verification activities occur throughout the project stages. For example, design reviews should verify specifications during the specification stage.

Testing computerized systems is a fundamental verification activity. Testing is concerned with identifying defects so that they can be corrected, as well as demonstrating that the system meets requirements.

The use of effective and appropriate testing tools is encouraged. Such tools should have documented assessments for their adequacy (refer to EU Annex 11 Clause 4.7) and be controlled in use; however, validation is not required.

Testing is often performed at several levels depending on the risk, complexity, and novelty. Tests may be defined in one or more test specifications to cover hardware, software, configuration, and acceptance.

An appropriate test strategy should be developed based on the risk, complexity, and novelty. Supplier documentation should be assessed and used if suitable. The strategy should define which types of testing are required and the level and purpose of test specifications.

4.2.3 查驗活動解析

查驗貫穿整個專案期

這是 GAMP 5 一個重要的視角修正：查驗不只是最後的測試執行，而是貫穿專案的持續活動：

  • 規格階段：設計審查（Design Review）確認規格合理且可實現
  • 組態設定階段：組態審查確認設定符合規格
  • 測試階段：各層次測試確認功能符合需求
  • 放行階段：驗證報告確認所有查驗活動已完成

測試工具的使用：不需要驗證，但需要評估

很多藥廠不敢使用自動化測試工具（如 Selenium、UFT），因為擔心「這些工具本身要不要驗證」。

GAMP 5 的答案明確：測試工具不需要驗證（validation is not required），但需要：

  • 記錄評估文件，確認工具適合於預定用途（adequacy assessment）
  • 在使用中保持受控狀態（controlled in use）

這大幅降低了引入自動化測試工具的合規門檻，CDMO 應積極利用。

4.2.4 Reporting and Release

The system should be accepted for use in the operating environment and released into that environment in accordance with a controlled and documented process. Acceptance and release of the system for use in GxP regulated activities should follow a defined process and involve oversight and input of the process owner, system owner, and the appropriate quality function as necessary and applicable.

This may be a continuously managed process rather than a one-off event, for example Continuous Integration and Continuous Deployment (CI/CD), and Software as a Service (SaaS).

A computerized system validation report should be produced summarizing the activities performed, any deviations from the plan, any outstanding and corrective actions, and provide a statement of fitness for intended use of the system.

A well-managed system handover from the project team to the process owner, system owner, and operational users is a prerequisite for effectively maintaining compliance of the system during operation.

4.2.4 報告與放行

驗證報告的必要內容

一份完整的 Validation Report（驗證報告）應包含：

  • 已執行的查驗活動摘要
  • 相對於計畫的偏差（Deviations from plan）
  • 未解決事項及其矯正行動
  • 適用聲明（Fitness for Intended Use Statement）——明確聲明系統適合在 GxP 環境中使用

移交（Handover）：被忽視的關鍵環節

GAMP 5 特別強調移交管理的重要性。在很多 CDMO 中，系統驗證完成後，專案團隊就解散了，但運維團隊對系統的了解遠不足夠。

良好的移交應確保：

  • 運維程序（SOPs）已制定並培訓
  • 隱性知識（implicit knowledge）已轉移——不只是文件，還有「為什麼這樣設計」的背景理解
  • 支援服務（如供應商合約、維護計畫）已就位

4.2.5 Supporting Processes

4.2.5.1 Risk Management
An appropriate risk-management process should be established throughout the project phase.

4.2.5.2 Change and Configuration Management
Appropriate configuration management processes should be established such that a computerized system and all its constituent components can be identified and defined at any point during its life cycle. Change management procedures covering software, hardware, and documentation should be established. Appropriate change processes should be applied to both project and operational phases.

4.2.5.3 Design Review
At suitable stages during the life cycle, planned and systematic design reviews of specifications, design, and development should be performed. This design review process should evaluate deliverables to ensure that they satisfy the specified requirements. The rigor of the design review process and the extent of documentation should be based on risk, complexity, and novelty. Design reviews are mainly applicable for custom applications and within the supplier product development processes.

4.2.5.4 Traceability
Traceability is a process for ensuring that:

  • Requirements are traceable back to business process needs
  • Requirements are addressed and traceable to the appropriate functional and design elements in the specifications
  • Requirements can be traced to the appropriate verification

Traceability should be focused on aspects critical to patient safety, product quality, and data integrity. The use of traceability tools and automated traceability methods is encouraged.

4.2.5.5 Documentation and Knowledge Management
Management of documentation includes preparation, review, approval, issue, change, withdrawal, and storage. Documentation, tools, and systems contain explicit knowledge that is captured and codified, whereas implied knowledge is context-specific knowledge acquired through personal experience. Both need to be considered for successful initial and subsequent system deployments.

4.2.5 支援流程解析

可追溯性矩陣（RTM）的實務價值

可追溯性（Traceability）的核心工具是需求可追溯性矩陣（Requirement Traceability Matrix, RTM），它確保：

  • 每個 URS 需求都有對應的規格條款
  • 每個規格條款都有對應的測試案例
  • 每個測試案例的結果都有記錄

RTM 在查廠時讓查廠官員可以快速確認：「這個需求，你是怎麼驗證它被滿足的？」

設計審查：什麼情況下需要正式進行？

GAMP 5 說設計審查「主要適用於客製化應用和供應商內部產品開發」。轉譯到實務：

  • Category 3 標準產品：通常不需要設計審查，規格審查即可
  • Category 4 組態設定產品：對複雜的組態設定可考慮進行組態設計審查
  • Category 5 客製化應用：必須進行設計審查，因為沒有現成的產品功能規格可以依賴

隱性知識管理：最常被忽視的合規風險

GAMP 5 提到「implied knowledge（隱性知識）」——這是指存在於人腦中、未被文件化的系統知識。

典型風險場景：唯一熟悉某 SCADA 系統設定邏輯的工程師離職，而文件中只記錄了「做了什麼」，沒有記錄「為什麼這樣做」。一旦系統出現問題或需要變更，繼任工程師根本不知道設計意圖，容易引入新的錯誤。

4.2.6 Practical Examples — GAMP Categories

This section shows how the general approach may be applied in a scalable manner to three common types of systems, using Categorization of software.

Computerized systems are generally made up of a combination of components from different GAMP Categories. Categories 3 to 5 should be viewed as a continuum with no absolute boundaries. Table-driven approaches purely based on categorization decisions should be avoided.

4.2.6.1 Category 3 — Standard Product: Software products used off-the-shelf (not configurable for a specific business process). Approach: one level of specification and verification is typically applicable. Testing typically covers correct installation, tests demonstrating fitness for intended use, and any further tests from risk/supplier assessments.

4.2.6.2 Category 4 — Configured Product: Commercial software products configured for a specific business process. A flexible approach to specification and verification may be applied. Testing covers correct installation, configuration of the system, functionality supporting the specific business process, and acceptance against requirements. Testing should be focused on the configuration.

4.2.6.3 Category 5 — Custom Application: Developed to meet individual user requirements where no commercially available solution is suitable. May use linear (waterfall) or Agile methods. Testing covers correct installation, functionality and design, fitness for intended use, and any further tests from risk assessments. Rigorous testing should be performed at both functional and design levels.

4.2.6 GAMP 分類實務應用

三種系統類型的驗證深度對比

類別典型系統規格文件測試重點
Cat. 3
標準產品		 Excel、電子磅秤軟體、Adobe Acrobat URS（簡化） 安裝確認 + 適用性測試
Cat. 4
組態設定		 LIMS（如 LabWare）、ERP（SAP）、CDMS URS + FRS（視規模）+ 組態規格 安裝 + 組態 + 業務流程測試
Cat. 5
客製化應用		 自行開發的批次記錄系統、客製報表工具 URS + FRS + 設計規格 + 程式碼審查 模組 + 整合 + 功能 + 使用者接受測試

分類只是起點，不是終點

GAMP 5 非常清楚地警告：不要純粹依賴分類表格來決定驗證活動（Table-driven approaches should be avoided）。

分類（Category 3/4/5）只是一個起點，實際的驗證深度還要考慮：

  • 這個系統功能對 GxP 的影響有多大？
  • 供應商的品質系統可靠度如何？
  • 系統的複雜度和新穎性是什麼水準？

同樣是 Category 4 系統，一個管理批次記錄的 LIMS 和一個管理員工訓練記錄的系統，驗證深度可以差距很大。

4.2.6.4 Terminology — IQ/OQ/PQ vs. GAMP 5

The specific terminology used to describe life cycle activities and deliverables varies from company to company. This Guide does not use traditional pharmaceutical process validation terminology such as IQ/OQ/PQ to describe system life cycle activities. This aligns with the US FDA, who also chose not to use the terminology in General Principles of Software Validation because the terminology may not be well understood among many software professionals. Such terminology implies an inherently linear approach.

Whatever terminology is used for verification activity, the overriding requirement is that the regulated company can demonstrate that the system is compliant and fit for intended use.

Traditional TermDescriptionGAMP 5 Verification Activity
DQ
Design Qualification		 Documented verification that the proposed design of facilities, systems, and equipment is suitable for the intended purpose Design review
IQ
Installation Qualification		 Documented verification that a system is installed according to written and approved specifications Checking, testing, or other verification to demonstrate correct installation of software/hardware and configuration
OQ
Operational Qualification		 Documented verification that a system operates according to written and approved specifications throughout specified operating ranges Testing or other verification of the system against specifications to demonstrate correct operation of functionality supporting the specific business process
PQ
Performance Qualification		 Documented verification that a system is capable of performing the activities of the processes it is required to perform, within the scope of the business process and operating environment Testing or other verification of the system to demonstrate fitness for intended use and to allow acceptance against specified requirements

4.2.6.4 術語對應解析

為什麼 GAMP 5 要放棄 IQ/OQ/PQ 術語？

傳統的 IQ/OQ/PQ 術語有幾個根本問題：

  • 隱含線性假設：IQ → OQ → PQ 的順序暗示驗證只能按照這個固定順序進行，與 Agile 方法不相容
  • 跨界溝通障礙：IT 工程師和軟體供應商不理解這些術語，溝通摩擦大
  • 誤導重點：許多藥廠把重點放在「完成 IQ/OQ/PQ 文件」，而非「確認系統適合用途」

實務轉換：如何在現有 GMP 體系中使用這個觀念？

很多監管機構和公司的 SOP 仍然使用 IQ/OQ/PQ 術語。GAMP 5 不是要你立刻廢除這些術語，而是要你理解：

  • IQ 的本質 = 確認安裝和組態設定正確（不一定需要一份叫做「IQ Protocol」的文件）
  • OQ 的本質 = 確認系統在規定操作範圍內運行符合規格
  • PQ 的本質 = 確認系統在實際業務環境中適合預定用途

如果你的公司的 SOP 要求做 IQ/OQ/PQ，可以繼續用這個框架，但在規劃時用 GAMP 5 的批判性思維決定每個部分要做多深。

FAT / SAT 的角色

GAMP 5 提到 Factory Acceptance Testing (FAT) 和 Site Acceptance Testing (SAT) 是受監管公司在正式放行前的驗收活動。重點原則：查驗活動不應不必要地重複。

如果供應商已在工廠做了充分的 FAT，受監管公司到現場後的 SAT 可以聚焦在安裝確認和現場特定條件的測試，而不是把 FAT 的所有測試案例在現場重跑一遍。

Phase 3: OPERATION

4.3 Operation

This section provides guidance on system operation. Not all the activities will be directly relevant to all systems. The approach and required activities should be selected and scaled according to the nature, risk, and complexity of the system in question through the application of critical thinking.

Once the system has been accepted and released for use, there is a need to maintain compliance and fitness for intended use throughout its operational life. This is achieved by the use of established and up-to-date procedures and training that cover use, maintenance, and management.

The operational phase of a system may last many years, and may include changes to services, software, hardware, the business process, and regulatory requirements. The integrity of the system and its data should be maintained at all times and verified as part of periodic review.

Change management should provide a dependable mechanism for prompt implementation of technically sound improvements following the approach to specification, design, and verification described in this Guide. The rigor of the approach, including the extent of documentation and verification, should be based on the risk and complexity of the change through the application of critical thinking.

Key operational process groups (Table 4.2):

  • Handover
  • Service Management and System Monitoring
  • Incident and Problem Management, Deviation, and CAPA
  • Configuration Management
  • Audits and Review (Periodic Review)
  • Continuity Management (Backup, BCP, Disaster Recovery)
  • Security and System Administration
  • Records Management
階段三：操作期

4.3 操作階段解析

操作階段：最長且最容易被忽視的階段

操作階段通常是整個系統生命週期中持續時間最長的——一個 SCADA 或 LIMS 系統的操作期可長達10-15年。然而在許多藥廠，驗證工作完成後，合規關注度就大幅下降。

GAMP 5 的立場是：操作階段的合規維護與初始驗證同等重要。維持合規的核心機制是有效的操作程序、培訓、變更管理和定期審查。

CDMO 情境：SCADA 系統的操作階段管理

你的 CDMO 已有一套 SCADA 系統控制無菌灌裝線三年了。操作階段的典型事件：

  • 供應商推送軟體更新（需要走變更控制，評估衝擊）
  • 新增一台灌裝頭（需要重新評估並驗證相關功能）
  • 電腦崩潰，需要重裝（備份與還原程序是否驗證過？）
  • 年度定期審查（確認系統仍符合現行法規要求）

操作階段的八大流程群組

GAMP 5 Table 4.2 列出了操作階段的主要流程群組，每個都有對應的附錄（O1-O13）。這不是說每個系統都要建立所有這些流程，而是根據系統的風險和複雜度選擇適用的項目。

4.3.1 Handover

Handover is the process for transfer of responsibility of a computerized system from a project team or a service group to the operations team or a new service group. The support group should be involved at the earliest opportunity to ensure effective knowledge transfer and establishment of operational procedures. A period of elevated support and maintenance, often referred to as Hypercare Services, may be arranged to facilitate the transfer.

4.3.3 Incident and Problem Management and CAPA

The incident management process aims to categorize incidents to direct them to the most appropriate resource or complementary process to achieve a timely resolution; whereas problem management involves analyzing root causes and preventing incidents from happening in the future.

There should be a procedure defining how problems related to software, hardware, and procedures should be captured, reviewed, prioritized, progressed, escalated, and closed.

CAPA is a process for investigating, understanding, and correcting discrepancies based on root-cause analysis, while attempting to prevent their recurrence. In the operational environment the CAPA process should feed into the overall CAPA system used for GxP operations.

4.3.4 Change Management

Change management is a critical activity that is fundamental to maintaining the proper functioning and controlled status of systems and processes. All changes that are proposed during the operational phase of a computerized system, whether related to software (including middleware), hardware, infrastructure, or use of the system, should be subject to a formal change-control process.

This process should ensure that proposed changes are appropriately reviewed to assess impact and risk. Regression analysis and regression testing may be required. The process should ensure that changes are suitably evaluated, authorized, documented, tested, and approved before implementation, and subsequently closed.

Configuration management includes those activities necessary to precisely define a computerized system at any point during its life cycle. Configuration items should only be modified by application of a change management process.

4.3 關鍵操作流程解析

Incident vs. Problem：兩個不同的管理流程

這組概念來自 ITIL（IT 服務管理框架）：

  • Incident Management（事件管理）：目標是「最快速度恢復服務」。例如 LIMS 突然當機，IT 重啟服務，系統恢復——這是 Incident 管理，重點是速度。
  • Problem Management（問題管理）：目標是「找到根因，防止再發」。同一台 LIMS 每個月都當機一次，這是 Problem，需要深入調查根因（資料庫索引效率？記憶體洩漏？）並解決。

在 GMP 環境中，Incident 需要記錄（偏差記錄），Problem 需要 CAPA。兩者要連動。

變更控制：與 GMP 設施變更控制的連結

GAMP 5 要求：所有電腦化系統的軟硬體、基礎設施、使用方式的變更，都必須走正式的變更控制流程（change-control process）。

這與 GMP 廠房的變更控制 SOP 是同一個邏輯框架。在 CDMO 中，電腦化系統的變更控制應整合到廠區統一的變更控制體系中，而非孤立運作。

關鍵要求：變更在實施前必須完成評估、授權、文件記錄、測試和審核。這意味著緊急變更也要有後補記錄機制，不能以「緊急」為由跳過文件要求。

組態項目（Configuration Item）概念

Configuration Item（CI）是系統中在正常操作下不應改變的組件。例如：

  • LIMS 的版本號和安裝包
  • 資料庫的 schema 設計
  • 系統設定參數檔
  • 整合介面的 API 定義

任何 CI 的變更都必須通過變更管理流程——不能直接在生產環境手動修改設定，然後事後補記錄。

4.3.5 Periodic Review

Periodic reviews are used throughout the operational life of systems to verify that they remain compliant with regulatory requirements, fit for intended use, and meet company policies and procedures, including those related to data integrity. Periodic reviews should be:

  • Scheduled at an interval appropriate to the impact and operational history of the system. Risk and other assessments should be used to determine which systems are in scope and the frequency of periodic review.
  • Performed in accordance with a predefined process
  • Documented with corrective actions tracked to satisfactory completion

4.3.6 Continuity Management

4.3.6.1 Backup and Restore: Processes and procedures should be established to ensure that backup copies of software, records, and data are made, maintained, and retained for a defined period within safe and secure areas. Restore procedures should be established, tested, and the results of that testing documented.

4.3.6.2 Business Continuity Planning (BCP): A series of related activities ensuring that an organization is fully prepared to respond effectively in the event of failures and disruptions. Critical business processes and systems should be identified, and the risks to each assessed. Plans should be established and exercised to ensure timely and effective resumption. Plans should be prioritized based on patient and business risk, in case of disruption to multiple systems.

4.3.6.3 Disaster Recovery Planning: A subset of BCP, plans should be specified, approved, and rehearsed for the recovery of specific systems in the event of a disaster. Disaster Recovery (DR) plans often require a shared responsibility model between internal organizations and external service providers (e.g., cloud service providers).

4.3.7 Security Management

Computerized systems and data should be adequately protected against willful or accidental loss, damage, or unauthorized change. Role-based security should be implemented. Security provisions should ensure that data is protected against unauthorized intrusions including cyber security attacks. Intrusion prevention and detection processes should be in place.

4.3.5–4.3.8 定期審查、持續運作與安全管理

定期審查的頻率：沒有固定答案

GAMP 5 沒有規定「每年一次」或「每兩年一次」，而是要求根據以下因素決定頻率：

  • 系統對患者安全和產品品質的影響程度
  • 系統的操作歷史（有沒有頻繁出現問題？）
  • 法規環境是否有變化

高風險系統（如直接控制無菌製程的 SCADA）可能需要每年審查；低風險的 HR 系統可能三年一次就足夠。

備份與還原：最容易被忽略的 GMP 要求

幾乎所有 IT 系統都有備份排程，但在 GMP 環境中，備份還原程序必須被測試，且測試結果要記錄。

常見問題：「我們有每天備份，但從來沒有試過從備份還原。」這在 GMP 環境中是不合規的——因為沒有測試過的程序，不能確保它能在緊急情況下正常運作。

BCP 的優先順序邏輯

當多個系統同時發生故障時，BCP 需要明確的優先順序。GAMP 5 要求基於患者風險和業務風險來排序。

CDMO 的典型優先順序：

  1. 批次記錄系統（直接影響產品放行決策）
  2. SCADA/製程控制系統（影響生產連續性）
  3. LIMS（影響放行測試）
  4. ERP/採購系統（影響業務，但可短期手動作業）
Phase 4: RETIREMENT

4.4 Retirement

This activity covers system withdrawal, system decommissioning, system disposal, and migration of required data.

4.4.1 Withdrawal

Withdrawal is the removal of the system from active operation, i.e., users are deactivated, interfaces disabled. No data should be added to the system from this point forward. Special access should be retained for data reporting, results analysis, and support.

4.4.2 Decommissioning

Decommissioning is a controlled process by which an application or system is removed from use in an organization once it has been retired and/or has become obsolete.

4.4.3 Disposal

Data, documentation, software, or hardware may be permanently destroyed. Each may reach this stage at a different time. Data and documentation may not be disposed of until they have reached the end of the record-retention period, as specified in the company's record-retention policy, following an authorized and documented process.

Consideration should be given to:

  • Establishing procedures covering system retirement, including withdrawal, decommissioning, and disposal as appropriate
  • Documentary evidence to be retained of actions taken during retirement of the system
  • GxP records to be maintained, their required retention periods, and which records can be destroyed
  • The need to migrate records to a new system or archive, and the method of verifying and documenting this process
  • Ability to retrieve these migrated records on the new system

4.4.4 Data Migration

Data migration may be required when an existing system is replaced by a new system, when an operational system experiences a significant change, or when the scope of use of a system is changed. The migration process should be accurate, complete, and verified.

階段四：退役期

4.4 退役階段解析

退役的三個步驟

GAMP 5 將退役拆解為三個概念上不同的步驟：

  • Withdrawal（撤除）：停止使用——用戶帳號停用、介面切斷、不再寫入新資料。但系統可能還在線上，供查閱歷史資料。
  • Decommissioning（除役）：受控地移除系統——從基礎設施中卸除，包含硬體和軟體層面的移除。
  • Disposal（銷毀）：永久刪除資料或銷毀硬體。注意：GxP 記錄必須等到記錄保留期限到期後才能銷毀。

CDMO 情境：舊 MES 退役

假設你的 CDMO 要用新的 MES 取代已用10年的舊 MES：

  • 撤除：切換至新 MES 後，舊 MES 禁止新批次建立，但保留查閱舊批次記錄的能力
  • 資料遷移：決定哪些歷史批次記錄要遷移到新系統？哪些保留在歸檔系統？遷移的準確性和完整性需要被驗證
  • 除役：確認記錄保留期限要求（通常批次記錄保留期為產品有效期 + 1 年或最低 5 年），滿足後才能進行伺服器下線
  • 銷毀：依資料安全要求，確保敏感資料的安全銷毀並留存記錄

資料遷移的三個驗證要求

GAMP 5 要求資料遷移必須是：

  • Accurate（準確）：遷移後的資料與原資料一致
  • Complete（完整）：所有應遷移的記錄都已遷移，無遺漏
  • Verified（已查驗）：上述兩點需要有文件化的確認活動

資料遷移是數據完整性（Data Integrity）的重大風險點。一旦資料在遷移中損壞或遺失，且未被發現，可能影響未來的批次回顧、趨勢分析或法規查詢。

Chapter Summary — Key Takeaways

  • Life cycle = 4 phases: Concept → Project → Operation → Retirement. Each phase has defined activities; the operation phase is typically the longest.
  • Specification & verification is not linear: GAMP 5 explicitly supports Agile, iterative, and incremental approaches alongside the traditional V-model.
  • CSV framework is built on system-specific validation plans and reports, with scalable rigor based on risk, complexity, and novelty — not on document count.
  • Critical thinking is a continuous mindset across all phases: consider multiple layers of assurance, avoid unnecessary paperwork, and document the rationale for your decisions.
  • IQ/OQ/PQ → GAMP 5 activities: DQ ≈ Design Review; IQ ≈ Installation/configuration verification; OQ ≈ Functional/operational testing; PQ ≈ Fitness-for-use acceptance testing.
  • Operation phase requires formal change control for all changes, periodic reviews, incident/problem management with CAPA integration, backup/restore testing, and security management.
  • Retirement is a controlled process: withdrawal → decommissioning → disposal, with data migration verified for accuracy and completeness.

章節摘要 — 核心要點

  • 生命週期 = 4個階段：概念→專案→操作→退役。操作階段通常持續最長，但合規管理要求最易被忽視。
  • 查驗方法多元化：V-model 只是眾多可接受方法之一；Agile 迭代方法在 GAMP 5 框架下完全合規。
  • 批判性思維貫穿全生命週期：合規程度與文件數量無關，與控制的針對性和有效性有關。多層保證思維是評估風險的核心工具。
  • 分類（Cat. 3/4/5）是起點，不是終點：實際驗證深度還要考慮 GxP 影響程度、供應商能力和系統新穎性。
  • 操作階段四大支柱：變更管理（所有變更走變更控制）、定期審查（依風險決定頻率）、CAPA 整合、業務持續計畫（BCP + DR + 備份還原測試）。
  • 退役不是簡單地關機：需要規劃記錄保留期、資料遷移驗證、安全銷毀，並留存退役活動的文件證據。
2

Section 2: Ch5-8: QRM, Regulated Company, Supplier & Efficiency

品質風險管理、法規公司與供應商活動 | p49-p84

ISPE GAMP 5 2nd Edition | Section 02a | Doc p49–p68

Learning Objectives  |  學習目標

  1. Explain the five-step QRM process defined in GAMP 5 and how it links to ICH Q9 principles — and how this changes from checkbox compliance to science-based validation strategy. 解釋 GAMP 5 的五步驟 QRM 流程及其與 ICH Q9 原則的連結，理解如何從勾選式法規遵循轉為科學基礎的驗證策略。
  2. Distinguish between process-level risk assessment and system-level functional risk assessment, and know when each applies. 區分流程層級風險評估與系統層級功能風險評估，並了解各自的適用時機。
  3. Describe the governance elements required for a robust computerized system compliance program, including policy, roles, inventory, and planning. 描述穩健電腦化系統合規計畫所需的治理要素，包含政策、職責、系統清單與驗證規劃。
  4. Identify the key roles (Process Owner, System Owner, Quality Unit, SME, Supplier, End User) and their specific responsibilities in the CSV life cycle. 辨識關鍵角色（流程負責人、系統負責人、品保單位、SME、供應商、使用者）及其在 CSV 生命週期中的具體職責。
  5. Map the 12 system-specific activities in Table 6.1 to a practical CDMO validation program, including how supplier data reduces in-house testing burden. 將 Table 6.1 的 12 項系統專屬活動對應至實際 CDMO 驗證計畫，包含如何運用供應商資料降低內部測試負擔。
  6. Apply the concept of system inventory and categorization to determine appropriate validation depth for any given GxP system. 運用系統清單與分類概念，為任何 GxP 系統決定適當的驗證深度。

Chapter 5: Quality Risk Management (Doc p49–p55)

5.1 Overview

QRM is a systematic process for the assessment, control, communication, and review of risks. It is an iterative process used throughout the computerized system life cycle from concept to retirement.

For a given organization, a framework for making risk-management decisions should be defined to ensure consistency of application across systems and business functions. Terminology should be agreed upon, particularly regarding definitions and metrics for key risk factors.

Such a framework is most effectively implemented when it is incorporated into the overall QMS and is fully integrated with the system life cycle.

Scope Note

This chapter is primarily aimed at new computerized systems. It does not imply that formal risk assessments are required for all existing systems. The extent of risk management required for existing systems should be considered as part of periodic review.

This chapter focuses on software products and custom applications rather than on infrastructure.

5.1 概覽 — 解讀與應用

QRM 是什麼？為什麼重要？

品質風險管理（QRM）不是一份要填完的表格，而是一個貫穿電腦化系統整個生命週期的決策框架。它回答的核心問題是：「這個系統需要多少驗證？」

對 CDMO 而言，這個問題每天都在發生——新的 LIMS 模組、新的環境監控系統、更新的 ERP 配置——QRM 框架讓每個決策有據可查，而非憑感覺或「以前都這樣」。

比喻：QRM 是「工程前的地圖」

想像蓋廠房前先進行地質調查——不是為了找麻煩，而是為了知道哪裡需要加強基礎、哪裡可以省料。QRM 對電腦化系統的作用完全相同：讓驗證資源集中在真正有風險的地方。

重要範圍限制

本章僅針對新系統，現有系統的風險管理程度應在定期審查中決定。這代表你不需要回頭對所有舊系統重做正式 RA，但定期審查時必須評估是否需要補做。

5.2 Science-Based Quality Risk Management

Determining the risks posed by a computerized system requires a common and shared understanding of:

  • Impact of the computerized system on patient safety, product quality, and data integrity
  • Supported business processes
  • CQAs for systems that monitor or control CPPs
  • User requirements
  • Regulatory requirements
  • Project approach (contracts, methods, timelines)
  • System components and architecture
  • System functions
  • Supplier capability

The organization also should consider other applicable risks, such as Health, Safety, and Environment (HSE).

Managing the risks may be achieved by:

  • Elimination by design — modifying processes or system design
  • Reduction to an acceptable level — applying controls to lower severity, decrease probability, or increase detectability
  • Verification — demonstrating that risks are managed to an acceptable level

It is desirable to eliminate risk, if possible, by modifying processes or system design. Design reviews can play a key role in eliminating risk by design.

A systematic approach should be defined to verify that the risk associated with a system has been managed to an acceptable level. The overall extent of verification and the level of detail of documentation should be based on the risk to patient safety, product quality, and data integrity, and take into account the complexity and novelty of the system.

The criticality of a business process is independent of whether it is manually processed, semi-automated, or fully automated. Systems that support critical processes include those that:

  • Generate, manipulate, or control data supporting regulatory safety and efficacy submissions
  • Control critical parameters and data in pre-clinical, clinical, development, and manufacturing
  • Control or provide data or information for product release
  • Control data or information required in case of product recall
  • Control adverse event or complaint recording or reporting
  • Support pharmacovigilance

5.2 科學基礎 QRM — 解讀與應用

「科學基礎」的真正意涵

GAMP 5 特別強調 science-based，是在對抗一種常見的壞習慣：把 QRM 當成「文件遊戲」——填完表格、蓋章，但完全不理解系統實際風險。

科學基礎 QRM 要求你真正理解：這個系統控制的是什麼 CPP？影響的是哪個 CQA？如果資料失真，對病患有什麼後果？

三種風險控制策略的優先順序

GAMP 5 明確排出優先順序，設計消除 > 控制降低 > 驗證確認。這對 CDMO 非常實用：

  • 設計消除：例如設定系統欄位限制，讓使用者根本無法輸入不合理的數值，比事後審查更可靠。
  • 控制降低：SOP、電子簽章、警報機制——降低發生機率或提升可偵測性。
  • 驗證確認：最後才是 IQ/OQ/PQ，用來證明前兩層控制確實有效。

「業務流程的嚴重性 ≠ 自動化程度」

GAMP 5 強調：無論是手工操作、半自動還是全自動，只要業務流程影響病患安全，就是關鍵流程。這意味著即使是一個「只是顯示數字」的老舊系統，若那個數字影響放行決策，它就是 GxP 系統，需要納入管理。

CDMO 實務：哪些系統最常被忽略？

  • 環境監控系統（EM）——數據直接進批次記錄
  • 稱量系統/天平介面——直接影響配方準確性
  • 冷鏈溫度記錄系統——支援放行決策
  • Excel 巨集——常被視為「不是系統」，但功能上完全是

5.3 Quality Risk Management Process

The ICH Q9 describes a systematic approach to QRM intended for general application within the pharmaceutical industry. It defines two primary principles:

"The evaluation of the risk to quality should be based on scientific knowledge and ultimately link to the protection of the patient; and the level of effort, formality and documentation of the quality risk-management process should be commensurate with the level of risk."

In the context of computerized systems, scientific knowledge is based upon the system specifications and the business process being supported.

Key ICH Q9 Terms Used in This Guide

  • Harm: Damage to health, including the damage that can occur from loss of product quality or availability.
  • Hazard: The potential source of harm.
  • Risk: The combination of the probability of occurrence of harm and the severity of that harm.
  • Severity: A measure of the possible consequences of a hazard.

Process Risk Assessment

QRM activities should start at the business process level, at a level higher than individual systems. A process risk assessment (also known as business process risk assessment) is a non-system-specific high-level assessment of the business process or data flow, which may occur before system-specific QRM activities.

The process risk assessment is aimed at identifying key high-level risks to patient safety, product quality, and data integrity, and identifying the required controls to manage those risks. Typical inputs include:

  • Defined business process scope
  • Process descriptions and/or diagrams
  • Identified regulatory requirements for the proposed process scope
  • Identified company quality requirements

Five-Step QRM Process

This Guide applies the general principles of ICH Q9 to describe a five-step process for risk management as an integral part of achieving and maintaining system compliance.

This process applies during the project phase. Examples of application include: determining the need for supplier audit, determining the rigor and extent of testing, determining corrective actions from test failures, determining impact of proposed changes, and determining the frequency of periodic reviews.

Step 1 – Perform Initial Risk Assessment and Determine System Impact

An initial risk assessment should be performed based on business processes and business risk assessments, user requirements, regulatory requirements, and known functional areas.
