The results should include a decision on whether the system is GxP regulated (i.e., GxP assessment) and an overall assessment of system impact.

A system cannot have a higher impact than the business process it supports.

Step 2 – Identify Functions with Impact on Patient Safety, Product Quality, and Data Integrity

Functions that have an impact on patient safety, product quality, and data integrity should be identified by building on information gathered during Step 1, referring to relevant specifications, and considering project approach, system architecture, and categorization of system components.

Individual functions cannot have a higher impact than the system as a whole.

Step 3 – Perform Functional Risk Assessments and Identify Controls

Functions identified during Step 2 should be assessed by considering possible hazards, and how the potential harm arising from these hazards may be controlled. A more detailed assessment may analyze severity of harm, likelihood of occurrence, and probability of detection.

Criteria to consider include: criticality of the supported process, specific impact of the function within the process, and nature of the system (e.g., complexity and novelty).

Appropriate controls include, but are not limited to:

  • Modification of process design
  • Modification of system design
  • Application of external procedures
  • Increasing the detail or formality of specifications
  • Increasing the number and level of detail of design reviews
  • Increasing the extent or rigor of verification activities

Step 4 – Implement and Verify Appropriate Controls

The control measures identified in Step 3 should be implemented and verified to ensure that they have been successfully implemented. Controls should be traceable to the relevant identified risks. The effort, formality, and documentation of the verification activity should be commensurate with the level of risk.

Step 5 – Review Risks and Monitor Controls

During periodic review of systems, or at other defined points, an organization should review the risks and verify that controls are still effective. The organization should consider whether:

  • Previously unrecognized hazards are present
  • Previously identified hazards are no longer applicable
  • The estimated risk associated with a hazard is no longer acceptable
  • The original assessment is otherwise invalidated (e.g., following changes to applicable regulations or change of system use)

The frequency and extent of any periodic review should be based on the level of risk and should consider previous findings and operational history.

5.3 五步驟 QRM 流程 — 解讀與應用

ICH Q9 的兩條核心原則解讀

第一條：風險評估要基於科學知識，最終目的是保護病患。注意這裡說的是「最終」——不是保護公司、不是通過查廠，而是病患。

第二條：投入的力度、正式程度、文件詳細程度，要與風險等級相稱。這是 GAMP 5 反對「一視同仁驗證」的理論基礎：低風險系統少做，高風險系統多做。

流程風險評估 vs. 系統功能風險評估

流程 RA 在系統選型前就應進行，評估的是「這個業務流程的風險」，不假設任何系統的存在。例如：無菌灌裝的環境監控流程，本身就是高風險，不管用什麼系統都一樣。

系統功能 RA 才是具體評估「這個系統的哪些功能有影響」。先有流程 RA，才能正確定位系統 RA 的範圍。

五步驟流程的 CDMO 對應

GAMP 5 步驟CDMO 實際作業
Step 1: 初始 RA & GxP 判定系統清單審查、GxP 影響評估表
Step 2: 辨識關鍵功能功能影響評估（FIA）
Step 3: 功能 RA & 控制措施詳細 RA 表格（FMEA/Risk Matrix）
Step 4: 實施並驗證控制IQ/OQ/PQ 測試、SOP 發行
Step 5: 定期審查風險週期性審查（Periodic Review）

Step 1 的關鍵限制：系統不能超過流程

「A system cannot have a higher impact than the business process it supports.」

這條規則意義重大：如果一個業務流程本身就不是 GxP 關鍵，那麼支援它的系統就不需要 GxP 驗證。反之，流程是關鍵的，系統就必須驗證。這是判斷驗證必要性的第一道防線。

Step 5 的重要性常被低估

定期審查風險不只是「確認舊 RA 還有效」，GAMP 5 要求主動評估：

  • 是否出現了以前沒識別到的新危害？（系統升級後常見）
  • 法規有無更新導致舊評估失效？（例如 Annex 11 修訂）
  • 某些風險是否已不再適用，可以放寬控制措施？

最後一點最常被忽略——GAMP 5 明確允許在審查後降低原有控制的嚴格程度，這是風險比例原則的體現。

Chapter 6: Regulated Company Activities (Doc p55–p68)

6.1 Governance for Achieving Compliance

Responsibility for the compliance of computerized systems lies with the regulated company. This involves activities at both the organizational level and at the level of individual systems.

Achieving robust, cost-effective compliance requires strong governance. Key elements of successful governance include:

  • Establishing computerized systems compliance policies and procedures
  • Identifying clear roles and responsibilities
  • Training
  • Managing supplier relationships
  • Maintaining a system inventory
  • Planning for validation
  • Continual improvement activities
  • Data governance

Effective governance is achieved by integrating these activities into the management of the organization.

6.1.1 Computerized Systems Policies and Procedures

Regulated companies should have a defined policy for ensuring that computerized systems are compliant and fit for intended use. The policy should typically include a commitment to:

  • Identify and comply with all applicable GxP requirements
  • Integrate life cycle activities into the regulated company's QMS
  • Identify and assess each system
  • Ensure GxP regulated systems are compliant and fit for intended use according to established SOPs
  • Follow a validation framework, including the use of validation plans and validation reports as necessary
  • Maintain compliance throughout the life of a system

Further details should be documented in SOPs, which may be supplemented by guidance and templates, typically addressing: system inventory, impact assessment, roles/responsibilities, life cycle approach, planning/risk management/specification/verification activities, system operation and management, record and data management, and security management.

6.1.2 Identifying Clear Roles and Responsibilities

Roles and responsibilities for activities should be documented, allocated, and communicated. Key responsibilities include:

  • Defining, approving, and maintaining policies and SOPs
  • Compiling and prioritizing the system inventory
  • Producing plans and reports
  • Managing compliance and validation activities
  • Maintaining compliance during operation

6.1.3 Training

Training ensures that persons who develop, validate, maintain, support, or use computerized systems have the education, training, and experience to perform their assigned tasks. A risk-based approach should be used to determine the rigor of training required.

For computerized systems, the regulated company should:

  • Establish the necessary training needs, including users, suppliers, data centers, IT departments, engineering, maintenance
  • Provide training to satisfy these needs
  • Evaluate the effectiveness of the training
  • Ensure that staff are aware of the relevance and importance of their activities (e.g., GxP)
  • Ensure that supplier staff are adequately trained, e.g., as part of supplier assessment
  • Maintain appropriate training records
  • Ensure training is maintained up-to-date, e.g., following system changes

6.1.4 Managing Supplier Relationships

Responsibility for activities may be with the suppliers, but in all cases regulatory accountability lies with the regulated company. The regulated company must have defined roles and responsibilities for acceptance and release of GxP computerized systems.

Even though regulated companies cannot delegate their regulatory accountabilities to a supplier, they may leverage the knowledge, experience, activities, and artifacts of an IT/IS service provider through risk-based assessment, management, and governance processes.

The regulated company should verify, prior to contract placement, that the supplier has adequate expertise and resources to support user requirements and expectations. The most common mechanism is the supplier assessment, which may include an audit depending on risk, complexity, and novelty.

6.1.5 Maintaining the System Inventory

Regulated companies should maintain an inventory of computerized systems, showing those that are GxP regulated. The inventory should provide summary information such as the validation status, ownership, impact, current system version, and supplier. Automated equipment may be listed separately and duplication should be avoided.

The inventory should be at the level of systems that support business processes, rather than individual items of hardware. The system inventory may be used for planning periodic reviews.

6.1.6 Planning for Validation

Computerized system validation within a business unit is typically performed using a hierarchical framework of plans covering GxP regulated computerized systems. Computerized system validation plans describe how to ensure compliance and fitness for intended use of specific systems, and specify scope, approach, resources, roles and responsibilities, and the types and extent of activities, tasks, and deliverables.

6.1.7 Continual Improvement Activities

Understanding the effectiveness of current processes is best gained by considering current levels of conformance (e.g., established by audit and trending performance), by reviewing current processes against recognized good practices, and applying critical thinking.

Metrics may be gathered throughout the system life cycle, including:

  • Design and development metrics (e.g., from design and code reviews)
  • Testing metrics (e.g., from analysis of test failures and resulting actions)
  • Operation and maintenance metrics (e.g., from incident management, change management, backup and restore)

6.1.8 Data Governance

"The arrangements to ensure that data, irrespective of the format in which they are generated, are recorded, processed, retained and used to ensure the record throughout the data lifecycle."

Data governance encompasses the people, processes, and technology required to achieve consistent, accurate, and effective data handling. It provides the structure within which appropriate decisions regarding data-related matters may be made according to agreed models, principles, processes, and defined authority.

6.1 治理框架 — 解讀與應用

治理（Governance）是 CSV 程序的「骨架」

GAMP 5 Chapter 6 分成兩層：組織層治理（6.1）和系統層活動（6.2）。許多公司跳過 6.1 直接做 6.2，結果每個專案都在重新發明輪子，缺乏一致性，查廠時被觀察到「缺乏系統性」。

好的治理意味著：即使換了人，下一個人拿起 SOP 就能按相同標準執行。

CDMO 的關鍵問題：誰擁有 CSV 計畫？

在許多 CDMO，CSV 計畫的歸屬是個灰色地帶：

  • 品保（QA）：知道法規要求，但不懂技術細節
  • IT：懂系統，但不懂 GxP 思維
  • 工程：懂設備，但不懂資料完整性

GAMP 5 的答案是：法規責任永遠在受法規規範的公司（品保主導），但執行必須跨部門協作。實務上，最有效的模式是由品保設定政策和最低標準，IT/工程按政策執行，並定期向品保報告。

6.1.3 訓練的風險比例原則

訓練本身也要做 QRM：高風險系統的使用者訓練要更嚴格、評估更完整、記錄更詳細。低風險系統（例如辦公室文書工具）則可簡化。

常見錯誤：對所有系統一律要求相同的訓練格式和紀錄，既浪費資源，又難以執行。

6.1.4 供應商關係：「不能外包責任」

這是 GxP 鐵律：不管你把系統建置、維護、甚至資料中心全部外包，法規責任永遠留在你這裡。GAMP 5 用的詞是 "regulatory accountability cannot be delegated"。

但你可以善用供應商的能力來降低你的驗證工作量——這是允許的，也是推薦的做法（透過供應商評估確認其 QMS 品質後）。

6.1.5 系統清單：CSV 的「資產地圖」

系統清單聽起來簡單，但實際上是 CSV 程序最容易失控的地方。以下是常見問題：

  • 清單不完整——有系統在跑但沒被列入
  • 清單不更新——系統版本、負責人已變但清單沒改
  • 清單過細——把每台 PC 都列進去，難以管理

GAMP 5 明確說清單應在「支援業務流程的系統」層級，不是硬體元件層級。一套 LIMS 是一筆記錄，而不是每個工作站一筆。

6.1.8 資料治理：超越電腦化系統的概念

資料治理涵蓋人、流程、技術——這意味著即使沒有電腦系統，資料治理依然存在。一份紙本批次記錄的產生、審核、保存方式，都屬於資料治理的範疇。

GAMP 5 把資料治理列為組織治理的一環，強調它不是 IT 部門的職責，而是全組織的責任。

6.2 System-Specific Activities

Table 6.1 shows the typical regulated company activities required for a configurable computerized system. Note: This table is indicative only. Activities required for a specific system should be determined based on risk, complexity, and novelty, by applying critical thinking.

Table 6.1: Typical Activities for a Configurable Computerized System

Step Task Description
1 Identify Compliance Standards Compliance activities should be performed in accordance with applicable company policies and procedures.
2 Identify System The system should be added to an inventory of systems in accordance with documented procedures.
3 Identify Key Individuals These include Process Owner, System Owner, Quality Unit, SME, Supplier, End User.
4 Produce Requirements Specification (RS) The RS should define clearly and precisely what the regulated company wants the system to do, state any constraints, and define regulatory and documentation requirements.
5 Determine Strategy (Risk Assessment, System Assessment, Supplier Assessment) Initial risk assessment during planning; system components assessed for architecture/complexity/novelty; supplier quality capability formally assessed.
6 Plan Activities, deliverables, procedures, and responsibilities defined in a plan.
7 Review and Approve Specifications Regulated company reviews and approves specifications as appropriate. Design reviews may be used.
8 Develop Test Strategy Determine what testing is required after considering existing documentation available. Depth and rigor consider intended use, impact, and risk.
9 Test Ensure testing defined in the test strategy is completed and ensure review of test results.
10 Report and Release Report provides evidence all planned deliverables and activities are complete and system is fit for intended use. Formal process for release to operational use.
11 Maintain System Compliance During Operation Establish adequate system management and operational procedures.
12 System Retirement Manage the withdrawal of the computerized system from use, including migration of data to a new system, if applicable.

6.2 系統專屬活動 — 解讀與應用

Table 6.1：GAMP 5 的「驗證路線圖」

這張 12 步驟表格是 GAMP 5 第二版最實用的工具之一。它把一個完整的 CSV 計畫濃縮成一個清單，適合用來規劃驗證專案、識別遺漏的活動、或向管理層說明 CSV 工作量。

重要提醒：GAMP 5 說這是「指示性的」——不是每個系統都需要做完所有 12 步。步驟的深度和正式程度要根據風險、複雜度、新穎度來決定。

12 步驟與 CDMO 實際驗證工作的對應

步驟CDMO 文件／活動
1 合規標準VMP 政策、SOP for CSV
2 辨識系統系統清單登錄表
3 確認關鍵人員驗證計畫中的職責矩陣（RACI）
4 需求規格URS（使用者需求規格）
5 合規策略System Assessment + Supplier Assessment
6 計畫Validation Plan（VP）
7 審查規格FS/CS/DS 審查記錄
8 測試策略Test Strategy / Test Plan
9 測試IQ / OQ / PQ 執行記錄
10 報告 & 放行Validation Summary Report
11 維持合規CC / PR / IM / CAPA SOP
12 系統退役Retirement Plan + 資料移轉紀錄

6.2.3 Key Roles and Responsibilities

6.2.3.1 Process Owner

The process owner is ultimately responsible for ensuring that the computerized system and its operation are in compliance and fit for intended use in accordance with applicable SOPs. Process owners are typically the head of the functional unit using the system. Specific activities include:

  • Approving key documentation as defined by plans and SOPs
  • Providing adequate resources (personnel and financial) to support development and operation
  • Ensuring adequate training for end users
  • Ensuring that SOPs required for the operation of the system exist, are followed, and are reviewed periodically
  • Ensuring changes are approved and managed
  • Reviewing assessment/audit reports and taking appropriate actions to ensure GxP compliance
  • Coordinating input from other groups (e.g., finance, information security, HSE, legal)

6.2.3.2 System Owner

The system owner is responsible for the availability, support, maintenance, and security of a system. For systems supporting regulated processes, the ownership of the data resides with the GxP process owner, not the system owner. The system owner acts on behalf of the users. Specific activities include:

  • Approving key documentation as defined by plans and SOPs
  • Ensuring SOPs for maintenance exist, are followed, and reviewed periodically
  • Ensuring adequate training for maintenance and support staff
  • Ensuring changes are managed
  • Ensuring availability of information for the system inventory and configuration management
  • Managing the system life cycle, including upgrade and replacement planning
  • Ensuring that data integrity risks are identified and controlled

6.2.3.3–6.2.3.5 Quality Unit (Corporate & Operational)

The quality unit provides an independent role in:

  • Approving or auditing key documentation (policies, procedures, acceptance criteria, plans, reports)
  • Focusing on quality critical aspects
  • Approving changes that potentially affect patient safety, product quality, or data integrity
  • Auditing processes to verify that compliance activities are effective

Corporate Quality operates at the corporate level: setting policy, maintaining oversight of company standards, auditing for compliance, reviewing effectiveness of quality systems. Regulatory authorities require independence from business activities.

Operational Quality (division/business unit level): implementing quality standards, reviewing risk assessment and control activities, supporting project phase activities, supporting life cycle processes (change control, document management), managing quality of external service providers. Specific operational quality activities can be delegated to IT departments or engineering departments with their own quality management functions.

6.2.3.6 Subject Matter Expert (SME)

SMEs have a key role in performing reviews and assessments, and taking technical decisions, based on science-based process and product understanding, and sound engineering principles. SMEs should take the lead role in the verification of the computerized system. Responsibilities include planning and defining verification strategies, defining acceptance criteria, selection of appropriate test methods, execution of verification tests, and reviewing results.

6.2.3.7 Supplier

Suppliers (including internal suppliers such as IT or engineering) play an important support role. Specific activities include: provisioning existing documentation, preparing and reviewing documentation, acting as SME for technical aspects, performing and supporting testing, managing changes and configuration, and supporting processes for maintaining system compliance.

6.2.3.8 End User

In addition to using the system in accordance with approved procedures, end users may be involved in: providing input to user requirements, evaluating prototypes, testing, acceptance and handover, developing SOPs for system use, reporting defects, and identifying opportunities for improvement.

6.2.3 關鍵角色 — 解讀與應用

流程負責人 vs. 系統負責人：最常混淆的區別

Process Owner（流程負責人）擁有業務流程的責任，也擁有資料的責任。通常是功能部門主管（例如生產部長、QC 主任）。他對「系統的合規性」負最終責任。

System Owner（系統負責人）擁有系統可用性的責任，通常是 IT 或工程部門。他對「系統能不能跑」負責，但不擁有 GxP 資料。

關鍵：資料所有權（data ownership）屬於 Process Owner，不屬於 System Owner。這在 CDMO 客戶審計時常被查到混淆。

比喻：租屋關係

System Owner 像房東——負責房子的維修和安全。Process Owner 像房客——負責在房子裡的活動符合法規（GxP）。資料（租屋中的財產）屬於房客，不屬於房東。

Corporate Quality vs. Operational Quality

大型製藥公司通常兩者都有，CDMO 規模較小時往往合而為一。但 GAMP 5 強調的原則依然適用：

  • Corporate QA：設政策、做稽核、保持獨立性——不能直接參與驗證執行
  • Operational QA：協助執行、審查文件、同意偏差處理方式

即使你的 QA 只有 3 個人，也應該明確定義誰做哪個角色，否則稽核時說不清楚。

SME 的角色被嚴重低估

GAMP 5 明確說 SME 應該「主導驗證工作」，而非只是被動簽名。這意味著：

  • 測試計畫應由 SME 起草，而非完全外包給供應商
  • 驗收標準（acceptance criteria）必須由 SME 定義
  • 測試執行中的技術判斷由 SME 負責

在 CDMO 中，SME 通常是生產工程師或 QC 科學家，他們的參與深度直接影響驗證品質。

End User 的角色：不只是使用者

GAMP 5 特別點名 End User 可以參與：需求撰寫、原型評估、測試執行、SOP 制定、缺陷回報、改善建議。這是使用者中心設計的 GxP 版本，目的是確保系統「真的適合使用」，而非只是「技術上通過了測試」。

6.2.4–6.2.9: Core System Activities

6.2.4 Requirements Specification (RS)

The RS describes what the system should do. The RS is the responsibility of the regulated company but may be written by a third party or supplier. It should be adequately reviewed by SMEs and approved by the process owner.

6.2.5 Determine Strategy for Achieving Compliance

6.2.5.1 Risk Assessment

An initial risk assessment should be performed during planning to determine whether the system is GxP regulated, the impact of the system, and the need for further risk assessments (described in Chapter 5).

6.2.5.2 Assessment of System Components

The process of assessing system components applies the GAMP software categories and hardware categories as input to establishing the required activities, based on how the system is constructed or configured. This should take into account architecture, complexity, and novelty, including maturity and level of configuration or customization. Categorization should, however, be regarded as only part of the process of defining the required life cycle strategy based on critical thinking.

6.2.5.3 Supplier Assessment and Education

The regulated company should formally assess each supplier to establish their quality capability. The assessment may find that a supplier has a well-established QMS or has attained recognized third-party certification such as ISO 9001. The strategy should take account of assessment conclusions.

If another regulated company has already assessed the supplier for the same reason, then subject to that company agreeing to share that information, an additional assessment may not be necessary. The justification for not assessing a specific supplier should be formally documented.

Regulated companies should be prepared to assist in the education and training of suppliers.

6.2.6 Planning

Planning is an essential activity for any system development and should address all aspects, including activities that demonstrate compliance and fitness for intended use. Since the supplier may provide deliverables or directly support activities, planning provides the opportunity to decide how best to leverage supplier activities and documentation to avoid unnecessary duplication.

6.2.7 System Specifications

Types of specifications may include functional specifications, configuration specifications, and design specifications. In Agile development, types and naming of deliverables may differ. The applicability depends on the specific system and should be defined during planning.

Design Reviews evaluate deliverables against standards and requirements, identify issues, and propose corrective actions. For GAMP Category 3, design reviews by the regulated company are not typically required. For Category 4, focus on configuration and customization. For Category 5, may be conducted at various levels of specification.

6.2.8 Development and Review of Software for Custom Applications

Code reviews by the regulated company are not required for standard and configurable software products. Custom applications and custom software should be developed in accordance with defined standards. The need for and extent of reviews should be based on risk, complexity, and novelty.

6.2.9 Test Strategy and Testing

The regulated company is responsible for ensuring that the test strategy will demonstrate compliance and fitness for intended use. The number and types of tests should be based on risk, complexity, and novelty. The role of the supplier, including use of existing supplier documentation, should be considered when developing the strategy.

The results of testing should be documented against defined acceptance criteria based on specifications. Test failures should be captured, reviewed, documented, and managed.

6.2.4–6.2.9 核心活動 — 解讀與應用

6.2.4 URS：被低估的最重要文件

需求規格（RS/URS）是整個驗證金字塔的基礎。一份模糊的 URS 會導致後續所有測試都失去錨點——測試什麼？驗收標準怎麼定？如何判斷偏差重不重要？

GAMP 5 強調 RS 是受法規規範公司的責任，可以請第三方或供應商起草，但 SME 必須審查、Process Owner 必須核准。不能只是「拿供應商給的文件蓋章」。

6.2.5.2 系統評估：分類不是目的，而是手段

GAMP 軟體分類（Cat 1, 3, 4, 5）是工具，不是終點。GAMP 5 明確說「分類應被視為定義生命週期策略的一部分，而非全部」。

實務含義：一個 Cat 4 的 COTS 系統，如果高度客製化、支援關鍵流程，可能需要接近 Cat 5 的驗證深度。相反，一個技術上是 Cat 5 但風險很低的系統，可以用較輕量的方式驗證。

6.2.5.3 供應商評估：最有槓桿效果的活動

這是 GAMP 5 2nd Edition 最強調的成本效益工具：透過評估供應商的 QMS 品質，直接減少你的內部驗證工作量。

  • 供應商有 ISO 9001 認證 → 開發流程有基本保證
  • 供應商有 SOC 2 報告 → 資訊安全和可用性有第三方評估
  • 其他法規公司已評估過同一供應商 → 可引用其結論（需書面同意）

這些都可以用來減少你的 IQ/OQ 測試範圍，前提是你要在驗證計畫中說清楚你是怎麼利用供應商資料的。

6.2.7 規格文件的 Agile 適應

GAMP 5 2nd Edition 特別提到 Agile 開發——傳統的 FS/DS 文件可能不存在，但核心要求不變：必須有足夠的規格資訊支援驗證，只是呈現形式可以不同（例如 User Stories + Acceptance Criteria）。

6.2.9 測試策略：先看供應商有什麼，再決定自己做什麼

許多 CDMO 的問題是：拿到系統就開始跑 IQ/OQ/PQ，完全不看供應商的測試文件。GAMP 5 的做法是先評估供應商有哪些測試文件，再決定哪些需要自己重做、哪些可以引用。這樣可以避免大量重複測試。

「數量和類型應基於風險、複雜度和新穎度」——這是 GAMP 5 對抗「反射式全測」的核心論述。

6.2.10–6.2.12: Reporting, Operation, and Retirement

6.2.10 Reporting and Release

At the conclusion of the project, a computerized system validation report should be produced summarizing:

  • The activities performed
  • Any deviations from the plan
  • Any outstanding and corrective actions
  • A statement of fitness for intended use of the system

In some cases, specific computerized system validation reports may not be required. Release of the system into the operating environment should be performed in accordance with a controlled and documented process.

6.2.11 Maintaining System Compliance During Operation

The regulated company is responsible for maintaining system compliance during operation. This includes the operational processes described in Section 4.3 of GAMP 5, covering:

  • Change and configuration management
  • Periodic review
  • Incident management
  • Business continuity and disaster recovery
  • Security management
  • Data backup and archiving

6.2.12 System Retirement

System retirement is the managed withdrawal of the computerized system from use. Key considerations include:

  • Migration of data to a new system, if applicable
  • Archiving of data and documentation for the required retention period
  • Ensuring continued accessibility to archived data
  • Decommissioning activities documented and controlled

6.2.10–6.2.12 — 解讀與應用

6.2.10 驗證報告：「Fit for Intended Use」聲明的重要性

驗證總結報告（VSR）的核心是一句聲明：這個系統適合其預期用途。這不只是格式要求，它代表有人對整個驗證過程做了判斷並承擔責任。

報告中未解決的偏差和待完成的 CAPA 必須被記錄，並說明它們不影響系統放行的理由。不能假裝問題不存在。

6.2.11 維持合規：「系統放行後才是真正挑戰的開始」

許多公司把所有資源投入驗證專案，放行後就忽視了維護。GAMP 5 列出的運營活動（變更管理、定期審查、事件管理等）才是系統生命週期中最長的階段，也是最容易失控的地方。

對 CDMO 而言，客戶審計最常查的就是：你的變更管理 SOP 有沒有被遵守？上次定期審查是什麼時候？

6.2.12 系統退役：最容易被忽略的生命週期階段

當新系統上線，舊系統的退役計畫往往沒有人去想。但 GxP 要求：資料必須在法定保留期限內保持可存取性。退役計畫必須回答：

  • 資料移到哪裡？格式是否保持可讀？
  • 保留多久？誰負責保管？
  • 如果稽核需要查五年前的數據，能在合理時間內找到嗎？

Section Summary  |  本節重點摘要

Key English Takeaways

  • QRM is iterative and proportional — not a one-time exercise, and effort must match risk level throughout the life cycle.
  • Process RA precedes system RA — a system cannot have higher impact than the business process it supports.
  • Five QRM steps: Initial RA → Identify critical functions → Functional RA & controls → Implement & verify → Review & monitor.
  • Governance is the foundation — policy, roles, inventory, and validation planning must be in place before system-specific activities.
  • Regulatory accountability cannot be delegated — supplier activities support compliance, but the regulated company remains responsible.
  • Table 6.1 is not prescriptive — apply the 12 steps with critical thinking based on risk, complexity, and novelty of each system.
  • Supplier assessment reduces testing — leveraging supplier QMS data and documentation is encouraged to avoid unnecessary duplication.
  • Data ownership ≠ system ownership — data belongs to the Process Owner, not the System Owner (typically IT).

中文關鍵洞察

  • QRM 是決策框架，不是文件格式 — 目的是讓驗證資源集中在真正有風險的地方，而非均勻分配。
  • 五步驟流程的精髓：先看流程風險 → 再看系統功能 → 找控制措施 → 驗證有效 → 定期審查。
  • 治理是 CSV 程序的骨架 — 沒有政策、清單、職責分工，單個驗證專案做得再好也無法持續。
  • CDMO 最常見缺口：系統清單不完整、Process Owner 與 System Owner 混淆、退役計畫缺失、定期審查形式化。
  • 供應商評估是槓桿工具 — ISO 9001、SOC 2 認證、其他公司的評估結論，都可用來減少內部測試範圍。
  • 科學基礎 QRM 的反面是什麼？ — 不問風險、不看流程、統一套用相同深度的驗證（過度驗證或不足驗證都是問題）。
  • SME 主導驗證 — 不是 QA 主導，不是供應商主導，是懂業務流程和系統的 SME 主導，QA 提供獨立監督。
ISPE GAMP 5 Second Edition | doc p69–p84

Learning Objectives  |  學習目標

  1. Distinguish the three supplier product categories (Cat 3/4/5) and how each changes the scope of supplier involvement in CSV.  區分三類供應商產品（Cat 3/4/5）及各類別對 CSV 範圍的影響。
  2. Describe the 12-step Supplier Good Practices framework (Table 7.1) and map it to your own vendor qualification workflow.  說明 12 步驟供應商良好實踐框架，並對應到自身的廠商資格確認流程。
  3. Explain when sub-supplier assessments are required and why cloud hosting introduces direct compliance risk.  說明次供應商評估的觸發條件，以及雲端託管如何直接影響法規遵循。
  4. Apply the criteria for leveraging supplier documentation to reduce regulated company verification burden, with documented rationale.  套用標準以借用供應商文件，減少受規管公司的驗證負擔，並保留書面依據。
  5. Explain all 9 efficiency improvement strategies and identify which ones offer the greatest time savings for a CDMO with limited CSV resources.  說明 9 項效率改善策略，並識別對資源有限的 CDMO 最具時間效益者。
  6. Evaluate whether screenshot/witness evidence is required for a given test, using the GAMP 5 secondary evidence framework.  運用 GAMP 5 次要測試證據框架，判斷特定測試是否需要截圖或見證。

Chapter 7 — Supplier Activities  |  第 7 章：供應商活動

7.1 Supplier Products, Applications, and Services

Although the responsibility for compliance with GxP regulations lies with the regulated company, the supplier may have considerable involvement in the process. Regulated companies may be able to leverage supplier knowledge and documentation, subject to suitability following formal assessment. This may involve an audit, depending on risk, complexity, and novelty.

Suppliers provide a range of products, applications, and services for hardware, software, and related technologies including cloud-computing services. The relationship between supplier and regulated company will vary significantly depending upon the product, application, or scope of service being provided. Consultants, for instance those acting as implementation partners, should have sufficient education, training, and experience to advise on the subject for which they are retained.

7.1.1 Standard Product (GAMP Category 3)

If the product is purchased off-the-shelf and does not require configuration to support business processes, or only offers defined ranges of factory-provided values or ranges (parameterization), supplier involvement with the regulated company is typically limited to the provision of documentation, training, support, and maintenance. The product should be developed and maintained by the supplier in accordance with good practices.

7.1.2 Configured Product (GAMP Category 4)

If the product requires configuration to support specific business processes, supplier involvement will typically include support with specification, configuration, verification, and operation of the system. Procedures to follow should be agreed between the regulated company and the supplier and be documented in the appropriate plan. Procedures adopted may be those of the regulated company or from the supplier QMS.

7.1.3 Custom Application (GAMP Category 5)

For a custom application, the regulated company typically contracts a supplier to develop the application based on defined requirements. Therefore, the supplier will be involved during the full project life cycle of the system, and also to provide support during system operation. Procedures to follow should be agreed between the regulated company and the supplier and be documented in the appropriate plan.

7.1.4 Service Provision

Suppliers that provide IT/IS services (including cloud-computing services) should operate within a QMS. Quality planning should define the activities, procedures, deliverables, and responsibilities for establishing delivery and monitoring of the service. Such a plan is a contractual document, and as such, should be approved for use by both the supplier and the regulated company.

The required information may be satisfactorily covered by other contractual documents such as a service level agreement (SLA), in which case a separate plan would not be required.

中文解說：供應商分類與責任分工

GAMP 三類供應商產品對比

類別 定義 供應商介入程度 CDMO 驗證重點
Cat 3
標準產品		 現成品，無需配置（或僅有廠家預設範圍） 最低：提供文件、訓練、支援即可 安裝確認 (IQ) + 操作確認 (OQ) 為主
Cat 4
可配置產品		 需根據業務流程進行配置 中等：協助規格制定、配置、驗證 配置規格確認 + URS 追溯性
Cat 5
客製化應用		 依受規管公司需求客製開發 全程：從設計到退役全生命週期 完整 V-model 驗證，含程式碼審查

實務類比：CDMO 常見系統如何分類

Cat 3 範例：天平 (Sartorius / Mettler-Toledo)，pH meter — 無需配置，只需校正記錄。

Cat 4 範例：SCADA 系統 (Wonderware、iFix)，LIMS (LabWare、SampleManager) — 需大量配置，但核心軟體由廠商維護。

Cat 5 範例：自研 BPR 系統、客製報表系統 — 廠商依你的需求開發，你要完整驗證，包括 FS/DS 審查。

誰負責合規？

GxP 法規責任永遠在受規管公司（即 CDMO），供應商只是協助者。即使供應商做了所有測試，CDMO 仍需評估並正式接受那些測試結果。這一點不因 Cat 3/4/5 而改變。

雲端服務 (SaaS/IaaS) 的特殊考量

雲端服務供應商必須在其 QMS 內運作，且質量計劃須由雙方共同核准。若 SLA 已涵蓋必要資訊，則可免除另立品質計劃。建議參考 ISPE GAMP GPG: Enabling Innovation Chapter 4 (IT Service Management)。

7.2 Supplier Good Practices

Table 7.1 lists good practice activities that apply to product and application development, support, and service provision.

Step Practice Description
1 Establish QMS Provide documented procedures and standards; ensure competent trained staff; provide evidence of conformance; enable continual improvement.
2 Establish Requirements Ensure clear requirements are defined or provided by the regulated company.
3 Quality Planning Define how the QMS will be implemented for a particular product, application, or service.
4 Assessments of Sub-Suppliers Formally assess sub-suppliers as part of selection and quality planning.
5 Produce Specifications Specify the system to meet the defined requirements.
6 Perform Design Review Formally review design against requirements, standards, and identified risks.
7 Software Production / Configuration Develop software per defined standards including code review. Document configuration per guidelines.
8 Perform Testing Test the system per approved test plans and test specifications.
9 Commercial Release Formal release process with criteria, responsibilities, records, and release notes.
10 User Documentation and Training Provide system management documentation, operational documentation, and training per agreed contracts.
11 System Support During Operation Support and maintain per agreed contracts; document change management process.
12 System Replacement and Retirement Manage replacement or withdrawal per documented process; support regulated company retirement activities.

中文解說：12 步驟供應商良好實踐

為何 CDMO 需要了解這 12 個步驟？

在供應商評估 (Supplier Assessment) 時，你需要驗證供應商是否執行這 12 個步驟。如果供應商的 QMS 已完整覆蓋這些活動，你可以借用他們的測試與文件，從而減少自身的驗證工作量。

實務對照：供應商審計核查清單

當你對 LIMS 或 MES 廠商進行書面審計 (Paper Audit) 或現場審計 (On-site Audit) 時，以下是高價值核查項目：

  • Step 1 (QMS)：供應商是否有 ISO 9001 認證？或等效的內部 QMS？
  • Step 6 (設計審查)：設計審查記錄是否可提供給你？能否支持你的 DQ？
  • Step 8 (測試)：FAT/SAT 測試腳本和結果記錄是否完整？格式是否適合納入你的驗證包？
  • Step 9 (商業發布)：供應商是否有明確的版本發布標準？Release Notes 是否說明已知缺陷？
  • Step 11 (維護)：補丁管理流程是否文件化？安全更新時間表是否透明？

重要區分：商業發布 vs GxP 發布

Step 9「商業發布」是供應商對客戶的正式發布行為，不是將系統放入 GxP 環境的行為。進入 GxP 生產環境的「放行」(Release to Production) 永遠是受規管公司的責任，須經過 IQ/OQ/PQ 及品質部門核准。

7.3 Quality Management System

It is recommended that suppliers follow a QMS, preferably based on recognized standards. The QMS should define:

  • The process being followed to deliver and support the product, application, or service
  • The process to understand customer business process needs and capture requirements (including business, quality, and regulatory requirements)
  • Responsibilities, including clear separation of authority between QA and other groups such as product development, product support, finance, or marketing
  • Deliverables
  • Management of documentation, records, and information
  • Planned reviews of the QMS and internal audits
  • Management of incidents/problems/non-conformities
  • Approach to continual improvement, including the adoption of current software development models, methods and good practices, and associated selection of supporting tools and automation

The QMS should be based on a life cycle concept. There are many equally valid life cycle approaches that may be used by suppliers, including Agile. This Guide does not recommend any particular approach, but rather highlights those activities expected of suppliers to support the regulated company in achieving and maintaining compliance.

The QMS should include procedures covering:

  • Software management, control, and release
  • Development change control
  • Configuration management
  • Traceability
  • Training of supplier staff
  • Document, records, and information management
  • Backup and restore

The QMS should cover the approach to continual improvement. CMMI provides an approach based on a framework for assessing and improving organizational capability and maturity. The use of ITIL for IT service delivery is encouraged. Industry guidance such as ISPE GAMP should be treated as supporting information and should not override the supplier's established QMS.

中文解說：供應商 QMS 要求

Agile 與傳統瀑布式開發都可接受

GAMP 5 第二版明確表示不偏好特定生命週期模型。無論是 Waterfall、Agile (Scrum/Kanban) 或混合方法，只要供應商能提供符合法規要求的可追溯文件，都是可接受的。

對 CDMO 的實務意義：當供應商說「我們用 Agile 所以沒有傳統 FS/DS」時，你應要求等效的 Agile 文件（User Stories、Sprint Review Records、Acceptance Criteria），而非直接拒絕。

QMS 中的 QA 獨立性

供應商 QMS 要求 QA 與開發、行銷、財務等部門有明確的職責分離。這與製藥 GMP 的 QA 獨立性概念相同。在評估供應商時，可詢問：「誰有權批准產品發布？QA 是否能夠獨立阻止不合規的發布？」

CMMI 與 ITIL 是加分項

供應商若持有 CMMI Level 3+ 認證，表示其軟體開發成熟度較高，可作為減少現場審計的依據。持有 ITIL 認證的 IT 服務供應商在事件管理、變更管理、問題管理方面有規範化流程，對 SaaS 平台特別重要。

7.4 Requirements

Requirements are captured and defined internally by the supplier (in the case of product development), and/or may be provided by the customer (for a configured product, custom application, or a service). The requirements should define clearly and precisely what the system should do and state any constraints.

Requirements should be developed, reviewed, and approved in accordance with the development method implemented by the supplier whether it be linear or iterative. Changes to requirements should be controlled.

Regulated companies wish to maximize the use of supplier testing to support their compliance activities. Therefore, requirements should be written such that they can be tested. Individual requirements should be traceable through the life cycle.

For configured products and custom applications, the regulated company should describe the business processes to be automated. In the case of configured products, these processes should be aligned with the functionality of the product to be used. This may require significant process reengineering.

The use of appropriate and effective software tools should be considered by suppliers to manage information/records that may otherwise have been managed via paper documentation.

中文解說：需求規格的可測試性

核心原則：需求必須可被測試

GAMP 5 強調供應商的需求必須「可測試」(testable)。這不只是對供應商的要求，也是受規管公司在審查 URS/RS 時的核心標準。不可測試的需求（如「系統應易於使用」）在驗證中毫無意義。

實務範例：可測試需求的寫法

不良範例（不可測試） 良好範例（可測試）
系統應快速回應 系統在正常負載下應在 3 秒內完成查詢回應
系統應保持資料完整性 所有資料變更應記錄於稽核軌跡，包含時間戳記、使用者、變更前後值
批次記錄不可被修改 批次記錄在放行後，任何欄位的修改嘗試應觸發警示並被阻擋，系統返回錯誤訊息 ERR-001

配置型產品可能需要流程再造

若採購 Cat 4 系統（如 SAP、Oracle），業務流程需要「配合系統標準功能」，而非強迫系統配合所有現有流程。GAMP 5 明確指出這「可能需要顯著的流程再造 (process reengineering)」。CDMO 在引入大型 LIMS 或 ERP 時，應提前評估這個代價。

7.5 Supplier Quality Planning

The supplier should define how the QMS will be implemented for a particular product, application, or service. This should include defining the life cycle model, project organization, activities, procedures, deliverables, and responsibilities for establishing fitness for intended use. The approach may include prototyping or other software development techniques. The role of supplier QA should be clearly defined.

These supplier quality requirements may be captured in a separate Quality Plan or other supplier documentation. Quality requirements should be clearly documented, reviewed, approved, accessible, and followed.

7.5.1 Prototyping

Prototyping methods may be used to clarify user requirements or to evaluate areas of risk. Typically, a prototype is used to evaluate the acceptability of a user interface, the performance of critical algorithms, suitability of the overall solution, or aspects of system performance such as capacity and speed.

The aims and objectives of the prototype should be clearly defined, and the prototype evaluated against these to ensure the objectives are met. Prototyping is often used as part of Agile software development where control is achieved through Agile ceremonies (e.g., daily Scrum), control of the sprint backlog, use of tools, and sprint reviews and retrospectives.

中文解說：供應商品質計劃

品質計劃 (Quality Plan) 的核心內容

對受規管公司而言，供應商品質計劃是非常重要的評估文件。它應涵蓋：

  • 採用的生命週期模型（Waterfall、Agile、混合）
  • QA 角色與職責分工
  • 關鍵交付物清單（Deliverables List）
  • 測試策略概述
  • 變更控制程序

若供應商無法提供品質計劃，這是一個警示信號（Red Flag），應在供應商評估報告中記錄。

原型法 (Prototyping) 對 CDMO 的意義

當你委託開發客製化系統（如 BPR 自動化、設備介面系統）時，建議要求供應商先提供原型。這讓你在大量開發投入前，能驗證關鍵功能是否符合需求，並識別潛在風險，降低後期變更的成本。Agile 的 Sprint Demo 即是原型法的一種形式。

7.6 Sub-Supplier Assessments

Suppliers should formally assess their sub-suppliers as part of quality planning. They also should be periodically reassessed in accordance with the QMS.

The decision whether to perform an audit of their sub-suppliers should be documented and based on a risk assessment.

In some cases, such as those sub-suppliers related to the location and hosting of GxP regulated data, sub-supplier management may have a direct impact on regulated company compliance, and should be made transparent.

See Appendix M2 for further details on supplier assessments.

中文解說：次供應商評估

雲端時代的次供應商風險

這是現代 CSV 最重要的課題之一。當你使用 SaaS LIMS（如 Veeva Vault、Benchling），而 LIMS 廠商的伺服器在 AWS 或 Azure 上，那麼 AWS/Azure 就是你的次供應商。

GAMP 5 明確指出：若次供應商涉及 GxP 數據的存儲與託管，次供應商管理對受規管公司的合規性有直接影響，必須透明化。

實務場景：如何處理雲端次供應商

  • 要求主供應商提供：其次供應商評估報告的摘要（或 ISO 27001、SOC 2 Type II 認證）
  • 在技術協議 (Technical Agreement) 中載明：數據存儲地點、備份策略、DR 計劃
  • 定期再評估：若次供應商（如雲端平台）發生重大安全事件，主供應商應通知你
  • 供應商切換條款：若主供應商更換雲端平台，應事先通知並允許你進行影響評估

第三方函式庫也是次供應商

當軟體供應商在其產品中使用開源或商業第三方函式庫（如 log4j、OpenSSL），這些函式庫的供應商也屬於次供應商範疇。近年來 log4shell 漏洞事件就是典型例子。優良供應商應維護軟體物料清單 (SBOM, Software Bill of Materials) 並進行依賴項安全掃描。

7.7 Specifications

For product development, the supplier should document the functionality and design of the system to meet the defined requirements. This should cover software, hardware, and configuration.

References to documentation and specifications should not be interpreted as requiring traditional documents, and the maintenance of records in appropriate and effective software tools is encouraged.

Functional specifications should clearly and completely describe what the product will do, produced such that objective testing can be subsequently performed. Design specifications should be based on the functional specifications and should be sufficiently detailed so that the product can be developed.

Specifications should be reviewed and approved with traceability established between related documents. They should be managed under change control.

If the supplier is involved in configuring a product, service, or developing a custom application, the number and level of specifications can vary considerably and should be agreed with the regulated company.

7.8 Design Reviews

Design reviews evaluate deliverables against standards and requirements, identify issues, and propose required corrective actions. They should be planned and systematic reviews of specifications, design, and development, and should be planned to occur at suitable stages during the life cycle, based on risk, complexity, and novelty. Design reviews aim to identify and eliminate issues that would otherwise lead to changes at a later stage.

7.9 Software Production / Configuration

The supplier should establish and maintain a formal system for controlling software production. Appropriate methods and tools should be used and defined. Rules and conventions, such as acceptable languages, coding standards, version control, and naming conventions should be established. The use of code reviews should be considered.

Existing software should be used in accordance with documented build processes and taking into account any changes in the system hardware, interfaces, and peripherals.

If the supplier is involved in configuring a product, it should be performed in accordance with the controlling configuration specification and follow appropriate guidelines and recommendations.

中文解說：規格、設計審查與軟體開發

規格文件的靈活性

GAMP 5 明確指出，規格文件不一定要是傳統的 Word 文件格式。供應商可以使用：

  • Jira 中的 Epic/Story（Agile 方法）
  • 需求管理工具（如 DOORS、Polarion）
  • 設計圖 + 技術規格表

重點是：這些記錄必須可追溯、受變更控制管理，且能支持後續測試。

設計審查 (Design Review) 的 CDMO 實踐

對於 Cat 5 客製化系統，建議你作為受規管公司參與供應商的設計審查，而非僅接收最終報告。這相當於在施工途中進行品質檢查，比交房後發現問題便宜得多。

參與設計審查的記錄可作為你的 DQ（設計確認）證據，減少後續需要進行的正式 DQ 工作量。

程式碼審查 (Code Review) 的重要性

GAMP 5 建議（非強制）供應商實施程式碼審查。對 Cat 5 系統，你應在供應商評估時詢問程式碼審查流程：是人工審查、自動靜態分析工具 (SonarQube)，還是兩者兼用？這直接影響你對系統可靠性的信心，也影響你後期需要做多深入的測試。

7.10 Testing

For product development, the supplier should test the product in accordance with approved test plans and test specifications. The test specifications, when executed, should demonstrate that all requirements, functionality, and design have been met.

This may involve one or many stages of testing depending on the nature of the product:

  • Module (unit) testing
  • Integration testing
  • System testing

Test records for each stage should be reviewed and approved, and retained for a period defined in the QMS (not to be shorter than the supported lifetime of the current software version). Test failures should be managed in accordance with a formal documented process.

If the supplier is involved in configuring a product or developing a custom application, the number and level of test specifications can vary considerably and should be agreed with the regulated company.

7.11 Commercial Release

System release to customers should be performed in accordance with a formal process that describes the criteria for release, responsibilities, records to be retained, and items to be released, including software, hardware, and documentation. Clear policies and criteria should be established for the acceptability or otherwise of product release, based on the number and severity of known defects. Release notes defining fixes, changes, known problems, and new features should accompany each release, including minor releases and patches.

Note: Commercial release by a supplier is not a release into the GxP environment, which is a regulated company activity.

7.12 User Documentation and Training

The supplier should provide adequate system management documentation, operational documentation, and training for both maintenance and operation in accordance with agreed contracts.

7.13 System Support and Maintenance During Operation

The supplier should support and maintain the system in accordance with agreed contracts. Formal procedures should be followed, typically covering:

  • Operational change control
  • Configuration management
  • Patch management
  • Incident management
  • Documentation management
  • Backup and restore
  • Business continuity
  • Disaster Recovery (DR)
  • Managing software product releases
  • Training of supplier staff
  • System maintenance
  • Security management

7.14 System Replacement and Retirement

The supplier should manage the replacement or withdrawal of products or service in accordance with a documented process and plans. Sufficient notice of the retirement of a system or version should be given to regulated companies to allow them to plan for their required activities. The supplier also may support the regulated company with the retirement of computerized systems.

中文解說：測試、發布與生命週期

供應商測試分層架構

理解供應商的測試層次，能幫助你判斷哪些測試可以接受借用，哪些你必須自己做：

測試層次 供應商負責 受規管公司補充
單元測試 供應商主導（通常可借用） 驗證測試報告的完整性
整合測試 供應商主導（可評估後借用） 確認覆蓋你的介面需求
系統測試 (FAT) 供應商執行，你可選擇見證 可作為你的部分 OQ 證據
使用者驗收 (SAT) 協同執行 你主導，驗證業務流程符合 URS
生產環境驗收 (PQ) 不適用 完全由你負責

Release Notes 是重要的供應商文件

GAMP 5 要求每次發布（包含小版本更新和補丁）都必須附帶 Release Notes，列出修復項目、變更、已知問題和新功能。

對 CDMO 的實務意義：在處理供應商版本更新時，Release Notes 是你評估影響範圍、決定是否需要重新驗證的第一手資料，也是變更控制記錄的支持文件。

退役通知 — 不能被遺忘的條款

GAMP 5 要求供應商在系統退役前給予「充足通知 (sufficient notice)」。在技術協議中，建議明確約定：最短通知期（建議至少 12 個月），以及供應商是否協助資料遷移。遺漏此條款的後果：供應商突然宣布停止支援某版本，你的驗證系統瞬間成為 unsupported software，面臨重大稽查風險。

維護期 13 項覆蓋範圍

Section 7.13 列出的 12 個維護領域（變更控制、配置管理、補丁、事件管理等）是評估供應商服務能力的完整框架。在起草技術協議 (Technical Agreement) 時，這 12 項應逐一確認責任歸屬，並在 SLA 中具體化（如：事件響應時間、備份頻率、DR 演練週期）。

Chapter 8 — Efficiency Improvements  |  第 8 章：效率改善

Chapter 8 Introduction

This Guide provides a flexible framework for achieving compliant computerized systems that are fit for their intended use. The benefits will be obtained only if the framework is applied effectively in the context of a particular organization.

In this Second Edition of the Guide many examples of efficiency improvements are also discussed in the context of critical thinking.

Aspects that can assist efficiency include:

  • Establishing verifiable and appropriate user requirements
  • Making risk-based decisions
  • Leveraging supplier input
  • Leveraging existing records and information
  • Using efficient testing practices
  • Employing a well-managed handover process
  • Managing changes efficiently
  • Anticipating data archiving and migration needs
  • Using tools and automation

中文解說：9 項效率改善概覽

CSV 專案經理的效率改善檢查清單

  • URS 是否每條需求都可被客觀測試？（8.1）
  • 是否對系統風險進行分級，高風險投入更多驗證？（8.2）
  • 是否評估供應商的 FAT/單元測試報告可否直接借用？（8.3）
  • 公司內部是否有類似系統的現有測試腳本可重用？（8.4）
  • 測試是否基於風險決定深度，而非「全部都測一遍」？（8.5）
  • 測試是否需要截圖和見證？還是電子記錄已足夠？（8.5）
  • 移交計劃是否包含 Hypercare 期與 Rollback 程序？（8.6）
  • 變更是否能快速通過，避免不必要的審批層次？（8.7）
  • 資料保留期、格式標準化是否在實施前就規劃好？（8.8）
  • 是否善用自動化測試工具、ALM、電子協議管理？（8.9）

CDMO 資源有限的現實

許多中小型 CDMO 的 CSV 團隊人手有限，無法對每個系統做同等深度的驗證。GAMP 5 Chapter 8 提供的 9 個策略，正是幫助有限資源做出最高效合規投入的工具。核心邏輯：把精力投在真正影響病人安全、產品品質和數據完整性的地方。

8.1 Establishing Verifiable and Objective User Requirements

Requirements should be analyzed to ensure that they are fully defined and are verifiable and objective. For example:

Incomplete Requirement: Room shall be controlled at 20°C.

Complete Requirement: Room shall be controlled at 20°C ± 2°C. Excursions of no greater than 7°C are permitted for <10 minutes.

The level of detail is dependent on the novelty and complexity of the processes and system being implemented. Table 8.1 lists aspects to consider when developing verifiable and objective requirements.

Aspect Purpose
Process Knowledge To identify key requirements related to the business or manufacturing process
Business Knowledge To ensure requirements are challenged against business need and benefits can be realized
Ownership To ensure clarity and understanding of the stated requirements
Analytical To ensure requirements are challenged to confirm they are complete and accurate
Technical/Product To ensure requirements are practical in terms of available technology
Process/Product Impact To ensure requirements impacting the process or product are clearly identified (including CQA or CPP)
Technical Authorship To ensure requirements are written in concise, correct, and unambiguous language

中文解說：可驗證的 URS

為什麼模糊的 URS 會浪費時間？

模糊的需求在 CSV 專案後期造成的損失遠超過前期釐清的時間成本：

  • 測試人員無法判斷測試是否通過（PASS/FAIL 標準不清楚）
  • 需要額外的審批循環來解釋需求含義
  • 稽查時監管機構可能質疑驗證的有效性
  • 變更控制時難以判斷是否為「同類替換 (like-for-like)」

Table 8.1 的七個面向：URS 審查會的角色分工

建議在 URS 審查會議中確保以下知識都有人代表：

  • 製程知識：製程工程師或批次生產人員
  • 業務知識：業務流程負責人（Process Owner）
  • 分析能力：品質工程師或系統驗證人員
  • 技術/產品：IT 或設備工程師
  • 製程/產品影響：品質保證人員（QA）
  • 技術寫作：文件管理人員或有寫作經驗的驗證工程師

CQA / CPP 需求要特別標注

與關鍵品質屬性 (CQA) 或關鍵製程參數 (CPP) 直接相關的需求，應在 URS 中明確標注（如加上「GxP Critical」標籤）。這些需求在後續風險評估和測試深度決策時有更高優先級，也是稽查重點。

8.2 Making Risk-Based Decisions

Risk management provides an opportunity to scale life cycle activities. Benefit may also be achieved if organizations use risk assessments as input to decisions to omit or include an activity. Examples of areas where risk assessments may help with scaling include:

  • Number and depth of design reviews required
  • Need for, and extent of, source-code review
  • Rigor of supplier assessment
  • Depth and rigor of testing

Similar opportunities exist during system operation:

  • Extent and level of specification and verification of changes
  • Rigor of the backup and restore process
  • Level of business continuity required
  • Frequency and level of DR
  • Degree to which identity checks are completed prior to providing access rights
  • Scope and frequency of periodic reviews

The benefits of risk-based decision-making can be maximized only if the conclusions and decisions can be leveraged. Therefore, there should be a practical, searchable means of access to conclusions and decisions available to those involved in decision-making — e.g., a risk register.

The risk-based approach should be focused and resourced for maximum effectiveness and efficiency. Organizations should not invest more effort and time into the risk-management process than is commensurate with the potential impact on patient safety, product quality, and data integrity.

中文解說：風險決策的務實應用

風險分層決定驗證深度

GAMP 5 的核心邏輯：不是所有系統和功能都需要相同深度的驗證。風險評估應能回答：

  • 此系統若失效，對病人安全、產品品質、數據完整性的影響為何？
  • 失效的可能性是否因供應商的良好實踐而降低？
  • 現有的其他控制措施（SOP、環境監控、人工覆核）是否降低了殘餘風險？

風險決策必須可查詢、可重用

GAMP 5 特別指出：風險評估的結論必須以可搜尋的方式存取。使用一個「風險登記冊 (Risk Register)」是最佳做法。每次做類似系統的驗證或變更評估，都能引用之前的風險結論，不必重頭開始。這是效率提升的關鍵工具。

警告：過度的風險評估也是浪費

GAMP 5 有一句關鍵警句：「組織不應在風險管理過程中投入超過其潛在影響所值的時間和精力。」換言之，為一台簡單的桌上型 pH meter 寫一份 20 頁的風險評估報告，本身就是一種資源浪費。根據比例原則，應用時間在高風險系統上。

8.3 Leveraging Supplier Input

Supplier activities, including testing, may be used by the regulated company as part of verification, provided the regulated company has assessed the supplier processes as suitable. This assessment may include a supplier audit, depending on the risk, complexity, and novelty of the system.

The regulated company should assess the supplier for evidence of:

  • An acceptable supplier quality system
  • Supplier technical capability
  • Supplier application of good practice such that activities performed by and information obtained from the supplier will be complete, accurate, and suitable to meet the purpose of verification

Supplier documentation, information, and records should be assessed for content and quality. Regulated company procedures and processes should be flexible regarding acceptable format and structures so that supplier documentation may be leveraged.

If inadequacies are found in the supplier quality system, technical capability, or documentation, then the regulated company may choose to manage potential risks by applying specific, targeted additional verification checks or other controls, rather than repeating supplier activities and replicating supplier documentation.

The decision and justification to use supplier activities to support verification should be based on the intended use of the system and should be documented and approved by SMEs, which may include the quality unit.

Suppliers also may have tools or techniques unique to the specification and testing of their product which may be leveraged by the regulated company during specification and testing.

中文解說：借用供應商文件的策略

CDMO 可節省最多時間的策略

對資源有限的 CDMO 而言，Section 8.3 是整個 Chapter 8 中最具實用價值的部分。正確應用可節省 30-60% 的驗證測試工作量。

借用供應商文件的三個前提

借用必須有書面依據，三個前提缺一不可：

  1. 供應商 QMS 評估通過：你必須對供應商的品質系統進行評估（書面審計或現場審計）並有書面結論
  2. 技術能力確認：供應商具備足夠的技術能力執行測試，測試方法是可靠的
  3. 文件格式可接受：你的 SOP 允許使用非標準格式的供應商文件（需要預先審視公司的驗證 SOP）

什麼可以借用？什麼必須自己做？

供應商文件類型 借用可行性 備註
FAT 測試報告 高（可作為 IQ/OQ 部分依據） 需審查測試覆蓋範圍是否符合你的 URS
單元/整合測試報告 中（Cat 5 可借用，Cat 3 通常不公開） 確認測試版本與你安裝版本一致
DQ 設計確認文件 高（設計審查記錄可支持 DQ） 需確認設計符合你的使用環境
IQ 安裝確認 中（部分可借用標準安裝步驟） 你的現場安裝條件須自行驗證
OQ 操作確認 低~中（功能測試可借用，業務流程需自測） 與你的 URS 直接相關的部分必須自測
PQ 效能確認 無（必須在你的生產環境自行執行） PQ 是你的專屬活動

實務建議：如何讓供應商文件更容易借用

在採購合約或技術協議的談判階段，主動要求：

  • 供應商提供符合 GAMP 5 格式的測試報告（非其內部格式）
  • FAT 測試腳本可依你的 URS 客製化
  • 測試記錄保留期不短於你的法規要求
  • 允許你查閱（不必全部持有）供應商的詳細測試記錄

8.4 Leveraging Existing Information

In addition to the use of supplier activities and information, regulated companies should also leverage their own activities and information related to existing systems when introducing new, similar systems. Examples include:

  • Laboratory equipment
  • Secondary manufacturing equipment
  • Packaging equipment

Relevant information to reuse may include risk assessments, RS, various plans, test specifications, test results, and design reviews.

The new system should be assessed and any differences with the existing system identified and managed by the introduction of appropriate specification and verification as required. A review of existing information should determine which may be used as is or updated as required. These conclusions should be documented.

The new system should be subject to installation and verification based on user requirements. The validation report should explain the rationale for reuse of documentation.

中文解說：重用既有文件

「類似系統」的文件重用策略

當公司已有某廠牌系統的驗證包，採購同廠牌相同型號（或相近型號）的新設備時，可大幅重用既有文件。重用範圍：

  • 風險評估 (RA)：更新差異分析，補充新設備特有風險
  • 需求規格 (RS/URS)：複製並修訂為適合新設備的版本
  • 測試腳本：直接複製，執行前確認版本差異
  • 驗證計劃/報告模板：複製並更新系統描述與資訊

重用必須有差異分析文件

GAMP 5 要求：若重用既有文件，必須正式評估新舊系統的差異，並在驗證報告中說明重用的理由。「因為一樣所以直接用」是不夠的——你需要書面記錄「評估後確認差異為 X，對原測試腳本的影響為 Y，因此決定重用/更新 Z 項目」。

CDMO 的典型場景

填充線從四頭擴充到六頭，新增兩台相同型號的灌裝泵。既有四台泵的 IQ/OQ/PQ 文件可作為起點：

  • IQ：直接複製安裝確認腳本，執行新機台的現場安裝確認
  • OQ：借用功能測試腳本，確認新機台的參數範圍一致
  • PQ：需在新配置下重新執行，因為整條線的流量分配已改變

8.5 Using Efficient Testing Practices

Testing is a major, time-consuming exercise. It perhaps offers the greatest opportunity for efficiency savings.

8.5.1 Reuse of Test Results

Many systems have large amounts of test results available due to suppliers following a QMS independently of a regulated company. On a project, there may be pre-delivery testing, which may include factory acceptance testing (FAT). Wherever possible, regulated companies should clearly communicate to suppliers the testing and document requirements in advance such that supplier test documentation is of the required standard to support compliance activities.

Testing also may take place to meet other business or legal requirements, such as HSE, and finance such as SOX. Unnecessary duplication of testing should be avoided.

8.5.2 Extent of Required Testing

The level and type of testing should be risk-based and based on the nature of the component involved (standard, configurable, or custom). Types of testing include:

  • Normal case (positive)
  • Invalid case (negative)
  • Repeatability
  • Performance
  • Volume/load
  • Regression
  • Structural testing

While user requirements should be verified by the regulated company through installation and acceptance tests demonstrating fitness for intended use, other required tests should be identified based on risk, complexity, and novelty. The regulated company's procedures should allow for the use of such existing test evidence subject to a documented and justified review and approval by an SME.

8.5.3 Secondary Test Evidence

The generation and retention of secondary supporting hard copy or image evidence such as screenshots, in addition to the primary test result or output, is unnecessary in most cases and does not add value. It often adds significant cost without associated benefit. Such additional evidence should be generated and maintained only where value-added and necessary for effective testing.

Examples where additional test evidence may be useful:

  • Complex results, which may be difficult or time consuming to record manually
  • When the result is essentially visual or pictorial
  • Where there is a need for before and after comparisons

Test evidence may be retained electronically provided adequate security and retention mechanisms are established. Systems may also have data audit trails or other system logs that capture much of the information traditionally captured by screen prints.

8.5.4 Use of Test Witnesses

The use of witnesses during testing is not a requirement and involves a significant overhead without added benefit. A regulated company may choose to witness some tests (e.g., site or factory acceptance testing) for commercial, contractual, communication, education, or training reasons. It is disproportionate and unnecessary to require test witnessing or requiring the tester to initial every test step to affirm they followed the instructions.

Decisions to use witnesses should consider knowledge and experience of testers, practical issues (e.g., two-person processes), level and degree of review by an SME, and degree of automation of tests and resulting test evidence.

中文解說：高效測試實踐

測試是最大的效率節省機會

GAMP 5 原文指出「測試可能提供最大的效率節省機會」。以下是 CDMO 可立即應用的策略：

8.5.1：FAT 前就應告知供應商你的要求

常見錯誤：等供應商做完 FAT 才去審查文件，發現格式不符，浪費雙方時間。

正確做法：在採購前或 Kick-off Meeting 時，提供供應商你的「可接受測試文件標準」清單，包含：測試腳本格式、Pass/Fail 標準記錄方式、測試員和審查員簽名要求、電子記錄保存格式。

8.5.2：測試取樣策略

不必測試所有可能的組合，基於風險決定測試覆蓋範圍：

  • 高風險功能：正常案例 + 邊界值 + 異常案例 + 重複性 = 完整測試
  • 中風險功能：正常案例 + 一個異常案例即可
  • 低風險功能：正常案例 + 引用供應商測試結果

例如：LIMS 中的「計算分析結果」是高風險功能（影響放行決策），必須完整測試。「修改個人密碼」是低風險功能，測試一次即可。

8.5.3：截圖不是必須的！

這是許多公司長期浪費大量時間的地方。GAMP 5 明確指出：截圖在大多數情況下不必要且不增加價值。

截圖有用的情況（只有這三種）：

  1. 結果複雜，難以手動記錄
  2. 結果本質上是視覺的（如圖表、介面外觀）
  3. 需要前後對比

大部分的數值型測試結果（數字是否在範圍內、計算是否正確），直接記錄實際值就夠了。系統的稽查軌跡本身就是記錄，不需要再截圖一遍。

8.5.4：見證測試不是必要的！

要求測試員在每個步驟旁首字母確認是「不必要且不合比例的」——GAMP 5 的原文措辭非常直接。見證測試的唯一合理理由是：

  • 商業或合約原因（客戶要求）
  • 溝通、教育或培訓目的
  • 系統性質需要兩人操作（如操作員在現場、工程師在控制室）

對 CDMO 的實務影響：可以廢除「每個測試步驟都要品質人員在場見證」的做法，改為 SME 審查測試記錄。這能釋放大量 QA 人員時間。

8.6 Employing a Well-Managed Handover Process

System handover (from the project team to the process owner, system owner, and operational users) should be well-managed. It is a prerequisite for the effective maintenance of system compliance during operation. Handover should be planned in accordance with agreed criteria and should consider:

  • Support requirements for maintenance, as defined by IT or engineering
  • Outstanding problems or deficiencies
  • How long business processes can be stopped to enable handover
  • Ability and steps required to roll back to a previous operational state
  • Situations where updates are not optional (e.g., updates pushed to SaaS applications)
  • Information required at handover (specification and verification documentation, user and maintenance manuals or guides), or new or updated user procedures
  • Training needs (user, support, and maintenance)
  • Clear communication between groups, e.g., with application support and client service groups
  • The impact on the change-control process to apply during the handover period, when handover is to be phased
  • Responsibilities during handover, e.g., for accepting the system and for assessing the severity of outstanding problems or deficiencies
  • Potential need of a period of elevated support and maintenance, often referred to as hypercare
  • Preservation of implied as well as explicit knowledge, e.g., through SME lists and recording of lessons learned

中文解說：良好的系統移交

移交是合規維持的先決條件

許多 CDMO 在驗證完成後急於上線，缺乏正式的移交計劃，導致：

  • 操作人員未接受足夠培訓
  • IT 不知道如何支持系統（備份程序、存取管理）
  • 未解決的問題在生產中暴露
  • 隱性知識只在專案團隊中，移交後流失

Hypercare 期：上線後的加強支援

GAMP 5 特別提到「Hypercare」——這是指系統正式上線後的一段時間（通常 2-4 週），在此期間供應商和/或專案團隊提供加強支援。對 CDMO 的建議：在技術協議和專案計劃中明確定義 Hypercare 的時間長度、支援管道和響應時間。

SaaS 系統的強制更新問題

GAMP 5 明確列出「SaaS 應用的強制推送更新」是移交計劃需要考量的因素。對 CDMO 而言：若使用雲端 LIMS 或 ELN，供應商可能在未徵詢你的情況下推送功能更新。你的移交計劃和持續變更控制程序必須包含「如何處理非自願更新」的機制，否則系統可能在未經驗證的狀態下持續運作。

移交檢查清單（CDMO 版）

  • ☐ 移交前所有 Outstanding Issues 已分級（Critical/Major/Minor）
  • ☐ Rollback 程序已測試並文件化
  • ☐ 所有使用者培訓已完成並有記錄
  • ☐ IT 已接收系統架構文件、備份程序、存取管理 SOP
  • ☐ QA 已核准上線（包含接受 Open OOS/Deviation 的決定）
  • ☐ Hypercare 期間的支援管道和聯絡人已確認
  • ☐ 專案經驗教訓已記錄（Lessons Learned）

8.7 Managing Changes Efficiently

Efficient change management should be executed in conjunction with configuration management. Key elements include:

  • Documented description and business benefit of the change
  • Confirmation of availability of resource
  • Assessment of the impact of the change on the application, the underlying infrastructure, the people (users and engineering support staff), and the documentation
  • Leveraging the risk assessment information from the original project and assessing any new risks introduced by the change to define the strategy for maintaining compliance — including the need for any regression testing
  • Evaluation of the change from the financial, technical (IT or engineering), and compliance perspectives at the lowest technically competent level prior to management approval
  • Establishing and maintaining the distinction between changes at the pharmaceutical quality system level (impacting the medicinal product life cycle) versus changes at the IT delivery and service management level
  • Minimizing the number of approval points in the process
  • Documentation and communication of the decision
  • Execution and verification of the change, using traceability to identify existing applicable tests
  • Closing the change record in a timely manner

Weaknesses in change management systems that may lead to inefficiencies include:

  • Lack of scalability for minor changes or standard infrastructure components
  • Failure to execute change management steps in the appropriate sequence
  • Failure in scheduling or identifying dependencies
  • Abuse or misapplication of emergency change processes
  • An inability to prevent unnecessary changes
  • Failure to keep specifications current
  • Failure to leverage existing documentation for risk assessment, traceability matrices, or protocols
  • Lack of follow-up processes to close a change record
  • Independent change processes leading to duplication of effort
  • Inappropriate application of like-for-like principles in change management
  • Inadequate management of changes conducted by a supplier, leading to life cycle documents and configuration management records that are out-of-date
  • Lack of adequate follow-up after emergency changes

中文解說：高效變更管理

藥品品質系統層級 vs IT 服務管理層級

GAMP 5 特別強調要區分兩個層次的變更：

  • 藥品品質系統層級：影響藥品生命週期的變更（如 BPR 格式變更、放行標準修改）— 須走 GMP 變更控制，QA 核准，可能需要重新驗證
  • IT 服務管理層級：基礎設施的技術變更（如伺服器更新、防毒軟體升級）— 可走 IT 變更管理流程，風險低時無需完整 GMP 驗證流程

混淆這兩個層次是效率低下的主要原因。

「緊急變更」濫用是常見問題

GAMP 5 列出「濫用或誤用緊急變更流程」是效率低下的警示項目。緊急變更應有明確定義（如系統停機影響生產），且每次緊急變更後必須有後續的補充評估和文件補全。若緊急變更佔總變更比例過高（如超過 20%），應重新評估變更管理流程本身。

實務改善：減少不必要的審批層次

GAMP 5 明確建議「最小化審批節點」。可考慮的改善措施：

  • 低風險基礎設施變更（如補丁、防毒更新）設立快速審批路徑
  • 使用「同類替換 (like-for-like)」快速通道，但注意界定標準，並確保不被濫用
  • 建立預批准的標準變更清單 (Standard Change Catalogue)
  • 變更評估在「最低技術能力層級」完成，只有涉及合規決策時才升級至管理層

供應商更新管理：文件同步的挑戰

當供應商進行系統更新，你的驗證文件（FS、測試腳本、驗證報告）必須同步更新。GAMP 5 將「供應商更新導致生命週期文件過時」列為效率低下警示項目。對 SaaS 系統尤為重要——若供應商每季推送功能更新，你的文件管理和再驗證評估流程必須能夠承載這個頻率。

8.8 Anticipating Data Archiving and Migration Needs

Data archiving and migration requirements should be considered to ensure that data structures and formats are efficient.

8.8.1 Different Retention Periods

It may be difficult to archive data with different retention periods that share the same data structures. It may also be difficult to destroy retained data that is no longer required (to reduce risk exposure and retention costs) where data with different retention periods share the same data structures. A data structure that separates data by retention period can address the requirements of archiving and data destruction, but may involve a complex database design.

8.8.2 Data Formats

The migration of custom data formats to a replacement system requires special attention and may cause difficulties. The use of standard data formats should assist subsequent data extraction and migration.

8.8.3 Static and Dynamic Data

Data migration may be complicated where static and dynamic data is combined in a form that is difficult to separate.

8.8.4 Data Ownership

Lack of clear data ownership can lead to failure to appropriately dispose of data at the end of its retention period or make such processes and decisions unnecessarily difficult.

中文解說：資料封存與遷移規劃

在實施前就規劃資料出口策略

許多公司在系統上線 5-10 年後更換系統時，才發現資料遷移是噩夢。GAMP 5 建議在系統實施階段就預先考慮：

  • 不同類型數據的保留期是否一致？（批次記錄 vs 系統日誌 vs 使用者活動記錄）
  • 資料是否使用標準格式儲存（CSV、XML）？還是私有格式？
  • 靜態數據（配置、主資料）與動態數據（批次結果、分析數據）是否可分離？
  • 資料的擁有者是誰？供應商或你？

CDMO 的實際風險場景

場景 1：批次記錄保留期 30 年，系統日誌保留期 2 年，但兩者在同一資料庫表中混合儲存。2 年後你必須刪除系統日誌，但技術上不可能只刪除部分記錄，結果要麼全保留（增加成本），要麼面臨誤刪批次記錄的風險。

場景 2：LIMS 廠商停業或被收購，你的分析數據以私有格式存儲在系統中，無法導出至新系統，被迫繼續支付昂貴的舊系統維護費。

資料所有權條款必須在合約中明確

技術協議應明確規定：你對儲存在供應商（特別是 SaaS 供應商）系統中的 GxP 數據的所有權；服務終止後的數據導出格式和時間框架；及數據保留期結束後的銷毀確認義務。這是資料完整性 (Data Integrity) 合規的基本要求。

8.9 Using Tools and Automation

The use of appropriate tools and automation to support IT process and infrastructure management, system life cycle management, and software specification, development, and testing, can bring significant efficiency improvements, while also increasing quality and lowering risk. The use of such tools is discussed in Appendix D9.

中文解說：工具與自動化

CSV 效率工具概覽

GAMP 5 鼓勵使用工具和自動化，但未指定特定工具。以下是 CDMO 常用的效率工具分類：

用途 工具類型 效率提升點
需求管理 DOORS, Polarion, Jira 追溯矩陣自動生成，變更影響分析
測試管理 ALM/QC, TestRail, Zephyr 電子測試執行，自動統計通過率
自動化測試 Selenium, UFT, Robot Framework 重複性測試自動執行，減少手動測試時間
文件管理 Veeva Vault, DocuSign 電子核准簽章，版本控制
程式碼品質 SonarQube, GitLab CI 自動靜態分析，持續整合測試

工具本身也需要驗證

使用自動化測試工具進行 GxP 系統測試時，測試工具本身也需要驗證（Computer Software Assurance）。這是許多 CDMO 在採用自動化測試時容易忽略的合規要求。相關指引可參考 ISPE GAMP RDI GPG: Data Integrity by Design, Appendix S2。

Section Summary  |  章節總結

Chapter 7 establishes that while GxP compliance responsibility remains with the regulated company, supplier activities can be formally leveraged to reduce the regulated company's validation burden — provided the supplier is properly assessed. The 12-step good practices framework (Table 7.1) defines what a qualified supplier should deliver, from QMS establishment through retirement management.

第 7 章確立了：GxP 合規責任雖始終在受規管公司，但在完成正式評估後，供應商的活動可被正式借用以減少驗證負擔。12 步驟良好實踐框架定義了合格供應商應提供的完整服務範圍。

Chapter 8 provides 9 actionable efficiency strategies. The most impactful for resource-constrained CDMOs are: (1) leveraging supplier test evidence with documented justification; (2) eliminating unnecessary screenshots and test witnesses; (3) reusing existing validation documentation for similar systems; and (4) applying risk-based test depth rather than uniform comprehensive testing.

第 8 章提供 9 項可操作的效率策略。對資源有限的 CDMO 最具價值的四項是：借用供應商測試證據（有書面依據）、取消不必要的截圖和見證、重用既有類似系統的驗證文件、以及基於風險決定測試深度（而非統一測試所有項目）。

  • GAMP Category 3/4/5 determines the scope and depth of supplier involvement and regulated company verification obligations.
  • Sub-supplier management, especially for cloud-hosted GxP data, directly impacts regulated company compliance and must be transparent.
  • Risk registers should be searchable and reused across projects and change events — not created anew each time.
  • Commercial release (supplier activity) is entirely separate from GxP release to production (regulated company activity).
  • Data archiving and migration strategy should be designed at system implementation, not at retirement.
3

Section 3: App M1-M4: Validation Planning, Supplier Assessment, QRM & Software Categories

附錄M1-M4：確效規劃、供應商評估、QRM與軟體類別 | p85-p134

ISPE GAMP 5 Second Edition | p85 – p106

Learning Objectives 學習目標

  1. Distinguish between a Validation Policy, Validation Master Plan (VMP), and a computerized system Validation Plan — and know when each is required. 區分驗證政策、驗證主計畫 (VMP) 與系統驗證計畫的層次，並知道何時需要各層文件。
  2. Define the mandatory content elements of a computerized system validation plan, including scope, risk management, validation strategy, deliverables, and acceptance criteria. 掌握系統驗證計畫的必備要素：範疇、風險管理、驗證策略、交付件與接受標準。
  3. Explain how to correctly scope a CSV validation project — which systems to include and what depth of testing is proportionate to risk. 能正確界定 CSV 驗證專案的範圍，判斷哪些系統須納入、測試深度如何與風險成比例。
  4. Describe the three types of supplier assessment (basic, postal/email audit, on-site/virtual audit) and select the appropriate method based on system impact and supplier risk. 描述三種供應商評估類型，並根據系統影響與供應商風險選擇適當方式。
  5. Apply the M2 supplier assessment process — from initial risk decision through audit, corrective actions, acceptance, and periodic re-evaluation. 執行 M2 供應商評估流程：初始風險決策 → 稽核 → 矯正行動 → 接受 → 定期再評估。
  6. Identify red flags in supplier assessment results that indicate more in-house regulated company testing is required. 識別供應商評估中的紅旗警訊，判斷何時需要強化自有測試以彌補供應商不足。

Appendix M1 — Validation Planning: Introduction & Scope

9.1 Introduction

Appendix M1 covers the production of individual validation plans for systems or projects (computerized systems validation plans), and also gives information on validation policies and Validation Master Plans (VMPs) for background and context.

Computerized system validation plans describe how the validation is to be performed for specific systems. Validation policies define management intent and commitment. VMPs describe the areas of the company where validation is required and provide an overview of validation planning for those areas.

It is a regulatory expectation that validation activities are planned — see for example EU Annex 11, Section 4.

Changes from GAMP 5 First Edition

  • Take into account the validation of SaaS solutions
  • Take into account the validation of systems developed in an incremental or iterative manner (Agile)
  • De-emphasize VMP, with the main focus remaining on computerized system validation planning

9.2 Scope

This guidance may be applied to all GxP regulated computerized systems — both new and existing systems, and sites and organizations in which these systems are used.

Where a computer system is regarded as one component of a wider manufacturing process or system — particularly in an integrated QbD environment — specific and separate computerized system validation may not be necessary, and separate computerized system validation plans would not be required. This environment requires both complete product and process understanding and that the CPPs can be accurately and reliably predicted and controlled over the design space.

For automated manufacturing equipment, separate computer system validation should be avoided. Computer system specification and verification should be part of an integrated engineering approach to ensure compliance and fitness for intended use of the complete automated equipment.

中文解說：文件層次結構

三層文件架構

GAMP 5 把 CSV 的規劃文件分成三個層次，很多人混用，但邏輯其實很清楚：

  • 驗證政策 (Validation Policy)：公司層級，定義整體方針與管理承諾。通常是一份 SOP 或 Corporate Procedure，說明「我們公司如何處理 CSV」。
  • 驗證主計畫 VMP：Site 或大型專案層級，列出範圍內所有設施/系統/流程及其驗證狀態、排程、變更控制方式。是稽查員常看的文件。
  • 系統驗證計畫 (CSV Plan / SVP)：單一系統層級，詳細描述如何驗證這個特定系統。這是 M1 的核心主題。

比喻：工廠建設

把這三個文件想成蓋工廠：

  • 驗證政策 = 公司的「建設規範手冊」
  • VMP = 整個廠區的建設總計畫書
  • 系統驗證計畫 = 某棟建築物的施工圖

沒有每棟都有施工圖，整個廠就蓋不起來。沒有總計畫，施工圖之間就沒有協調。

GAMP 5 第二版的重要轉向

第二版明確「去強調 VMP」——這是個值得注意的訊號。監管機關越來越在意你每個系統有沒有做好，而不是有沒有一份漂亮的 VMP 文件。

SaaS 和 Agile 的納入也很重要：LIMS 越來越多走 SaaS，MES 廠商開始用 Agile 開發，傳統的 V-model 驗證計畫需要調整。

範圍判斷：什麼系統要獨立做 CSV？

GAMP 明確說：如果電腦系統是「製程設備的一部分」（例如填充機的 PLC），就應該整合在設備確效 (Equipment Qualification) 裡，不要單獨做 CSV。

CDMO 常見錯誤：對每台高壓滅菌器的控制器各做一份 CSV 計畫，造成文件爆炸但沒有實質效益。正確做法是在設備 IQ/OQ 裡涵蓋 PLC 的軟體確認。

9.3 Computerized System Validation Plans — Content Requirements

9.3.1 General Guidelines

A computerized system validation plan should be produced for each GxP regulated computerized system focusing on aspects related to patient safety, product quality, and data integrity. It should summarize the system and/or project, identify measures for success, and clearly define criteria for final acceptance and release of the system.

The plan should define:

  • What activities are required
  • How they will be performed and who is responsible
  • What the output will be
  • What the requirements are for acceptance
  • How compliance will be maintained for the lifetime of the system

The level of detail in the plan should reflect the risk, complexity, and novelty of the system. For simple or low-risk systems a separate plan may not be needed — applicable aspects of planning may be covered within another document or process.

Planning should commence as early as possible, ideally no later than during the development of the initial user requirements.

The plan, along with the associated report, may be one of the first documents offered during an inspection or audit to demonstrate regulatory compliance. It should therefore be written at a level suitable to be understood by a wide readership. Jargon and technical detail should be avoided.

9.3.2 Roles and Responsibilities

Responsibility for computerized system validation planning ultimately rests with the process owner. This may be delegated to a project manager and also may involve the system owner.

Typically, the computerized system validation plan is approved by the process owner and quality unit.

Even though regulated companies cannot delegate their regulatory accountabilities to a supplier or service provider, they may leverage the knowledge, experience, and activities of the supplier or service provider through risk-based assessment, management, and governance processes.

In the case of SaaS, the plan should describe how the regulated company will leverage product specification and verification activities performed by the supplier as part of product development and performed under the supplier's QMS. The plan should describe the configuration specification and verification activities and user acceptance activities required to ensure fitness for intended use.

中文解說：驗證計畫的本質

驗證計畫 = 策略文件，不是測試腳本

很多人把驗證計畫寫成測試腳本的目錄，這是誤解。驗證計畫的核心功能是回答：

  • 這個系統的 GxP 風險在哪？
  • 我們打算用什麼策略確認它合規且適合使用？
  • 整個生命週期誰負責什麼？

測試腳本是執行層的文件，會在後面的 OQ/PQ Protocol 裡。

稽查員的視角

GAMP 明確說：驗證計畫是稽查中「第一個被拿出來看」的文件。稽查員用它來了解你的整體策略，再決定要深挖哪裡。

所以寫驗證計畫時要想：「這份文件能讓一個不熟悉這個系統的 FDA 稽查員，在 15 分鐘內理解我們的合規策略嗎？」

SaaS 系統的特殊處理

用 SaaS LIMS（如 LabVantage Cloud、Veeva Vault）時，供應商負責大部分基礎架構和應用程式的驗證。你的驗證計畫需要說明：

  • 你如何「借用」供應商的驗證文件（SOC 2 報告、IQ/OQ 文件）
  • 你自己要做哪些 Configuration Qualification 和 UAT
  • 供應商更新版本時你的維護策略

監管責任永遠在你這邊，不能推給供應商。

CDMO 實務：誰核准驗證計畫？

GAMP 說：流程負責人 (Process Owner) + 品質單位 (QU)。

在 CDMO 實際操作中，通常是：

  • LIMS → QC 主管 (Process Owner) + QA
  • MES → 製造主管 + QA
  • ERP → IT/Finance 主管 + QA（GxP 範圍內的模組）

IT 部門通常不是 Process Owner，他們是技術支援者。這個角色釐清非常重要，否則驗證計畫永遠找不到人負責。

9.3.3 Contents of the Computerized System Validation Plan

Required Content Sections

9.3.3.1 Introduction and Scope

  • The scope of the system
  • The objectives of the validation process
  • Applicable main regulations
  • Review, maintenance, or update process for the plan itself

9.3.3.2 System Overview

  • Business purpose and intended use for the system
  • A description of the system and its data at a high level
  • System scope and boundaries, and overview of the system architecture

Diagrams are encouraged. If the system is being developed using an incremental and iterative approach (Agile), information relevant to the initial release should be provided.

9.3.3.3 Organizational Structure

Roles and responsibilities should be described. Regulated company roles typically include:

  • Project manager — project management, planning, control of resources and costs, monitoring progress, reporting to senior management, liaising with the quality unit
  • Quality unit — ensuring compliance, reviewing and approving deliverables, approving the release of the system
  • Process owner / system owner — implementing and managing the system
  • SMEs — planning and defining verification strategies, performing reviews, defining acceptance criteria, selecting test methods, executing tests, reviewing results

The number of personnel required to approve specific documents should be kept to a minimum.

9.3.3.4 Quality Risk Management

An initial risk assessment should be performed based on an understanding of business processes, initial user requirements, regulatory requirements, and known functional areas. The results should include a GxP assessment decision and an overall assessment of system impact.

Large enterprise systems (e.g., ERP) may have some functionality declared GxP relevant while other functionality is outside the GxP scope. The method by which this decision is made should be described.

9.3.3.5 Validation Strategy

The strategy should be based on:

  • Risk assessment
  • Assessment of system components and architecture
  • Supplier assessment

The validation strategy should describe the life cycle model; specification and verification approach (linear, iterative, incremental, or Agile); inputs and outputs required for each stage; acceptance criteria; approach to traceability; approach to design review; and approach to leveraging supplier activities.

9.3.3.6 Deliverables

The deliverable items to be produced should be listed, including responsibility for production, review, and approval. Note that deliverables may include records within tools and supporting systems and are not constrained to traditional documentation.

9.3.3.7 Acceptance Criteria

The overall acceptance criteria for the system should be described. The approach to handling significant deviations should be defined. For Agile development, acceptance criteria are typically defined in the Minimum Viable Product (MVP) and Definition of Done (DoD).

9.3.3.8 Change Control

Requirements for project change control should be defined, including reference to relevant procedures and/or tools. The stage at which operational change control will be applied should be defined.

9.3.3.9 Standard Operating Procedures

The SOPs to be created or updated as a result of the implementation of the system should be defined, with responsibility for their production, review, and approval.

9.3.3.10 Supporting and Operational Processes

  • Training (including project team and user training)
  • Documentation, record, and knowledge management
  • Configuration management
  • Maintaining compliance and fitness for intended use
  • Operational processes

9.3.3.11 Glossary

Definitions of any terms and abbreviations that may be unfamiliar to the readership should be included.

中文解說：驗證計畫各要素的實務意義

必備內容要素總覽
