The use of tables and diagrams to illustrate CS and DS is highly recommended. Standardized tables help ensure all relevant parameters and settings have been defined. Diagrams can clarify data flow, control logic, data structures, interfaces, and mapping to corresponding business processes.

Configuration and design should cover both hardware and software aspects. Each specification in a tier should be uniquely referenced and traceable back to its appropriate higher-level specification.

Where a system is hosted by a service provider, the CS/DS are typically produced and maintained by the service provider. The regulated company should leverage the service provider effort and where necessary produce a supplementary specification based upon the system configurations required to support the intended business process. Oversight should be maintained through a quality agreement.

All specifications should be structured in a way that supports traceability through the life cycle from individual requirements to associated testing.

中文解說：CS vs. DS — COTS 與客製軟體

配置規格 (CS) vs. 設計規格 (DS)

這是 Appendix D3 最核心的區分：

  • Configuration Specification (CS)：用於已存在的商業軟體 (COTS) 或可配置產品。你不修改原始碼，只設定參數。CS 記錄「我把這個設定設為什麼值，以及為什麼這樣設。」
  • Design Specification (DS)：用於客製化軟體開發。你要設計模組、定義數據結構、撰寫邏輯。DS 記錄「軟體怎麼被建構的。」

比喻：LIMS 配置 vs. 客製系統設計

COTS LIMS（例如 LabWare）：不需要 DS。你需要的是 CS，記錄：哪個樣品類型啟用了哪些欄位？哪個工作流程啟用了電子簽名？稽核軌跡的保存設定是多少天？

客製開發的 MES 模組：需要 DS。詳述：批次記錄的資料庫 schema、每個功能模組的邏輯流程圖、各模組之間的 API 介面定義。

關鍵：如果你無法修改軟體的原始碼（COTS），就不需要 DS——因為軟體的設計由供應商負責，你的責任是配置正確並驗證配置符合你的需求。

CDMO 陷阱：過度指定 COTS 系統的需求

這是 CDMO 採購標準 LIMS 時的常見問題：在 RS 裡寫入非常詳細的配置細節，例如「稽核軌跡畫面需要有特定的欄位排列順序」。

問題在於：COTS 軟體的 UI 是固定的，你無法改變。如果 RS 要求不可能實現的配置，要麼你的 RS 永遠無法被滿足，要麼你需要不斷地 justify deviation。

正確做法：RS 描述業務需求（能查詢稽核軌跡），CS 記錄系統提供的實際配置（稽核軌跡在 Admin > Reports > Audit Trail 模組），並確認它滿足業務需求。

SaaS / 雲端系統的特殊考量

當使用雲端 SaaS 系統（例如 Veeva Vault QMS）時：

  • CS/DS 通常由服務供應商維護
  • CDMO 應要求供應商提供系統配置文件，並在質量協議中明確要求
  • CDMO 需要產出「補充配置規格」，記錄你在 SaaS 系統中做的客戶端配置（如工作流程、角色權限、自定義欄位）
  • 供應商的基礎設施驗證（IQ）由供應商承擔，但你需要確認他們有適當的 SOC 2 或等效認證

D3.3.3 Configuration Specification Content

Configuration Specification

The required configuration of components to be provided as all or part of the solution should be defined. This includes but is not limited to:

  • Required configuration settings or parameters
  • Reason for setting, with reference to controlling specification (i.e., the RS requirement it fulfills)
  • Tools or methods that will be used to set the required options
  • Dependencies and impacts on other modules or systems
  • Infrastructure items such as operating systems and layered software
  • Security of settings

For simple systems it may be possible to incorporate this information into the RS.

Configuration Introduction Section

The introduction to a CS/DS should contain:

  • Ownership of the document
  • Who produced the document, under what authority, and for what purpose
  • The contractual status of the document (if applicable)
  • Relationship to other documents (RS, other configuration or design specifications, etc.)

Configuration Overview Section

The overview should briefly describe the configuration and/or design as defined in the document, including the storage and in some cases, location of the records and the involved systems. The overview may be illustrated using diagrams. The overview should not contain detailed design information.

中文解說：CS 的關鍵要素

CS 最重要的欄位：「為什麼這樣設定」

一份合格的配置規格不只記錄「設定值是什麼」，更要記錄「為什麼這樣設定」——並連結到 RS 中對應的需求 ID。

例如：

配置項目設定值理由/RS 需求 ID
密碼最短長度8 字元RS-SEC-003：符合公司密碼政策及 21 CFR Part 11 §11.300
Session 逾時30 分鐘RS-SEC-004：防止未授權存取，符合 Annex 11 §12
稽核軌跡保存7 年RS-DATA-008：EU GMP Part II §4.9 批次記錄保存要求
電子簽名欄位已啟用：批次放行、偏差關閉RS-GMP-012：需要 Qualified Person 電子簽名符合 21 CFR §211.68

這個追溯結構，讓驗證測試人員在撰寫 OQ/PQ 測試案例時，能直接對應到 CS 中的配置，再對應到 RS 中的需求。

配置管理：設定不能隨便改

一旦系統通過驗證（已核准的配置基準 Configuration Baseline），任何配置更改都需要走 Change Control 程序，重新評估影響並進行再驗證。

常見問題：IT 管理員在維護時「順手」改了某個系統參數（例如把 Session 逾時從 30 分鐘改成 120 分鐘），沒有走 Change Control。這在稽核時是重大缺失，因為已驗證狀態（Validated State）已被破壞。

D3.3.4 Hardware Design Specification

Hardware Design

Hardware Design Specifications (DS) are required for custom applications. The overall architecture of the hardware required should be defined. At a high level this may be illustrated by an annotated block diagram.

Computer System Architecture

The following should be covered as appropriate:

  • Main computer system: primary hardware components (CPU, memory, bus type, clock accuracy) or Virtual Machine (VM) components (VM software, processing unit, memory, elasticity of setup)
  • Storage including location of data: all proposed storage devices with maximum storage capacities (hard disk, cloud storage)
  • Peripherals: including sensors, wearables, mobile devices, and BYOD setups
  • Interconnections/networks: all interconnections of hardware components and connections to external equipment, including cable specifications, connector specifications, network connections, wireless connections, and bandwidth capabilities
  • Configuration: DIP switch settings, device addresses, pin assignments, encryption, mobile device lockdown
  • Embedded systems (within process equipment): layout diagrams, location diagrams for sensors, electrical wiring diagrams, P&ID drawings

Inputs and Outputs

Input and output formats should be specified where necessary. For external equipment: accuracy, isolation, range of current and voltage, type and numbers of interface cards, timing, and encryption and security.

Environment & Electrical Supplies

The operating environment for hardware should define: temperature, humidity, external interference, physical security, shielding against RF/EMI/UV, hardening against dust or vibration, and location. Electrical supply requirements should address: filtering, loading, grounding protection, UPS, and power consumption/heat emission for HVAC capacity calculations.

中文解說：硬體設計規格

哪種系統需要硬體 DS？

並非所有電腦化系統都需要硬體 DS。以下是判斷指南：

  • 需要 HDS：客製化嵌入式控制系統（如灌裝機 PLC 控制盤）、客製化硬體整合（如特殊感測器介面）、複雜的網路架構設計
  • 通常不需要 HDS：標準 COTS 軟體執行在供應商提供的伺服器上、SaaS 系統（硬體由雲端供應商管理）、標準 PC 工作站執行 LIMS 用戶端

CDMO 實務：環境條件需求

在無菌製藥 CDMO 環境中，硬體設計需特別注意：

  • 潔淨室內的觸控螢幕：IP 防護等級（通常需要 IP65+）、易清潔表面設計
  • 電磁干擾 (EMI)：灌裝設備的電機可能影響附近的 PLC 訊號，需要適當屏蔽
  • UPS 需求：批次記錄系統在停電時必須有足夠時間完成資料儲存
  • 嵌入式系統（灌裝機）：必須有硬體設計文件（P&ID、電氣圖）才能進行 IQ

D3.3.5 Software Design Specification

Software Design

Software should be designed in accordance with recognized design standards where appropriate. Design Specifications covering software design are required for custom applications. This is not normally required for configurable products, where software design is normally reviewed or evaluated as part of the supplier assessment and is often proprietary.

Software Description

The modules that will form the system should be described, briefly stating the purpose of each. A list of all interfaces between modules, and any interfaces to external systems should be given. A system diagram is recommended. For SaaS the delivery model (e.g., single-instance-multitenant) should be described.

System Data

System data and the major data objects should be defined. Data should be characterized in a hierarchical manner with complex objects built up of simpler objects:

  • Instances and tenants
  • Databases and collections of files
  • Files / Records

Data objects should include: data types, data format, data precision, and data accuracy. Each file and data structure should be uniquely identified. The use of formal data description methods such as Entity Relationship Models should be considered. In multitenant environments, the method of data separation and security should be described.

Module Description

For each software module:

  • Module operation: may take the form of pseudo code or a flow chart
  • Interfaces to other modules
  • Error handling and data checking
  • Data mapping to each module
  • Data load and module performance aspects

For each sub-program:

  • Sub-program operation (pseudo code or flow chart)
  • The steps and inputs/outputs from each step
  • Parameters: input/output/input-output, pass by value/reference
  • Algorithms, side effects, language including version
  • Reference to programming standards
  • Description of all display screens and all implemented reports

中文解說：軟體設計規格與可追溯性

追溯性：從需求到設計，再到測試

DS 不只是技術文件，它是驗證計畫的骨架。完整的追溯矩陣結構：

RS 需求 ID → CS/DS 設計章節 → 驗證測試案例 ID → 測試結果

例如：

  • RS-SEC-003（密碼最短 8 字元）→ CS 第 4.2 節（密碼策略配置）→ OQ-TC-015（密碼長度驗證測試）→ PASS
  • RS-AUDIT-007（批次數據修改記錄稽核軌跡）→ DS 模組 3.4（稽核軌跡引擎設計）→ OQ-TC-042（稽核軌跡完整性測試）→ PASS

沒有追溯矩陣，驗證測試就是「測了什麼東西」，而不是「證明了系統滿足了哪些需求」。

設計審查 (Design Review)：不只是文件審查

Appendix M5 更詳細地涵蓋設計審查。但 D3 中的核心訊息是：設計審查是確保 CS/DS 正確的關鍵步驟。

誰需要參加設計審查？

  • 系統擁有者（System Owner）
  • 業務流程擁有者（Business Process Owner）
  • IT 代表（確認技術可行性）
  • QA 代表（確認 GxP 合規性）
  • 驗證工程師（確認可驗證性）

設計審查要檢查什麼？

  • 每個 RS 需求都有對應的 CS/DS 章節嗎？（完整性）
  • 配置/設計是否確實滿足了需求？（充分性）
  • 配置/設計是否引入了 RS 中未提及的功能？（範圍控制）
  • 所有 GxP critical 需求都有對應的驗證測試案例嗎？

CDMO 陷阱：不做設計審查

許多 CDMO 跳過設計審查，直接進入 OQ 測試。結果是在 OQ 時才發現設計（或配置）與需求不符，需要重做配置並重新測試，浪費大量時間。

設計審查的成本永遠低於驗證後的返工。一般規則：在開始 IQ/OQ 之前，CS/DS 必須已完成設計審查並核准。

多租戶 SaaS：數據隔離的重要性

當 CDMO 使用多租戶 SaaS 系統（例如 Veeva Vault）時，DS 必須清楚說明各租戶的數據如何隔離。這對 CDMO 尤其重要，因為你可能同時為多個客戶（Sponsor）管理數據，必須確保客戶 A 的數據不可被客戶 B 存取。這項需求通常需要在供應商的安全架構審查中確認，並記錄在質量協議中。

The Traceability Chain: Requirements → Design → Testing

Complete Lifecycle Traceability

A fundamental principle throughout Appendices D1 and D3 is that all specifications should be structured to support traceability through the entire life cycle from individual requirements through configuration/design and into testing. This is referenced in both appendices as fundamental to GxP validation.

Traceability Requirements for RS

  • Requirements should be uniquely identified and version controlled
  • Requirements should enable clear communication and management of critical requirements throughout the life cycle
  • Requirements should be linked to the associated business-process step(s) where appropriate
  • Requirements should support full traceability through configuration/design and testing — see Appendix M5

Traceability Requirements for CS/DS

  • All specifications should be structured in a way that supports traceability through the life cycle from individual requirements to associated testing
  • Each specification in a tier should be uniquely referenced and traceable back to its appropriate higher-level specification
  • This high-level design should also be traceable to the RS, where appropriate

Design Review and Traceability (Reference to Appendix M5)

Further information on design review and traceability is provided in Appendix M5. The design review process is the formal mechanism through which the traceability chain is verified — confirming that the CS/DS adequately addresses all requirements in the RS before proceeding to testing.

中文解說：可追溯性是驗證計畫的骨幹

完整追溯鏈結構

業務流程需求
    ↓
RS 需求 ID（例：RS-GMP-007）
    ↓
法規依據（例：EU GMP Annex 11 §9）
    ↓
CS/DS 章節（例：CS 第 5.3 節：電子簽名配置）
    ↓
驗證測試案例 ID（例：OQ-TC-023）
    ↓
測試結果 + 通過/失敗 + 測試人員簽名

全部整合於「追溯矩陣（Traceability Matrix）」

追溯矩陣的實際用途

追溯矩陣不是一份「做給查核員看的」文件，它在專案中有實際的工程用途：

  • 計畫驗證範疇：所有 GMP critical 需求都需要測試——追溯矩陣讓你確保沒有遺漏
  • 評估變更影響：系統變更時，快速識別哪些需求、哪些測試案例需要重新評估
  • 稽核準備：查核員要求「請給我看稽核軌跡需求如何被驗證」——追溯矩陣一秒找到答案
  • 偏差調查：系統出現異常時，快速追溯到相關的設計決策和驗證依據

追溯矩陣的最小化範例（CDMO LIMS）

RS ID需求描述CS/DS 章節測試案例結果
RS-SEC-003密碼最短 8 字元CS §4.2OQ-TC-015PASS
RS-AUDIT-007批次數據修改記錄稽核軌跡CS §6.1OQ-TC-042PASS
RS-INT-011與 SAP 雙向批號介面DS §8.3OQ-TC-067PASS
RS-DATA-015資料保存 7 年CS §9.4OQ-TC-089PASS

Section Summary — 章節總結

  • RS is the "what," CS/DS is the "how." A Requirements Specification defines business needs independent of technical solutions. Configuration and Design Specifications explain how those needs will be implemented. Never mix the two. — RS 是「要做什麼」，CS/DS 是「怎麼做」。兩者的界線是驗證邏輯的基礎。
  • SMART requirements enable validation. A requirement that cannot be tested cannot be validated. The most common failure is writing compliance statements instead of testable functional requirements. — 可測試性是 SMART 的核心。「符合 Part 11」不是需求——具體的密碼策略、稽核軌跡欄位才是。
  • The requirements hierarchy flows top-down. URS (business) → FRS (functional) → CS/DS (implementation). Each level derives from the one above and must remain traceable to it. — 需求從業務到技術層層細化，每層都可追溯到上一層。
  • CS for COTS, DS for custom. Configured commercial software needs a Configuration Specification recording parameters and their business justification. Custom-developed software needs a full Design Specification including module architecture, data structures, and algorithms. — COTS 軟體用 CS（記錄配置參數與理由），客製軟體用 DS（設計模組與邏輯）。
  • Traceability is the backbone of validation. Every requirement should trace forward to a design decision and a test case. The Traceability Matrix is the instrument that makes this explicit, supports impact assessment, and provides evidence for regulatory review. — 追溯矩陣不是裝飾品，是變更控制和稽核防禦的核心工具。
  • Two critical CDMO pitfalls: over-specifying COTS and under-specifying URS. Over-specifying COTS creates requirements that cannot be met (you can't configure what the software doesn't allow). Under-specifying URS leads to scope creep and a system that doesn't meet business needs. — 對 COTS 過度規格化 → 無法實現的需求；對 URS 規格不足 → 範圍蔓延。兩者都是系統驗證專案失敗的常見原因。
ISPE GAMP 5, 2nd Edition | Appendices D4–D5 | p207 – p234

Learning Objectives — 學習目標

  • Understand the GAMP 5 approach to software development lifecycle, version control, code review, and release management for GxP systems (理解 GAMP 5 對 GxP 系統軟體開發生命週期、版本控制、代碼審查及發布管理的要求)
  • Distinguish IQ, OQ, and PQ in the context of computerized systems (computer CSV) versus traditional equipment qualification (區分電腦化系統驗證情境下 IQ/OQ/PQ 與傳統設備確認的差異)
  • Apply a risk-based test strategy to determine the appropriate level and type of testing required for different software categories (應用風險為基礎的測試策略，決定不同軟體類別所需測試層次與類型)
  • Differentiate scripted vs. unscripted testing approaches and know when each is appropriate (區分腳本式與非腳本式測試方法，並了解各自的適用情境)
  • Explain defect management during validation: how to classify critical, major, and minor defects, and apply a go/no-go decision framework (解釋驗證期間缺陷管理：如何分類嚴重、主要、次要缺陷，並應用放行決策框架)
  • Describe regression testing and test environment management best practices, including why a dedicated validated test environment separate from production is essential (說明迴歸測試與測試環境管理最佳實踐，包括為何需要獨立的已驗證測試環境)
Appendix D4 — Management, Development, and Review of Software (軟體管理、開發與審查)

D4.1 Introduction & Scope

This appendix provides guidance for the management, development, and review of software. It also includes general guidance on coding practices. Software tools to assist with these activities are available, and in general, automation of these processes will lead to better compliance, efficiency, and reproducibility when compared to manual approaches.

Software development should be performed within a defined life cycle. The criteria for releasing developed and tested software should be understood and defined. Software released into the GxP environment should be based on, and meet, defined requirements.

This appendix is not intended to constrain the choice of development methods and models. Suppliers should select and use the most appropriate methods and models for their use. Any examples used, or technologies assumed, are intended to illustrate general principles and are not intended to be restrictive.

Scope: While the main focus is on software development using high-level and low-level languages, the principles of this appendix also may be applied to various techniques used for process control system software development/configuration.

Changes from GAMP 5 First Edition

This appendix has been updated in line with changes made to Appendix D1 (Specifying Requirements), and also to align with information in new appendices D8 (Agile) and D9 (Tools).

中文解說：D4 引言與範圍

D4 的定位：給誰看的？

D4 主要面向軟體供應商（如 LIMS、MES、ERP 廠商）和客製化開發團隊（自行開發 Category 5 軟體的製藥公司）。

核心訊息：GxP 環境中的軟體開發不是「寫完能跑就好」，而必須有定義的生命週期、版本控制、代碼審查，且須在發布前通過定義的驗收準則。

類比理解：軟體開發就像批次製造

製藥生產中，每批原料都有批號、配方、製造步驟記錄、QC 檢驗，且須符合規格才能放行。

軟體開發也一樣：每個版本 (build) 都應有版本號、需求對應、代碼審查記錄、測試報告，且須符合定義的驗收標準才能部署到 GxP 環境。

實務重點

D4 明確指出本指引不限定開發方法（瀑布、Agile 都接受），但要求生命週期必須被定義。這是 GAMP 5 的核心哲學：規定「要做什麼」，不規定「怎麼做」。

D4.3.1 Software Development

The software development method should be defined and regardless of the model used, should also define:

  • Coding standards
  • Code repository standards
  • Software development tools
  • Naming conventions
  • Configuration and use of build and deployment systems

Source code should be subject to review with the approach and extent of such reviews based upon the coding language, tools, and risk to patient safety, product quality, and data integrity.

D4.3.1.1 General Design and Documentation Principles

Software design artifacts should be sufficient to initially develop and subsequently support working software. The degree and nature of the design will be based on the life cycle model used, software complexity, code/configuration language, and interfaces. Design artifacts may be in documentation form or as records within software development tools.

It is good practice to include a Software Bill of Materials (SBOM) that provides the list of components/modules that make up the overall software and can also be used to identify/track inter-dependencies.

Software should ultimately:

  • Meet requirements
  • Be reliable and robust
  • Be maintainable
  • Be capable of handling error conditions
  • Be well designed and sufficiently commented

D4.3.1.2 Software Module Identification

Each software module should include the following attributes:

  • Module name
  • Reference/traceability to associated design artifacts
  • Constituent source file names
  • Module version number
  • Project name/reference (if applicable)
  • Brief description of the module
  • References/dependencies to other software modules
  • Any specific command files required to compile and build the module

中文解說：軟體開發生命週期

SBOM（軟體物料清單）— 新增亮點

GAMP 5 第二版新增了 Software Bill of Materials (SBOM) 的概念。這是仿照製造業 BOM（物料清單）的做法：

  • 列出系統由哪些元件、模組、第三方函式庫組成
  • 識別各元件間的相依關係
  • 在資安漏洞出現時，能快速判斷哪些系統受影響

在驗證 LIMS 時，要求供應商提供 SBOM 已成為新的最佳實踐。

軟體模組識別 = 藥品成分標示

就像每種藥品必須標明活性成分、賦形劑、批號、有效期；每個軟體模組也必須有版本號、對應的需求文件、依賴的其他模組。沒有這些資訊，維護和故障排查將極為困難。

稽核重點

FDA/EMA 查廠時，常見問題是：「你們的 LIMS 版本 3.2.1 與 3.1.0 有什麼差異？是否有變更記錄？」

若無法回答，代表版本控制不足，可能引發 483 observation。

D4.3.1.3–1.7 Version Control, Maintainability & Code Quality

Software Module Change Traceability

All software module changes should be clearly identified according to the chosen software development life cycle and technology used. It should be possible to obtain a history of changes made, which should include the following information for each change:

  • Change request number(s) (if applicable)
  • Applicable version number(s)
  • Dates change(s) made
  • Identity of person(s) changing the code
  • Summary of the changes

D4.3.1.4 Maintainability

Software should be written and structured in a way that a competent person (other than the original author) would be able to understand and modify it safely. The software should be created using the coding standards relevant to the technology.

D4.3.1.5 Open-Source Modules

Where modules are imported from an open-source code repository, updates as and when the open-source code is updated need to be determined. In addition, occasionally open-source modules may be retired, in which case future vulnerabilities will not be addressed, which increases risk.

D4.3.1.6 Removal of Dead Code

Dead code is code that cannot be executed due to the logic of the program, and should be removed. It is usually a symptom of poor maintenance. Code that has been included for purposes of testing or for later diagnosis during support work, and which can be configured on or off, is not regarded as dead code.

D4.3.1.7 Reliability and Error Recovery

"Defensive" coding techniques should be employed. Input values should be checked, and subroutines should check that the values of the received parameters are within range. In the event of a failure, a safe, documented error recovery or a controlled shutdown should be performed, with an informative error message.

Software Configuration Management

Software should be subject to a defined software configuration management process that includes version control of software code, scripts, and any relevant artifacts required by the technologies in use. Such change and version control is especially important during software development, as mistakes in this regard can lead to problems such as reintroduction of previously removed defects.

中文解說：版本控制與代碼品質

版本控制 (Version Control) 的 GxP 意義

版本控制不只是 IT 工具（如 Git），在 GxP 語境下，它必須確保：

  • 可追溯性：每次代碼變更都能追溯到對應的變更請求 (Change Request)
  • 不可篡改：已審查、已測試的版本不能被未授權修改
  • 可重現：能重建任何歷史版本，以便調查問題

Dead Code = 過期庫存

想像工廠倉庫中有一批過期原料，沒人知道能不能用。Dead code 也一樣——存在的代碼應該有明確目的。無法執行的代碼意味著維護不佳，可能有資安或數據完整性風險。

開源軟體 (OSS) 的特殊考量

GAMP 5 第二版顯著擴展了開源軟體的指引。許多 LIMS、MES 都使用開源元件（如 PostgreSQL、Python 函式庫）。監管重點：

  • 開源社群是否仍活躍維護？
  • 安全漏洞更新是否被追蹤？
  • 版本是否被鎖定並文件化？

防禦性程式設計 (Defensive Coding)

對 QC 系統特別重要。例如：儀器傳入異常值（如 -999 的 pH 值）時，系統應拒絕並記錄錯誤，而非接受並計算出荒謬結果。這直接關係到數據完整性。

D4.3.2 Source Code Review

Source code reviews have three objectives:

  • To ensure that programming standards, such as those described above, are consistently and correctly applied
  • To ensure that the code is written in accordance with the design
  • To identify and enable removal of defects

The review aims to ensure that the code is fit to release, and that the code can be effectively and efficiently maintained during the period of use of the application.

The review should be performed by at least one independent person with sufficient knowledge and expertise, in conjunction with the author of the code.

Automated source code review comparison tools are particularly useful when making small changes to existing code.

D4.3.2.1 Static Analysis of Software

"Static analysis involves a set of methods, supported by tools, used to analyze software source code or object code to determine how the software functions and establish criteria to check its correctness."

These include:

  • Control Analysis – analysis of the controls used in calling structure, control flow, and state transitions
  • Data Analysis – ensures proper operation is applied to data objects and data structures
  • Fault/Failure Analysis – identifies incorrectly specified or built components and incorrect behavior of components
  • Interface Analysis – checks the accuracy of interface structure, and the ability to prevent errors during user interaction

Formal Verification methods may also be considered for high-risk areas of code using formal mathematical methods to provide "proof" of algorithms under multiple input conditions.

A decision based upon known risks should determine the extent of software review required for a given project. The criteria for making this assessment, and the outcome, should be documented.

中文解說：源代碼審查

代碼審查的三個 GxP 目標

代碼審查 (Code Review) 在 GxP 環境中不只是品質工具，更是驗證活動的一部分：

  • 合規性確認：編碼標準是否被遵守？
  • 設計一致性：代碼是否實現了設計規格 (DS) 中定義的邏輯？
  • 缺陷識別：在測試前發現問題，成本最低

靜態分析 = 製程前的原料檢驗

靜態分析 (Static Analysis) 是在「不執行代碼」的情況下分析代碼結構。就像進廠原料先做 CoA 審查和鑑別測試，不需要先放入製程才發現問題。

工具範例：SonarQube（代碼品質）、Checkmarx（資安漏洞）

獨立審查 (Independent Review) 的重要性

GAMP 5 要求由不是原始作者的人執行代碼審查。這與 GMP 中「操作者不能是審查者」的原則一致。

在 Category 5 自開發系統驗證中，代碼審查的記錄會被監管機構查核。

D4.3.3 Third-Party Software (including Open-Source)

D4.3.3.1 Purchased Software

In most cases evidence of software control can be obtained through standard mechanisms for supplier assessment, such as supplier audit (see Appendix M2). Conclusions of the assessment should be documented. If inadequacies are noted, the regulated company may require remedial actions by the supplier, possibly enforced via a Service Level Agreement (SLA), or may decide that further testing is required.

D4.3.3.2 Free and Open-Source Software (OSS)

OSS often plays an important role in the infrastructure of regulated companies. Examples include the Linux operating system, R environment for statistical computing, and many web design, programming, and support tools.

Note that commercial software may contain open-source components incorporated into it. It is becoming more common to request a SBOM when evaluating new commercial software or validating in-house developed systems.

If a decision is taken to use OSS, then such software should be implemented in accordance with the appropriate life cycle activities as for commercial software, with consideration of the following:

  • Knowing the size and sustainability of the open-source community
  • Checking for development standards and good documentation
  • Knowing what version is in use — verify download from a reputable source and ensure code was not altered (via checksum)
  • Understanding the governance model for updates and patches
  • Keeping up-to-date with patches and updates; vulnerabilities are often exposed in software using outdated versions of open-source libraries
  • Participating in the open-source community

To determine whether there is an adequate level of software maturity and control, a risk assessment should be performed to determine the business and GxP risks of using OSS products, and to identify appropriate controls.

中文解說：第三方與開源軟體

商業軟體 vs 開源軟體的監管策略

方面 商業軟體 開源軟體 (OSS)
主要控制手段 供應商評估、SLA、稽核 風險評估 + 生命週期管理
代碼可見性 通常不可見 完全公開，可審查
更新控制 供應商負責 使用者自行追蹤
漏洞回應 依 SLA 時限 可能更快，但需主動監控

實際場景：R 語言在 QC 統計分析中的使用

許多 QC 部門使用 R 進行統計分析（如製程能力分析 Cpk）。按 GAMP 5 D4.3.3.2：

  • 需鎖定使用的 R 版本（不能自動更新）
  • 使用的 packages 版本需文件化（SBOM 概念）
  • 更新前需評估對 GxP 功能的影響
  • 統計計算邏輯需經驗證
Appendix D5 — Testing of Computerized Systems (電腦化系統測試)

D5.1 Introduction

This appendix covers the testing of GxP computerized systems. It is not intended to offer a prescriptive approach — it does not require that testing must be done a certain way in a particular sequence. Instead, this appendix identifies the influences on testing and offers information on the types of testing and testing approaches that can be used selectively and in combination for optimal assurance that the system is fit for its intended use.

The application of critical thinking is vital to achieve effective testing that adds value and fulfills objectives such as:

  • Identifying defects so they can be corrected or removed before operational use
  • Reducing the risk of failures that might affect patient safety, product quality, or data integrity
  • Demonstrating that the system as installed and configured meets its requirements
  • Providing evidence that the system is fit for its intended use
  • Offering a basis for user acceptance
  • Meeting a key regulatory requirement
  • Ensuring that risk management controls are effective

Testing should be carried out in accordance with an appropriate test strategy based on the risk to patient safety, product quality, and data integrity. Testing may occur both in the vendor's development life cycle and in the regulated company's implementation life cycle.

Key Changes from GAMP 5 First Edition

  • Critical thinking should be applied when planning testing efforts such that the level of effort is commensurate to the risk acceptable within the organization
  • Testing by any means and in any part of the life cycle all contributes to finding defects and confirming fitness for intended use
  • Testing should not be limited to detailed and prescriptive step-by-step scripted protocols. Exploratory testing and other unscripted techniques are encouraged
  • Modern approaches may rely on records and artifacts in automated tools in place of formal specification and test documentation — either approach is acceptable

中文解說：D5 測試附錄引言

GAMP 5 第二版的測試哲學轉變

與第一版相比，第二版最大的改變是：

  • 去除處方化：不再要求一定要有 URS → FS → DS → IQ → OQ → PQ 的線性流程
  • 擁抱非腳本式測試：探索性測試 (Exploratory Testing) 獲得官方認可
  • 承認工具記錄的有效性：Jira tickets、CI/CD 日誌等工具記錄可作為測試證據
  • 批判性思維是核心：比規程遵從更重要

測試的七大目的 — 記憶要點

這七個目的覆蓋了測試的三個維度：

  • 技術維度：找缺陷、確認需求滿足
  • 監管維度：符合法規要求、提供符合使用目的的證據
  • 風險維度：降低影響病患安全/產品品質/數據完整性的風險、確認風險控制有效

D5.3 Roles and Responsibilities

The regulated company should define roles and responsibilities covering testing. Such definitions typically are included in an appropriate planning document, test strategy, or company procedure. Traditional roles and responsibilities may include:

Role Responsibility
Process Owner Responsible for the business process supported by the system and for the approval of the test strategy and overall test coverage
System Owner Responsible for the system in question and for ensuring system prerequisites are satisfied to allow testing to proceed
SMEs Essential for input to the test strategy and test case design
Test Manager Plans testing approaches and types of testing
Test Analyst Responsible for developing test cases
Tester Should be as independent as possible; should not be the author of the function/feature being tested
Test Reviewer Responsible for reviewing test cases and completed testing; should not be the same person who executed the specific test case
Quality Oversight If applicable and necessary
Supplier Should have already completed substantial testing in their development life cycle. Final responsibility for compliance remains with the regulated company irrespective of any outsourcing.

The quality of the test cases and the functionality they cover directly impact the effectiveness of the testing. No matter who is creating the test case, they should be an SME in the associated field.

中文解說：測試角色責任

獨立性原則 (Independence Principle)

GAMP 5 強調兩個關鍵的獨立性要求：

  • 開發者 ≠ 測試者：寫代碼的人不能測自己的代碼（因為只會確認預期行為，發現不了設計盲點）
  • 執行者 ≠ 審查者：執行測試的人不能審查自己的測試結果

這與 GMP 中「雙人復核」原則相同，確保客觀性。

SME 在測試設計中的角色

GAMP 5 特別強調：測試案例的設計者必須是該領域的 SME。

以 LIMS 的樣品接收功能為例：

  • IT 測試師寫的測試：「填欄位、存檔、確認無錯誤」
  • QC SME 寫的測試：「測試樣品ID重複時系統是否警示」、「測試緊急樣品優先級標記」、「測試跨部門接收時通知邏輯」

SME 測試覆蓋業務場景，IT 測試覆蓋系統功能——兩者缺一不可。

供應商責任 vs 受規管公司責任

無論外包多少，法規合規的最終責任永遠在受規管公司。供應商的測試可以被利用（leveraged），但不能取代受規管公司的驗證決策。

D5.4 Influences on Test Activities & Table 25.1

Test coverage and approaches are influenced by the:

  • Criticality of the business process supported by the system, including the GxP impact
  • Requirements for the system
  • Supplier's development life cycle and quality system
  • Regulated company's internal computerized systems validation policy
  • Risk culture within the company
  • Use and existence of additional controls elsewhere in the business process
  • Level of test automation available

Table 25.1: Key Testing Activities and Their Influences

Activity Key Objectives/Focus Influenced By
Defining Requirements Identifies what the system must do to support the business process and the data integrity technical controls needed. Requirements form the specifications against which test cases will be run. Applicable GxP Regulations; Business Process Map; Data Flow Diagram; Process Risk Assessment
Supplier Assessment Evaluate if the supplier can provide a system of acceptable quality. Extensive well-executed supplier testing can reduce the amount of testing the regulated company needs to complete. Supplier Qualification Process; Requirements; SLA
Validation Planning Defines the GxP impact of the system, the life cycle and test strategy, and the decisions made based on the outcome of the supplier assessment. Applicable GxP Regulations; CSV Policy; Requirements; Supplier Assessment; GxP Risk
Functional Risk Assessment Assesses and prioritizes the risks from the system functionality with the potential to impact patient safety, product quality, and data integrity. Requirements; Risk Assessment Procedure
Test Planning/Coverage Defines the depth and rigor of test coverage and documentation needed based on the assigned risk priority of the function. Requirements; Validation Planning; Supplier Assessment; Functional Risk Assessment
Test Management Processes Defines the testing approach and execution instructions. Often captured in a test plan or SOP. CSV Policy; Validation Planning
Creating Test Cases Test types include scripted/unscripted, manual/automated, exploratory, regression, etc. Most tests have at minimum a defined objective, pass/fail criteria, and reference to the requirement. Test Planning/Traceability Matrix; Configuration Specification
Executing Tests Test execution should meet the objectives of the test cases and generate records/evidence to demonstrate fitness for intended use or allow defects to be addressed. Test Management Processes; Scripted and Unscripted Tests
Reviewing and Reporting Confirm if the functionality operated correctly. Any test failures should be assessed to confirm that defects have been fixed or dispositioned satisfactorily. Test Management Processes; Test Planning/Traceability Matrix; Executed Tests
Validation Reporting Confirms if the validation strategy was implemented as planned and if all requirements have been met and verified based on risk. Document the impact of any non-conformances or outstanding deviations. Applicable GxP Regulations; Validation Planning; Requirements; SLA

中文解說：測試活動的影響因素

風險為基礎的測試策略 — 核心概念

GAMP 5 最重要的訊息之一：不是所有功能都需要相同程度的測試。

測試投入應與風險相稱 (commensurate with risk)：

  • 高風險功能（如電子簽名、批次放行計算）→ 詳細腳本式測試 (Scripted Testing: Robust)
  • 中等風險功能（如報表生成）→ 腳本式有限測試 (Scripted Testing: Limited)
  • 低風險功能（如 UI 偏好設定）→ 非腳本式探索性測試即可

LIMS 驗證的測試規劃實例

以驗證一套 LIMS 為例，根據 Table 25.1 的邏輯：

  • 需求定義：先完成 URS/FRS，確認 GxP 影響範圍
  • 供應商評估：供應商有 GAMP Category 4 軟體的完整測試記錄？可降低受規管公司的測試負擔
  • 功能風險評估：樣品追蹤功能（高風險）vs 報表格式設定（低風險）
  • 測試規劃：高風險功能需 100% 腳本式測試；低風險功能可用探索性測試

驗證報告 (Validation Report) 的關鍵內容

驗證報告不只是「所有測試通過」的總結，還需要：

  • 記錄測試記錄的存放位置（工具中？紙本協議書？）
  • 列出未解決的偏差及其影響評估
  • 確認驗證策略是否按計畫執行

D5.9.1.1 Installation Qualification (IQ) Context for Computerized Systems

Although the term is not used in this Guide (which refers to "installation verification activities" in general), many companies still use the traditional process validation term Installation Qualification (IQ).

The purpose is to verify and document that system components are combined and installed in accordance with specifications, supplier documentation, and local and global requirements. Installation testing provides a verified configuration baseline for subsequent verification and validation activities, and verifies any installation methods, tools, or scripts used.

For cloud-native or virtualized software, the use of automated installers combined with configuration management tools and service management tools will be more effective than conventional installation approaches. If they provide dashboard functionality, then a review-by-exception approach can replace many of the static verification activities.

Whatever the approach, the availability of appropriate technical information should be verified. Examples include:

  • User and technical guides; SOPs; Training schedules
  • SLAs; Security procedures; Log books
  • Hardware inventory; Instrument lists; Specification sheets
  • Certificates and calibration procedures
  • Software inventory (including installation procedure, system software list, application software list, data list, initial data settings)
  • Preventive maintenance program; List of critical spare parts

中文解說：IQ/OQ/PQ 在電腦化系統中的意義

重要：電腦化系統的 IQ/OQ/PQ 與設備確認不同！

許多工程師和 QA 用設備確認的思維套用到軟體驗證，這是常見錯誤。讓我們用 LIMS 為例比較：

LIMS 系統 IQ：安裝確認

目的：確認系統已按規格正確安裝

檢查項目：

  • 硬體規格確認（CPU、RAM、儲存空間是否符合最低需求）
  • 作業系統版本、補丁級別確認
  • LIMS 軟體版本確認（與採購規格一致）
  • 配置文件記錄（資料庫連線設定、網路配置）
  • 安全設定確認（防火牆、使用者權限架構）
  • 備份與還原功能已設置

注意：IQ 確認的是「正確安裝了什麼」，不是功能是否正常運作。

LIMS 系統 OQ：運作確認

目的：確認系統的所有配置功能在預期條件下正常運作

測試內容（對應 FRS 中每一個功能需求）：

  • 樣品接收工作流程測試（正常案例 + 邊界案例）
  • 測試方法配置驗證（計算邏輯、規格限制）
  • 電子簽名功能（簽名、意義、不可否認性）
  • 稽核追蹤（記錄創建、修改、刪除）
  • 使用者權限隔離（QC 人員不能修改方法規格）
  • 儀器接口數據傳輸測試

OQ 是最耗時的階段，通常佔驗證工作量的 60-70%。

LIMS 系統 PQ：性能確認

目的：用真實使用場景（end-to-end）確認系統在實際操作條件下符合使用目的

測試方式：

  • 由實際使用者（QC 分析師、樣品接收人員）執行「Day in the Life」測試
  • 使用真實樣品類型和典型批次數量
  • 完整工作流程：樣品登錄 → 指派 → 分析 → 審查 → 報告 → 批次放行
  • 跨部門整合測試（LIMS ↔ ERP 批次記錄系統）

PQ 回答的問題是：「這套系統真的能支撐我們的業務嗎？」

風險為基礎：不是所有系統都需要 PQ

GAMP 5 不強制要求每個系統都必須有 IQ/OQ/PQ 三階段。低風險 Category 3 系統（如辦公室文書工具）可能只需要安裝驗證 + 有限功能測試。測試的深度由風險決定，不由傳統慣例決定。

D5.5 Test Planning/Coverage & Test Cases

D5.5.1 Test Management Processes

Early and efficient testing, during development as well as during the verification phase, improves defect detection and reduces the occurrence of defects surviving into the operational phase.

A test management process may include:

  • Any special prerequisites to testing
  • Identifying what combination of scripted or unscripted, manual or automated testing will be used
  • The personnel required for each test or group of tests
  • The expectations regarding test evidence (including the recording and reporting of test pass/fail results)
  • How the environment in which the testing is to occur will be identified and recorded
  • How the progress and outcome of testing will be monitored
  • How test cases and completed tests will be reviewed and approved

D5.5.2 Scripted vs. Unscripted Testing — Table 25.2 Summary

Table 25.2: Acceptable Assurance Approaches and Records

Assurance Approach Test Plan Required Test Results Record
Unscripted: Ad-hoc
(least-burdensome)		 Testing of requirements or functions with no test plan; details regarding any failures/deviations found Summary description of requirements or functions tested; issues found and disposition; conclusion statement; record of who performed testing and date
Unscripted: Error Guessing Testing of requirement or function failure modes with optional listing of expected failure modes in advance Summary description of failure modes tested; issues found and disposition; conclusion statement; who performed and date
Unscripted: Exploratory Testing Establish high-level test plan objectives for requirements or functions (no step-by-step procedure necessary) Pass/fail for each test plan objective; issues found and disposition; conclusion statement; who performed and date
Unscripted: Day in the Life Testing Establish high-level test plan objectives for normal day-to-day activities (no step-by-step procedure necessary). Test using business process experience and against SOPs where available. Pass/fail for each test plan objective; summary of activities or business operation challenged; issues found; conclusion; who performed and date
Scripted: Limited Limited test cases (step-by-step procedure) identified; expected results and values; independent review and approval of test plan Pass/fail for each test case; result for each test case (critical values + pass/fail indication); issues found and disposition; conclusion; who performed and reviewed with dates
Scripted: Robust Test objectives; test cases (step-by-step procedure); expected results and values; independent review and approval of test cases Pass/fail for test case; details regarding any failures/deviations found and disposition; detailed report of assurance activity; result for each test case; issues found; conclusion; who performed and reviewed with dates

Table 25.3: Comparison of Unscripted vs. Scripted Testing

Dimension Unscripted Testing Scripted Testing
Primary use Supplement scripted testing; used for low/medium risk functions using critical thinking Used alone or in combination for high-risk functions affecting patient safety, product quality, data integrity
Defect detection Uncovers defects from poorly defined/implemented specs. Dynamic test design allows exploration against specs. Tests against specs to confirm fitness. May miss issues not identified at time of test design.
Repeatability Lower — no detailed step-by-step script Higher — detailed scripted nature enables regression testing
Tester requirements Relies on tester intuition, knowledge, and experience. More sensitive to inexperienced testers. Tests expected user/system behaviors. Uses specification as the standard to verify.
Regression testing Not directly suitable for regression testing Manual or automated scripted testing can provide the basis for regression testing

中文解說：測試文件要求

核心問題：哪些文件需要事前批准？哪些是事後記錄？

這是 QA 審查員最常問的問題。Table 25.2 給出了清晰答案：

  • 腳本式測試（Scripted: Limited/Robust）：測試腳本 (test script) 必須在執行前經過獨立審查和批准
  • 非腳本式測試：只需在執行前有高層次的測試目標，步驟不需要預先定義
  • 所有測試：結果記錄（包括誰做、何時做、發現了什麼）在執行後記錄即可

「非腳本式 ≠ 未文件化」

GAMP 5 明確指出："Unscripted testing does not mean undocumented testing."

非腳本式測試的最低文件要求：

  • 測試了什麼（what was tested）
  • 由誰測試（by whom）
  • 何時測試（when）
  • 發現了哪些問題（any issues found）

探索性測試 = 製程開發中的 DOE

在製程開發中，實驗設計 (DOE) 讓你系統性地探索參數空間，發現意料之外的交互作用。探索性測試類似：測試者用自己的知識系統地探索軟體，發現腳本式測試可能遺漏的邊界案例。

PDCA 循環：計劃探索目標 → 執行 → 記錄發現 → 調整方向繼續探索

截圖過多不是好事

GAMP 5 明確批評「prolific screenshots」的做法。原則：

  • 通過 (Pass)：記錄「Pass」即可，不需截圖
  • 失敗 (Fail)：記錄「Fail」+ 描述實際結果 vs 預期結果的差異
  • 截圖只在需要「前後對比」的複雜數據場景下才有價值

D5.5.3 Executing Tests

The quality of testing is significantly impacted by the knowledge and skill of the tester, therefore:

  • Day in the life testing needs to be executed by a skilled business process user
  • All other manual testing needs to be executed by a skilled software tester; where unscripted testing is used, knowledge of the system under test is also essential
  • All staff responsible for test execution, including end users, should be trained in test procedures and should be able to demonstrate sufficient confidence in operating the system under test
  • Training should be documented

The identity of the tester should be recorded for all executed test cases. It is disproportionate and unnecessary to use test witnessing or to require the tester to initial every test step.

Automated test tools require a documented assessment of their adequacy prior to use.

Test Evidence — Critical Thinking

It is recommended to apply critical thinking when defining the need for test records and evidence:

  • Ensure that even where testing is not scripted in detail, the objective of the test remains clear, and the results record adequately what testing was carried out
  • Ensure that test evidence is only collected for proving steps that are not inherently covered by evidence from another test
  • Adopt an exception-reporting approach: if the system response matches expected results, a simple "Pass" can be recorded. If the system responds unexpectedly, record both a "Fail" and a description of how the response differed
  • Recognize that routine requirements for screenshots as objective evidence bring little value to verification activities

D5.5.4 Reviewing and Reporting Completed Tests

Completed testing should be reviewed to verify that the computerized system is fit for its intended use. While test evidence should be reviewed to confirm completeness and accuracy, there is little value in:

  • Looking for minor errors in documentation that have no impact on patient safety, product quality, or data integrity
  • Scrutinizing test evidence in extreme detail to assess whether the tester has exactly followed the test instructions for non-critical functionality

Unusual patterns of test failures associated with particular authors and/or individual testers should be investigated to determine whether there are any wider testing implications.

Test reports should be produced that summarize activities and findings and state the final conclusions.

中文解說：測試執行與缺陷管理

缺陷管理 (Defect Management) — 驗證期間的決策框架

測試期間發現的缺陷需要按嚴重程度分類，然後決定是否可以繼續推進驗證：

缺陷類型 定義 處置方式 Go/No-Go
嚴重 (Critical) 直接影響病患安全、數據完整性，或導致 GxP 不合規（如電子簽名功能失效） 必須修復，重新執行相關測試，更新測試報告 No-Go — 不得放行
主要 (Major) 影響核心業務功能，但不直接危及患者安全；有可行的暫時性工作繞道方案 記錄缺陷、記錄暫時性工作程序 (workaround)、排入補丁計畫 可有條件 Go — 需 QA 批准風險評估
次要 (Minor) UI 問題、非 GxP 功能的小錯誤、格式問題 記錄缺陷、排入未來版本修復 Go — 可放行，但需在驗證報告中說明

例外報告原則 (Exception-Reporting Approach)

GAMP 5 的高效測試記錄原則：

  • 正常情況：記錄「Pass」就足夠
  • 異常情況：記錄「Fail」+ 預期結果 + 實際結果 + 差異描述

這消除了大量不必要的文件工作（如逐步截圖），讓測試者可以專注在真正有價值的缺陷記錄上。

測試審查的重點是功能，不是文件格式

GAMP 5 明確指出，測試審查的焦點是：「功能是否正確運作？」，而非「測試者是否精確遵循每個步驟？」

常見的過度稽核現象（GAMP 5 明確不鼓勵）：

  • 要求測試者在每一步旁邊簽名確認
  • 因為日期格式寫成 01/04 而非 2026-04-01 就 reject 整份測試記錄

D5.6 Types of Testing

D5.6.1 Test Types Unique to Unscripted Testing

  • Ad-hoc testing — unscripted testing performed without planning or predefined documentation. Aimed at finding defects as early as possible.
  • Error guessing — a testing technique designed to expose anticipated and potential defects based on the specialist tester's knowledge and experience of failure modes.
  • Exploratory testing — experience-based testing where the tester spontaneously designs and executes tests based on existing specialist knowledge, prior exploration, and typical common software behaviors and types of failure and defects.
  • Day in the life testing — allows users of the system to carry out their normal day-to-day activities to uncover issues not identified by scripted testing. These testers need real-life business process experience and knowledge.

D5.6.2 Other Test Types (Scripted or Unscripted)

  • White box testing (structural testing) — test cases identified based on the internal structure (source code) of the component or system.
  • Black box testing (functional testing) — based on an analysis of the specification, without reference to internal structure.
  • Normal Case testing — challenges the system's ability to do what it should do, including triggering alerts and error messages per specifications.
  • Negative Case testing — challenges the system's ability to correctly prevent actions that specifications state should be prohibited or blocked.
  • Repeatability testing — challenges the system's ability to repeatedly do what it should.
  • Performance testing — challenges the system's ability to perform as fast and effectively as required by specifications.
  • Volume/Load testing — challenges the system's ability to manage high loads. Typically automated. Required when system resources are critical.
  • Structural/Path testing — challenges a program's internal structure by exercising detailed program code.
  • Smoke testing — superficial testing to check critical functionality as a measure of system build stability.
  • Regression testing — challenges the system's ability to still do what it should after being modified; verifies that portions not involved in the change were not adversely affected.

D5.6.3 Contractual/Acceptance Testing: FAT and SAT

Acceptance tests are a predefined set of functional tests that demonstrate fitness for intended use. Acceptance may be carried out in two stages:

  • Factory Acceptance Tests (FAT) — performed at the supplier site before delivery to show that the system is working well enough to be installed and tested on-site.
  • Site Acceptance Tests (SAT) — show that the system is working in its operational environment and that it interfaces correctly with other systems and peripherals.

These acceptance tests may be leveraged in support of, but do not replace the need for, process qualification including Process Performance Qualification (PPQ) where relevant.

中文解說：測試類型詳解

黑盒 vs 白盒測試 — 誰來做？

黑盒測試 (Black Box) 白盒測試 (White Box)
執行者 業務 SME、QA、使用者 開發工程師、測試工程師
關注點 輸入/輸出是否符合規格 代碼路徑、邏輯分支
GAMP 角色 受規管公司 OQ/PQ 主要方式 供應商開發測試的主要方式

迴歸測試 (Regression Testing) — 軟體更新後最關鍵的測試

當 LIMS 供應商發布 v4.1 → v4.2 更新時，需要判斷哪些測試必須重跑：

  • 受影響的功能模組：根據供應商提供的 Release Notes 和變更清單，識別哪些功能被修改
  • 相依功能：修改了樣品接收模組，可能影響樣品狀態追蹤、報告模組
  • 核心 GxP 功能：電子簽名、稽核追蹤、批次放行 — 無論更新內容是否涉及，都建議納入迴歸測試
  • 不需重跑的測試：完全未受影響的功能，有書面風險評估支持

FAT/SAT vs IQ/OQ/PQ — 關係釐清

在自動化設備（如無菌灌裝線控制系統）的驗證中：

  • FAT：在供應商工廠確認系統基本功能（接近 IQ + 部分 OQ）
  • SAT：在現場確認系統在實際環境中運作（接近 OQ + 部分 PQ）
  • FAT/SAT 可以被利用 (leveraged) 作為 IQ/OQ 的證據，減少重複測試
  • 但 FAT/SAT 不能取代 PQ（製程性能確認需要在實際生產條件下進行）

負面案例測試 (Negative Case Testing) 常被忽略

許多驗證方案只測試「系統會做什麼」，卻忘記測試「系統是否正確拒絕不該做的事」。

LIMS 負面測試例子：

  • 在檢驗未完成時，系統是否拒絕批次放行？
  • 當輸入超出規格的數值時，系統是否正確觸發 OOS 警示？
  • 無權限用戶嘗試修改已簽名記錄時，系統是否阻止？

D5.7 Test Environments

Testing may take place in different environments during a project, which may include:

  • Development environment — where prototyping or programming takes place
  • Formal testing environment — dedicated environment for structured validation testing
  • Operational environment — the target production environment

The use of multiple environments provides the opportunity to:

  • Assess changes before they are rolled out to production
  • Provide a target for restore testing of backup data
  • Reduce risk to the live operational environment and data

The DevOps environment used in Agile approaches may be replicated into multiple test environments on demand. The test environments, whether on-premise or hosted by the SaaS provider, need to be functionally equivalent for the testing to be representative and effective. Differences should be assessed and mitigated.

It is essential that a record is kept of the environment in which a test case was run, and the current build and configuration of that environment. This record may reside in an automated tool (e.g., continuous integration orchestration).

There is no benefit to repeating testing already performed in another, but still adequately controlled environment just because it was not the formal test environment.

It is the scope, rigor, and coverage of the testing that ensures the quality of the system as implemented. Any significant differences between the environments used for testing should be assessed to determine the equivalency of test results.

中文解說：測試環境管理

為何需要獨立的測試環境？

在生產環境 (Production) 中直接進行測試是 GxP 的重大風險：

  • 測試數據可能污染真實的 GxP 記錄
  • 測試步驟可能意外修改已驗證的配置
  • 測試失敗可能導致生產中斷
  • 難以維持「已驗證狀態」的完整性

三層環境架構的最佳實踐

環境 用途 GxP 控制程度
開發 (DEV) 代碼開發、單元測試 低 — 允許快速實驗
測試/UAT (TEST) 功能測試、整合測試、用戶驗收測試 中 — 需記錄環境版本，功能等同於生產
生產 (PROD) 日常 GxP 操作 高 — 完全受變更管控保護

環境等同性 (Functional Equivalency) = 分析方法轉移

如果在實驗室 A 驗證了分析方法，要在實驗室 B 使用，需要做方法轉移確認，證明兩個實驗室的結果具有可比性。

測試環境也一樣：在 TEST 環境中完成的測試，若環境配置與 PROD 有差異，需要評估差異是否影響測試結果的有效性。若不影響（例如：審計追蹤功能的測試結果在兩個環境中相同），則無需在 PROD 中重複測試。

SaaS 環境的特殊考量

對於雲端 SaaS 系統（如某些雲端 LIMS），測試環境由供應商管理。關鍵要求：

  • 確認供應商提供的 sandbox/staging 環境與生產環境在功能上是等同的
  • 記錄每次測試時的環境版本（供應商可能隨時更新）
  • 在合約 (SLA) 中明確測試環境的維護責任

D5.8 Leveraging Previous Testing Including Supplier Testing

D5.8.1 Supplier Testing

The more extensive and effective the testing done by the supplier during their life cycle, the less testing the regulated company may need to do. If the supplier testing is confirmed as sufficient to demonstrate that the system functions correctly against supplier specifications, then the regulated company verification activity may be limited to a subset of requirements testing.

Common test types executed during a supplier development life cycle are:

  • Acceptance Testing for Purchased Hardware and Software — subject to acceptance testing before being used for the system's development
  • Unit/Module Tests — stand-alone tests for software components, ensuring readiness for further integration
  • Integration and Functional Tests — testing of integrated software components, sub-systems, and the complete system

In order to leverage supplier testing, the regulated company should first consider:

  • The extent, coverage and quality of the supplier testing
  • How supplier test records can be made available for appropriate assessment and review
  • How traceability between the regulated company's requirements and the supplier's test cases will be established

D5.8.2 Ongoing Life Cycle Maintenance

New releases of the software by the supplier will result in the need for the regulated company to actively maintain the validated state after upgrading. Critical thinking and risk management should be used to determine the extent of the effort required.

As a minimum, the regulated company will need to verify the updated software remains fit for their intended use. The supplier should provide a clear understanding of the changes being implemented. Regression testing of the configuration and workflows — whether manual or automated — may be implemented to confirm the latest software version still provides a system fit for the regulated company's intended use.

D5.8.3 Testing in Multiple Environments

Testing in environments other than the validation or production environment contributes to finding defects and confirming the system is fit for intended use. Where there is no impact to the particular test types arising from the difference in the environments, the testing should be leveraged no matter what environment it occurred in — there is no benefit to repeating that testing in the formal test or production environments.

中文解說：利用供應商測試

供應商測試的「利用」策略

GAMP 5 的核心效率原則：不重複已完成的良好測試。

能夠利用供應商測試的前提：

  1. 供應商評估已完成（Appendix M2）：確認供應商的品質體系和開發流程符合要求
  2. 供應商測試記錄可以被審查：測試計畫、測試案例、測試結果都可取得
  3. 可追溯性已建立：供應商的測試案例可以對應到受規管公司的 URS/FRS 需求

類比：信任經認可的原料供應商

經過認證的原料供應商提供的物料，不需要每批都做全項檢驗——可以依賴 CoA 並只做鑑別測試。

同樣地，已完成良好審計、測試記錄完整的軟體供應商，其測試結果可以被受規管公司部分採信，減少重複測試。

軟體更新後的迴歸測試決策

當供應商發布 patch 或新版本時，受規管公司的決策流程：

  1. 獲取 Release Notes：理解變更內容
  2. 影響評估：這些變更是否影響我們配置的 GxP 功能？
  3. 決定測試範圍：
    • 若只有安全補丁，無功能變更 → 最小測試（如 smoke test）
    • 若有功能變更 → 受影響功能的完整迴歸測試
    • 若有架構重大更改 → 重新執行全部測試
  4. 文件化決策理由：風險評估記錄

D5.9 Testing Applied to Different Software Categories

D5.9.1.2 Points to Consider for All Systems

This is an aide memoire only and does not replace the need to apply critical thinking and a risk-based approach. Test coverage may include:

  • Power failure testing — prevention against loss of critical data; ease of controlled restart
  • System access and security features
  • Data audit trails for creation, modification, and deletion of GxP records
  • Manual data entry features, input validation
  • Electronic signature features
  • Alarms and error messages
  • Critical calculations
  • Critical transactions
  • Transfer of critical data into other packages or systems
  • Interfaces and data transfers
  • Backup and restore
  • Data archival and retrieval
  • Ability to deal with high-volume loads

D5.9.2 Category 3: Standard Product Testing

Software products used off-the-shelf (not configurable, or limited parameterization). Testing should focus on:

  • Installation testing as described above
  • Requirements testing that demonstrates fitness for intended use (may include testing against requirements depending on risk)
  • For very simple measurement systems, regular calibration may substitute for testing
  • Any further or more rigorous tests as a result of risk and supplier assessments

D5.9.3 Category 4: Configured Functionality Testing

Commercially available software configured for a specific business process. Testing should focus on:

  • Installation testing
  • Configuration testing — verifying that the system has been configured in accordance with the agreed specification
  • Functional testing — challenging functionality supporting the specific business process based on risk and supplier assessments
  • Requirements testing — challenging the configuration and user-defined workflows to ensure business process needs have been met

D5.9.4 Category 5: Custom Application Testing

Custom-developed software. Testing should include Category 4 approaches, plus:

  • Code review for new code required as a result of risk assessments (see Appendix D4)
  • Software module testing — testing software modules defined in the design specification
  • Software integration testing — testing that the modules work when operating together

中文解說：各軟體類別測試策略

四個 GAMP 類別的測試策略比較

類別 典型例子 測試重點 代碼審查？
Cat 1
基礎設施		 OS、網路設備 安裝確認 + 配置確認 不適用
Cat 3
標準產品		 簡單測量儀器軟體 安裝測試 + 需求測試 否
Cat 4
配置化產品		 LIMS、MES、ERP 安裝 + 配置 + 功能 + 需求測試 否 (配置審查即可)
Cat 5
客製開發		 自行開發的計算腳本、介面程式 Cat 4 全部 + 代碼審查 + 模組測試 + 整合測試 是 (必要)

重要的「全系統通用」測試清單

不論 Category 為何，D5.9.1.2 的清單中有幾項幾乎每次都會被查核：

  • 稽核追蹤 (Audit Trail)：21 CFR Part 11 / Annex 11 核心要求
  • 電子簽名：必須測試意義聲明、不可否認性
  • 備份與還原 (Backup & Restore)：還原測試常被忽略，但後果嚴重
  • 關鍵計算：所有數值計算必須用已知數據驗證結果

LIMS 是 Category 4 的代表

大多數 LIMS（如 LabWare、Thermo LIMS、Veeva Vault QMS 的實驗室模組）屬於 Category 4：

  • IQ：確認安裝版本、資料庫設置、網路配置
  • OQ：測試所有已配置功能是否符合 FRS（功能需求規格）
  • PQ：業務使用者用真實場景執行端對端工作流程
  • 供應商的測試可用於減少 OQ 中對標準功能的重複測試

Section Summary — 章節總結：Appendices D4 & D5

Key Takeaways — English

  • D4 Software Development: GxP software must follow a defined development lifecycle with version control, code review, and release criteria. SBOM is a new best practice for tracking software components and dependencies.
  • Code Review: Source code review has three objectives — verify coding standards, verify design compliance, and identify defects. Review must be performed by an independent person. Static analysis tools can complement manual review.
  • D5 Test Strategy: Risk-based approach is mandatory. Not all functions require the same depth of testing. Critical thinking must be documented.
  • IQ/OQ/PQ in CSV: IQ verifies correct installation and configuration baseline. OQ tests all configured functions against FRS. PQ uses real-world end-to-end scenarios by business users to confirm fitness for intended use.
  • Scripted vs Unscripted: Both are valid. Scripted testing is pre-approved and provides the basis for regression testing. Unscripted testing (exploratory, day-in-the-life) improves defect detection. Unscripted does NOT mean undocumented.
  • Defect Management: Critical defects require fix before go-live. Major defects may allow conditional release with documented workarounds and QA-approved risk assessment. Minor defects can be deferred with documentation.
  • Regression Testing: After software updates, determine test scope by: supplier release notes, impact assessment on GxP functions, and risk-based decision on which tests to re-run.
  • Test Environment: A separate validated test environment is essential. It must be functionally equivalent to production. Record the environment version for every test execution. Testing in other environments (dev, supplier) can be leveraged if equivalency is assessed.

重點總結 — 中文

  • D4 軟體開發：GxP 軟體必須有定義的開發生命週期，涵蓋版本控制、代碼審查、發布標準。SBOM（軟體物料清單）是第二版新增的最佳實踐，用於追蹤軟體元件和相依關係。
  • 代碼審查：三個目標（驗證編碼標準、設計合規性、缺陷識別），必須由獨立人員執行。靜態分析工具可補充人工審查。
  • D5 測試策略：風險為基礎是必要條件。批判性思維的理由必須文件化。並非所有功能都需要相同程度的測試。
  • 電腦化系統的 IQ/OQ/PQ：IQ 確認安裝和配置基線；OQ 對照 FRS 測試所有已配置功能；PQ 由業務使用者用真實場景執行端對端測試，確認符合使用目的。
  • 腳本式 vs 非腳本式測試：腳本式測試需事前批准，是迴歸測試的基礎；探索性/Day-in-the-Life 測試提升缺陷發現率。非腳本式不等於未文件化。
  • 缺陷管理：嚴重缺陷 → 修復再放行；主要缺陷 → 有條件放行（需 QA 批准風險評估 + 暫時工作程序）；次要缺陷 → 記錄後延後修復。
  • 迴歸測試：軟體更新後，依據 Release Notes、GxP 功能影響評估、風險決策，確定需要重新執行哪些測試。
  • 測試環境管理：獨立的已驗證測試環境是必要的，必須與生產環境功能等同。每次測試都需記錄環境版本。已在其他環境完成的測試，在評估等同性後可被利用，無需重複。
6

Section 6: App D6-D11: System Descriptions, Agile, Blockchain & AI/ML

附錄D6-D11：系統說明、敏捷開發、區塊鏈與人工智慧 | p235-p280

ISPE GAMP 5 Second Edition | Appendix D6–D9 | p235–p256

Learning Objectives — 學習目標

  1. Explain the purpose and required content of a System Description under EU GMP Annex 11 and its role as a regulatory-facing document. ／解釋系統描述的目的、必要內容及其作為法規面向文件的角色。
  2. Identify the key risk categories and quality management controls required for compliant data migration in a GxP environment. ／辨識GxP環境中合規資料遷移所需的主要風險類別與品質管理控制措施。
  3. Describe the data migration plan structure, including data mapping, verification strategies, rollback planning, and reporting requirements. ／描述資料遷移計畫的架構，包括資料映射、驗證策略、回滾計畫與報告要求。
  4. Explain how Agile/Scrum methodology can be implemented in a GxP regulated environment while maintaining compliance and quality. ／說明Agile/Scrum方法論如何在GxP法規環境中實施，同時維持合規與品質。
  5. Apply the Agile quality concepts (Definition of Done, sprint testing, DevOps/CI/CD) within a CDMO computer validation context. ／在CDMO電腦驗證情境中應用Agile品質概念。
  6. Determine the appropriate level of control for software tools (GAMP Category 1) versus GxP-regulated business applications, and apply risk-based management accordingly. ／判斷軟體工具（GAMP第1類）與GxP法規業務應用程式的適當控制等級，並據此應用風險基礎管理。

Appendix D6 — System Descriptions / 系統描述

D6: System Descriptions

26.1 Introduction

This appendix provides guidance on the contents of System Descriptions. EU GMP Annex 11 requires that there is an up-to-date description of critical GxP regulated computerized systems:

"For critical systems an up to date system description detailing the physical and logical arrangements, data flows and interfaces with other systems or processes, any hardware and software pre-requisites, and security measures should be available."

The need for a system description may be covered by one or more existing specifications or other documents, or a separate document may be produced. The principal use of such a document is to help new users and regulators understand what the system does, and as such is written in non-technical language as far as possible.

26.2 Scope

This appendix covers information that may be required for a wide range of GxP computerized systems. Not all the information will be required or relevant for all systems. The level and detail of information should be based on system risk, complexity, and novelty.

26.3 Guidance

26.3.1 General Guidelines

The system description should be maintained up-to-date throughout the life cycle of the system. For complex systems spanning multiple departments or sites (e.g., ERP systems), a separate document may be appropriate. For simpler systems it is common practice to include the system description in another specification or other document.

The development of the system description may begin early in the life cycle and evolve iteratively as the development process progresses. A complete system description meeting regulatory expectations should be established before the system is released for operational use.

The system description should be subject to change control and periodic review.

26.3.2 Contents of the Document

Listed below are topics that may be required in the system description depending on the nature and type of system. The guidance is neither prescriptive nor exhaustive. The system description should cover only the main features — detailed information on specific topics should be included in other specifications and not repeated.

26.3.2.1 Introduction

This should explain the context of the system within the business process and regulated company in general, considered from the following perspectives as appropriate:

  • Departmental
  • Site-wide
  • Division-wide
  • Global

26.3.2.2 Main System Functionality

A description of the key functions of the system, both GxP and non-GxP. The functions may be grouped to maintain the description at a high level. The use of diagrams is encouraged to explain relationships between key functions.

26.3.2.3 Regulatory Impact

This should include a description of the key GxP functions of the system. The impact that the system has upon patient safety, product quality, and data integrity should be considered. Other regulatory requirements should also be covered as appropriate.

26.3.2.4 The Computing Environment

This may be covered by a high-level diagram of the architecture supporting the system, covering as appropriate:

  • The infrastructure that supports the system (e.g., server configurations, storage arrangements)
  • Interfaces to users
  • Interfaces to equipment
  • Interfaces to other systems
  • Interfaces outside the company
  • The flow of data through the interface
  • Security features such as firewalls

26.3.2.5 System Components

An indication of the main hardware and software components should be provided. This may include servers and storage devices, operating systems, databases, and application layers, plus references to configuration documentation. A detailed inventory of all components is not required here.

26.3.2.6 System Interfaces

An overview of the key interfaces to other systems and equipment, and the data flowing to or from the system.

26.3.2.7 Access Control

An overview of the access control features of the system, both physical (if relevant) and logical.

26.3.2.8 Security Controls

An overview of the established system security controls both physical and logical, including software for the protection of data and records (e.g., virus protection software).

26.3.2.9 Electronic Records and Signatures

An indication of the types of electronic records created and managed by the system, and the type of electronic signatures used, should be provided if relevant.

26.3.2.10 Glossary

Definitions of any terms that may be unfamiliar to the readership should be provided.

D6 中文解析：系統描述

比喻：系統描述是GxP系統的「護照」

就像護照一樣，系統描述必須在系統「出關」（上線投入GxP使用）之前就備齊。它用非技術語言說明這個系統是誰、做什麼、跟誰連線、誰能進入。

法規查核官員（稽核員）第一眼看的往往就是這份文件——他們想快速理解這個系統的「邊界在哪裡」、「管到哪些資料」。護照沒更新，就是問題所在。

EU GMP Annex 11 的明確要求

Annex 11 明文規定「關鍵系統」必須有up-to-date的系統描述，涵蓋：

  • 實體與邏輯架構（Physical & Logical arrangements）
  • 資料流與介面（Data flows & interfaces）
  • 硬體/軟體先決條件（Prerequisites）
  • 安全措施（Security measures）

這不只是「最好有」，而是法規硬性要求。很多公司在稽核時才發現系統描述已過期三年，這是常見的483觀察項來源。

CDMO實務要點：什麼時候需要獨立的系統描述？

GAMP 5說複雜系統（如ERP、MES）才需要獨立文件；簡單系統可以把描述放進URS或其他規格文件中。

在CDMO環境，以下系統通常需要獨立的系統描述：

  • LIMS（Laboratory Information Management System）
  • MES（Manufacturing Execution System）
  • EBR/eBatch系統
  • 跨廠區共用的ERP模組

SCADA或獨立HMI通常可以將系統描述整合進IQ/OQ文件。

系統描述 vs. 其他驗證文件

文件目的受眾
系統描述說明系統全貌（非技術語言）稽核員、新使用者、管理層
URS使用者需求規格開發者、驗證工程師
FS/DS功能/設計規格供應商、IT
IQ/OQ/PQ安裝/操作/效能確認品保、法規

系統描述是「門面文件」——它不重複其他規格的細節，但提供整合性的概覽。

稽核現場重點：邊界定義

稽核員在查電腦化系統時，最重要的問題之一是：「這個系統的邊界在哪裡？」系統描述必須清楚回答：

  • 哪些資料在系統內部管理
  • 哪些介面連到外部系統
  • 誰負責哪個部分（系統擁有者 vs 供應商）

邊界不清楚 = 責任不清楚 = 稽核風險。

Change Control + Periodic Review 的重要性

系統描述必須受到變更管制並定期審查。常見的失效模式：系統已升版（例如從v8升到v9），但系統描述還停在舊版架構。這在稽核中會被認定為「documented system不符合實際運作狀態」。

建議：每次系統重大變更（infrastructure change、interface增減）必須觸發系統描述審查。

Appendix D7 — Data Migration / 資料遷移

D7: Data Migration

27.1 Introduction

This appendix provides guidance for the migration of electronic data in the regulated environment, covering planning, execution, and reporting. Migration activities should be focused on aspects critical to patient safety, product quality, and data integrity, commensurate with risk, complexity, and novelty.

27.3 Guidance

27.3.1 General Guidelines

Data migration is the activity of transporting electronic data and associated metadata from one system to another, or the transition of data from one state to another. Data migration can occur often during and/or at the end of the life cycle of various computerized systems. Migration efforts can vary greatly in scope, complexity, and risk, including:

  • An in-place version upgrade of a database or application
  • Data conversion (e.g., from one supplier's database to another)
  • Same system – different platform migration (e.g., on-premise to cloud)
  • Migration from one source system to a different target system
  • Migration from multiple source systems to a single target system

The ultimate goal of any data migration is to have data that remains usable and retains its contextual meaning. Quality management controls should be in place to ensure data migration efforts are successful, compliant, and repeatable. Each data migration should be managed within the framework of a data migration plan and report, or through following an established data migration procedure.

27.3.2 Quality Management

27.3.2.1 System Life Cycle

Data migration may take place multiple times during the life cycle of a single computerized system, such as during initial system development and deployment, application upgrades, and system retirement. A data migration SOP may be the best method for describing and documenting the process expectations, including quality and compliance requirements. It must utilize a risk-based approach to ensure the effort is appropriately rightsized.

27.3.2.2 Risk Management

The following should be evaluated when migrating regulated data:

  • The inherent quality and compliance risk associated with the data being migrated, including impact upon patient safety, product quality, and data integrity; risk associated with the business processes; and risk associated with incomplete source data
  • Risk to the business due to systems being unavailable or data being unreliable
  • The level of complexity (e.g., multiple source or target systems; multiple phases; a high degree of data transformation)
  • Technology risk due to the use of complex or leading-edge systems or tools
  • Risks associated with the use of system vendors and third-party contractors

27.3.2.3 Configuration Management and Change Control

Migration of electronic data in the regulated environment should be performed under change control. All appropriate data migration project documents and tools should be controlled using configuration management and good documentation practices, including ALCOA+ principles.

During a data migration project, system changes unrelated to the migration should be prohibited, as unrelated system changes can increase complexity and overall project risk.

Typical good practice is to use one or more intermediate staging areas for data extracted from source systems prior to being loaded into the target system. At least three system platforms should remain under configuration management during the entire project: the source system(s), the staging area, and the target system. A rollback strategy should be established, including a full source-system backup prior to any migration activities.

27.3.3 Areas of Concern

27.3.3.1 Fitness of Software Tools for Intended Use

Data migration efforts typically involve software tools to automate extraction, transformation, loading, and verification activities. These tend to be GAMP software Category 1 infrastructure tools or Category 5 custom applications. The infrastructure tools and custom applications should be fit for intended use. For software tools that move or transform data, there are three principal areas of risk:

  • Data will be moved or transformed incorrectly or incompletely (incorrect data format, accuracy and/or completeness of the information, loss of information, orphan records)
  • Data residing in the target system will be harmed (deletion and/or overwriting of data, breaking and/or modification of data links, loss of metadata)
  • In cases where not all data is being migrated, residual data in the source system is adversely affected by the removal of the migrated data

Through the use of data verification, these risks can be significantly mitigated and therefore the rigor of software migration tool verification can be reduced. Development and approval of a data mapping table is still necessary.

27.3.3.2 Data Verification

Data should be verified each time it is moved or its state is transformed. There are two general types of post-migration data verification:

  • Test environment verification: A target test system is initially populated with data, then a migration test run is performed, and finally data is verified to show that all required data migrated successfully. A typical approach is to work with a relatively small amount of data, which can then be completely verified.
  • Operational environment verification: The same intent but the amount of data is typically very large. Automated software tools can be used to verify 100% of data in the target environment.

An important part is confirming that all of the required data has been migrated. Verification techniques such as checksum can be used to corroborate complete data transmission and locate failed records. Objective evidence of data verification should be generated.

27.3.3.3 Reliability of Source Data

The reliability of the source-system data must be considered as part of the migration process. If the reliability of the source system and data are unknown, the veracity of data migrated from the source system may not be verifiable; additionally, the migrated data will mix with reliable data already in the controlled target system. If inconsistencies are possible, they should be documented with justification of why the migrated data should be trusted.

27.3.3.4 Usability of Migrated Data in Target System

Four main issues to consider:

  • Target-system functionality does not allow performance of tasks previously carried out in the source system
  • Lack of completeness of migrated data affects the usability of the data
  • Separate migration of metadata or configuration may also be required (e.g., user groups and access rights)
  • Need for multiple migrations through various versions of a system to ensure full compatibility in the final target system

27.3.3.5 Audit Trails

Audit trails can be problematic for data migration efforts. If the target system has an audit trail but the source system does not, documentation should be created reflecting that auditing for migrated records began when they were loaded onto the target system. If both the source and target systems have audit trails and it is technically feasible, the audit trail should be migrated along with the audited data. If technically unfeasible, the original audit trail should be archived in a format that can be retrieved and used for support or investigational purposes.

When possible, a computer-generated audit trail should be created during the movement and transformation activities associated with the data migration effort. If the audit trail must be turned off during migration, the rationale should be documented.

27.3.3.6 Use of System Vendors and Third-Party Contractors

System vendors and third-party vendors should be assessed/audited to ensure they are capable of performing the work and that tools utilized are validated for their intended use. Master Service Agreements (MSAs), SLAs, Statements of Work (SOW), and/or quality agreements should be established.

27.3.4 Data Migration Plan

Every data migration project should have a data migration plan as a required deliverable. The data migration plan should describe the entire migration process, including as a minimum:

  • Migration project purpose and scope
  • System description(s)
  • Roles and responsibilities
  • Required deliverables
  • Risk-management strategy
  • Configuration management strategy (source, staging, and target environments)
  • Software tool overview and strategy for ensuring compliance and fitness for intended use
  • Migration steps, technical activities, and impacted business area activities
  • Data mapping and modeling activities
  • Transformation rules
  • Data verification strategy and acceptance standards
  • Cutover plan (including communication activities)
  • Rollback strategy

The data migration plan should be approved by the process owner, system owner, quality unit, and SMEs as appropriate.

27.3.5 Data Migration Report

The data migration report summarizes the activities conducted during the data migration effort. It describes any anomalies or deviations encountered and lists the results of verification activities. Because the report will be used to establish the reliability of the migrated data, it should clearly state the overall outcome of the migration activity (e.g., full success, partial success, failure). The data migration report should be approved by the same individuals who approved the migration plan.

D7 中文解析：資料遷移

比喻：資料遷移是「搬家」，不只是「搬箱子」

很多人以為資料遷移就是把資料庫的資料複製過去。但GAMP 5提醒我們：搬家時不只要搬家具（資料），還要確保：

  • 家具到了新家還能用（可用性）
  • 鑰匙、門禁也要跟著設定好（metadata、存取權限）
  • 搬家過程有完整紀錄（稽核軌跡）
  • 搬錯了能搬回來（rollback strategy）

CDMO最常踩的坑：從紙本或舊LIMS遷移到新系統

CDMO環境中最常見的資料遷移場景是：更換LIMS（舊系統 → 新系統），或將紙本批次記錄數位化後匯入EBR系統。

這種情況特別棘手，因為：

  • 舊系統的「資料可靠性」難以確認（有沒有audit trail？）
  • 紙本資料沒有audit trail，遷移後要怎麼交代稽核軌跡的起始點
  • 資料格式不統一（例如舊系統用文字儲存數值，新系統需要數字型別）
  • 業主覺得「copy-paste就好」，低估了驗證工作量

資料映射表（Data Mapping Table）：必備交付物

即使使用自動化遷移工具，也必須建立data mapping table，說明：

來源欄位目標欄位轉換規則驗證方式
Batch_No (text)batch_number (varchar)直接對應100%比對
Test_Result (text)result_value (decimal)型別轉換抽樣+checksum
Analyst_Nameuser_id (FK)查表對應人工確認清單

這份表格要放進遷移計畫，並獲得QA批准。

三環境架構：Source → Staging → Target

GAMP 5明確建議使用staging area（暫存環境）作為中間緩衝：

  • Source system：原始資料，在整個遷移期間不得有無關的系統變更
  • Staging area：資料清理、格式轉換、規則應用的工作區
  • Target system：最終生產環境，只有驗證通過的資料才進入

三個環境都要在configuration management控制下。Rollback計畫要在遷移開始前就準備好。

驗證策略：測試環境 vs 正式環境

測試環境驗證：先用少量資料（例如100筆）在test環境跑一次完整遷移流程，並進行100%比對驗證。目的是確認工具和流程可行，取得evidence before go-live。

正式環境驗證：資料量龐大，通常需要自動化工具進行100%比對（或統計抽樣加checksum）。自動化驗證工具本身的適用性也需要評估。

Checksum驗證的原理：計算來源資料的記錄數量與特定欄位的加總值，遷移後再次計算，兩個值相符才代表沒有漏筆或資料損失。

稽核軌跡的棘手問題

如果舊系統沒有audit trail，資料遷移到有audit trail的新系統後，稽核員會問：「這些記錄在遷移之前誰改過？」

GAMP 5的建議：在遷移計畫中明確記載「遷移前的稽核軌跡不存在」，並在每筆遷移記錄中標記migration date作為audit trail的起始點。若能在遷移過程中產生computer-generated log，更佳。

CDMO資料遷移計畫的最低清單

  • 遷移範疇與系統描述
  • 風險評估（source data reliability + tool risk）
  • Data mapping table（含轉換規則）
  • 三環境架構說明（source / staging / target）
  • 驗證策略（test run + production run）
  • Cutover計畫（誰負責通知使用者、系統停機窗口）
  • Rollback計畫（何時觸發、如何恢復）
  • 遷移報告範本（成功/失敗判準）
  • QA批准（流程擁有者、系統擁有者、QA、SME）

Appendix D8 — Agile Software Development / 敏捷軟體開發

D8: Agile Software Development

28.1 Introduction

Agile software development practices are widely adopted by many industries, including medical devices. Agile approaches focus on delivering quality and value to the customer at speed, and in an incremental fashion, enabling technical innovation and flexibility.

FDA's Technology Modernization Action Plan (TMAP) identified Agile software development and DevOps as foundational requirements for a modern FDA technology infrastructure. Such approaches are very well suited to the development of GxP regulated systems if correctly applied by trained and qualified practitioners supported by appropriate tools.

This appendix provides a summary of the principles underpinning Agile and illustrates how it can be implemented in a way that is aligned with GAMP 5 and GxP principles. The focus is on how to use well-implemented standard Agile processes to deliver software for GxP applications — it does not advocate modifying Agile for GxP (e.g., by superimposing linear V-model activities).

The planning, specification, verification and reporting activities within this Guide are not inherently linear, and the approach described is designed to be compatible with a wide range of models, methods, and schemes including incremental, iterative, and exploratory models.

The key principles behind Agile software development are that of discovery and of iteration (ongoing changes) as opposed to waterfall software development, where there is a linear flow of defining all requirements before transforming them into a complete set of specifications that are then configured/coded before testing commences.

Agile Manifesto Statements

"Individuals and interactions over processes and tools
Working software over comprehensive documentation
Customer collaboration over contract negotiation
Responding to change over following a plan"

These principles need to be taken in the context of emphasis rather than a binary choice.

28.2 Scope

Agile software practices can be applied across many types of computerized systems, including custom application development and configuration of configurable products in an incremental manner. Where the regulated company is looking at less clearly defined scope/requirements, Agile is likely to be the preferred approach to commence with a discovery phase to develop the initial backlog requirements and enable faster initial system deployment and subsequent incremental development.

28.3 Guidance

28.3.1 Agile Basics (Scrum Framework)

There are many different frameworks for Agile; the popular Scrum framework will be used as the reference. Agile is not a reason to accept a lower level of quality or GxP compliance. Evidence of fitness for intended use may be generated and maintained in tools and supporting systems, rather than in traditional documentation.

  • A Product Owner is responsible for collecting requirements into a product backlog, typically containing larger sets of requirements (epics) which are further split into sets of (user) Stories.
  • The Scrum cross-functional team takes a subset of the backlog items and develops/delivers and tests these during a sprint.
  • A sprint retrospective evaluates the business value of the completed sprint, and drives continuous improvement.
  • The cycle then repeats with another subset of the backlog.

Sprints are governed by time and designed to be a short period, 2 to 4 weeks. Backlog items unable to be completed during the Sprint return to the backlog.
