Regulated company quality roles typically provide oversight and subject matter expertise on regulations and potential areas of product quality, patient safety, and regulated data impact. Ultimate accountability for quality and compliance lies with the regulated company.

The concepts of a Definition of Ready (DoR), Definition of Done (DoD), and also a Minimum Viable Product (MVP) are used to determine activities to be completed before a requirement can be considered complete and to define the minimum set of features needed for initial release.

Due to the iterative nature of Agile software development, regression testing, often performed using automated test tools, is typically applied to ensure stability of the system within sprints.

28.3.2 User Requirements

With Agile, by planning and storing requirements differently and following Agile principles, teams can successfully deliver effective and useful software in a controlled way that is compliant with GxP regulations, with a clearly identifiable set of fulfilled requirements at the point the system is released into the live GxP operational environment. The delivered description of system functionality is provided by the list of completed Agile artifacts such as epics and user stories obtainable directly from the Agile software development tools.

28.3.3 Mindset and Culture

A shift in culture and behaviors is required, according to the following principles:

  • An agile-first mindset and ways of working, using a Discovery Mindset, rather than a Certainty Mindset
  • A culture of innovation and continuous improvement
  • Empowered teams with the ability to deliver across geographies
  • A consistent and repeatable way of agile delivery
  • Much-improved alignment across all stakeholders

The discovery mindset also applies to business process owners and quality groups. With the traditional approach they are involved at the beginning (requirements) and end (acceptance testing). Agile is a continuous cycle of involvement and the resourcing and planning impact of this needs to be taken into account.

28.3.4 Tools Instead of Documents

Agile is typically used with sets of tools providing control over the product backlog, configuration, testing, and release activities enabling shorter cycle times and higher quality. From a quality and GxP compliance perspective, tools perform an essential role in demonstrating that the system is fit for intended use, functionality can be traced back to requirements, and testing completed.

Tools manage a variety of Agile activities such as user-story risk assessments, testing, and traceability. A backlog with continuously changing user stories is extremely difficult to manage on paper; a tool can provide an efficient and effective means to manage user stories throughout updates and changes. Reports may be generated from tools, for instance during regulatory inspections to provide evidence of status.

Tool TypeQuality Benefit
Backlog Management SoftwareReal-time status of requirements including traceability and approval status; audit trail for changes
Testing ManagementEvidence of test status, automation and regression testing; negative and stress testing
Orchestration SoftwareAutomated assurance of working and tested code; defined workflow for code moving between environments
Code Repository SoftwareReduces configuration management issues; enables traceability from requirements to code level
Large Binary File RegistryAccurate configuration management across multiple repositories
Knowledge Management SoftwareContext repository assisting team members in locating information quickly and accurately

The tools used as part of Agile are covered within the scope of Appendix D9 and do not require computerized system validation, but should be subject to risk assessment, assessed for adequacy by appropriate SMEs, used by trained and qualified individuals, and appropriate controls applied according to intended use.

28.3.5 Approvals and Acceptance

There is a misconception that approval means sign, and by extension that there is the need to comply with the life-sciences regulatory requirements on electronic signatures (e.g., 21 CFR Part 11). This is not the case for software life cycle deliverables (except for SaMD or software embedded in a regulated medical device). Approval can be achieved by many other means such as status change, email, audit trails, and in many cases evidence of acceptance rather than an approval is sufficient.

Modern tool sets frequently have immutable change logs built into them, recording exactly who did what and when against each product backlog item, and can be configured to enforce security rights.

28.3.6 DevOps

DevOps is an extension of Agile where the development and maintenance activities are combined within a single team. In a DevOps environment, systems will undergo many changes/releases. This concern can be mitigated with the level of control and oversight of the process. However, there is still a level of risk/impact assessment required for higher-risk GxP functions undergoing change.

Continuous Integration (CI) and Continuous Deployment (CD) is an extension of DevOps where there is increased use/reliance on automated software analysis tools. DevOps provides additional controls such as:

  • No development before an accepted user story
  • Source code review and automated testing as part of the CI process
  • Ensuring close alignment and constant engagement with the product owner

28.4 Agile Approach to Quality

By following the agreed Agile process and associated ceremonies, a state of control can be demonstrated and quality built into the product. User stories can be assessed against INVEST criteria:

  • I – Independent
  • N – Negotiable
  • V – Valuable
  • E – Estimable
  • S – Small
  • T – Testable

A typical GxP regulated system has functional requirements that have GxP impact along with nonfunctional requirements (e.g., security) that need to be in place to support GxP regulations including data integrity. There must be a "potentially shippable product at the end of each sprint" — an untested product is not shippable. Agile testing uses a combination of exploratory testing and test automation with regression testing to verify that sprint developments do not impact correct functioning of software developed in previous sprints.

Agile is by its essence about tightly controlled management of change. Adherence to the defined Agile process (Scrum ceremonies such as sprint planning, daily meetings, sprint reviews, and sprint retrospectives) drives quality, ensures timelines can be adjusted quickly, and provides a focus on learning by addressing issues as they appear.

D8 中文解析：敏捷軟體開發

核心張力：Agile的速度 vs GxP的文件要求

Agile宣言說「Working software over comprehensive documentation」，但GxP說「沒有文件就等於沒發生」。這難道是根本矛盾嗎？

GAMP 5的回答是：No。關鍵在於「文件的形式可以改變」——工具裡的backlog記錄、test run的audit trail、sprint report，這些都是合法的GxP evidence。重點是可追溯性和完整性，而不是紙本或PDF的數量。

Scrum在GxP環境的角色對應

Scrum角色GxP對應責任
Product Owner業務流程擁有者 + 用戶代表，負責定義GxP功能需求
Scrum Master確保流程合規、ceremonies執行、問題升報
Development Team實際開發與測試，對sprint內交付品質負責
Quality/Compliance SME識別GxP影響，提供法規建議，不是審批瓶頸

注意：QA在Agile環境中的角色是「嵌入式夥伴」，不是最後的守門員。這需要QA思維轉型。

CDMO如何落地：Sprint文件策略

在CDMO的電腦驗證專案（例如新LIMS、MES）中採用Agile，建議的文件策略：

  • Sprint Planning：產出backlog item list（含GxP影響評估）→ 等同於傳統的功能規格片段
  • Sprint Execution：在工具中記錄user story完成狀態、test results、defect resolution
  • Sprint Review：產出sprint summary report（誰測了什麼、通過/失敗、未解決的問題）→ 等同於測試記錄
  • Sprint Retrospective：流程改善記錄 → 持續品質改善的evidence
  • Release：所有sprint的cumulative backlog + DoD verification = 驗證總結報告的基礎

Definition of Done (DoD) 與 GxP合規

DoD是Agile中最重要的品質控制機制。在GxP系統中，DoD應包含：

  • 功能已開發完成（code complete）
  • 單元測試通過（unit test pass rate > X%）
  • Regression testing通過（不影響之前sprint的功能）
  • GxP影響評估已完成（如有資料完整性影響，已記錄）
  • Defect已close或risk-accepted（附justification）
  • User acceptance已確認（業主簽核或工具狀態記錄）

一個未通過DoD的user story不能計為「完成」，也不能進入下一個sprint作為基礎。

INVEST標準：寫好User Story的關鍵

如果user story寫得不好（太大、太模糊、無法測試），整個Agile流程都會出問題。INVEST是一個自我檢查框架：

  • I (Independent)：這個story可以獨立開發，不依賴未完成的其他story
  • N (Negotiable)：細節可以討論，不是不可更改的契約
  • V (Valuable)：對使用者或業務有明確價值
  • E (Estimable)：團隊能夠估算開發工作量
  • S (Small)：一個sprint內可完成（通常1-3天開發量）
  • T (Testable)：有清楚的acceptance criteria，知道怎麼測試

電子簽名的誤解：Agile中的approval不等於21 CFR Part 11

很多GxP從業者看到Agile工具的「approve」按鈕就緊張：這需要符合21 CFR Part 11嗎？

GAMP 5明確回答：不需要（除非是SaMD或醫療器材嵌入軟體）。軟體生命週期文件（user story approval、sprint sign-off）的「批准」不等於法規上需要具法律效力的電子簽名。工具的audit trail（誰、何時、做了什麼）就足夠作為acceptance evidence。

DevOps + CI/CD 在GxP環境的適用性

DevOps將開發與維運整合到同一個團隊，CI/CD實現自動化測試和部署。這在GxP環境聽起來很可怕（「系統每天都在變？」），但實際上可行的前提是：

  • 每次change都有risk assessment（高風險GxP功能需要更嚴格的評估）
  • CI pipeline包含自動化regression testing
  • 部署需要DoD + change control gate
  • Compliance accountability在DevOps團隊內部，不是外部的人在審批

在CDMO中，這種模式適合SaaS-based系統（如cloud LIMS）的持續更新管理。

Appendix D9 — Software Tools / 軟體工具

D9: Software Tools

29.1 Introduction

This appendix describes the recommended risk-based approach and considerations when using tools supporting computerized systems life cycle processes, IT processes, and IT infrastructure processes. Such tools do not directly support GxP regulated business processes or GxP records and data directly supporting the regulated product life cycle.

The tools described in this appendix are GAMP software Category 1. Classification as GAMP software Category 3–5 applies only to business applications (either GxP or non-GxP). Tools, like systems supporting IT processes and infrastructure, are all GAMP software Category 1 and should be managed through the application of good IT practices, within a defined IT management framework such as ITIL.

Such tools and systems supporting system life cycles, IT processes, and infrastructure should not be subject to specific validation, but rather managed by routine company assessment and assurance practices and good IT practices. Compliance and regulatory resources should not be focused on audit and review of activities related to systems with little or no direct impact to patient safety or product quality.

EU GMP Annex 11 requires that automated testing tools and test environments should have documented assessments for their adequacy, supported by appropriate controls following good IT practices.

29.2 Scope

This appendix applies to software tools used as part of software development, support, and maintenance activities. It does not apply to software components/applications that are part of a GxP regulated business process, or can directly impact GxP data/records directly supporting the product life cycle; in this case risk-based computerized system validation is required.

For example: software used to migrate or convert GxP records would require computerized system validation; however, a tool used to mask or obfuscate data to be used as system test data would not.

Test tools perform an important role by helping to assure thorough testing. Such tools also often store the associated test results, but even though these records may support the computerized system life cycle, the test tools themselves do not require validation. The records they maintain should be preserved and protected, and the tools need to work reliably — this can be achieved through a basic risk assessment and application of normal IT practices.

29.3 Guidance

29.3.1 Selection of Tools

Some basic assessments should be performed as part of tool selection. The key criteria are whether the tool is the appropriate tool to support the life cycle process we are trying to automate/support: does it meet the need of the SMEs who are going to use the tool, and is it fit for purpose? It is not envisaged that any tool would need to have anything other than a desktop assessment, unless the use was considered business critical.

29.3.2 Risk Assessment

Some of the factors to consider as part of risk assessment are:

  • Is the tool an industry standard one in common use?
  • What data/records are generated/stored by the tool, and does the tool have adequate controls to maintain data integrity?
  • What is the required operational lifetime of the tool, and how will this be supported?
  • Is the tool open source; are the download locations verified to avoid cybersecurity issues?
  • Will the tool require any level of workflow/configuration, including any key activities that need to be manually performed?
  • For automated tools, how are any alerts monitored and acted upon?
  • If the tool fails, could it impact an operational computerized system or infrastructure operation?
  • Could the tool have any potential negative impact on system or network performance?
  • Could the tool introduce any cybersecurity risks, e.g., facilitate the introduction of malware?

29.3.3 Inventory/Deployment

As part of good practice, it is sensible to have some form of inventory, for example within a Configuration Management Database (CMDB), of what tools are used by the organization, where they are deployed, and the nature of any data/records potentially supporting GxP and required retention period. Identifying a single point of contact/owner for the tools is also recommended.

29.3.4 Installation and Configuration

Tools, even when off-the-shelf, often will require some degree of configuration or parameterization in order to correctly install and establish any workflows and associated aspects such as naming conventions or access levels. These are basic good software engineering practices that need to be applied along with version and appropriate change control.

29.3.5 Life Cycle Management

Tools typically have a defined lifetime, upgrades, and eventually are retired and/or decommissioned. One person or role should be designated to be the owner of the tool to provide the required level of oversight. In general, tools that have the ability to impact system or network performance require more oversight than those used as part of software development activities. It is best practice to ensure tools in use are at versions supported by the supplier.

29.3.6 Security Considerations

Cybersecurity considerations should be included for tools. Tools that are deployed across the network (e.g., for performance monitoring) may require more detailed security analysis. Security considerations should be included as part of the initial risk assessment and also as part of the life cycle management (e.g., ensuring tools are maintained as patched and up-to-date). Access privileges for tools should be set as low as possible to allow the tool to perform the task.

29.3.7 Data and Records

Where tools are storing information/records that support the validated status of the system (e.g., system requirements, design, code, or test results), controls for maintaining integrity, security, and availability should be determined and applied. Note that increasingly tools and the records/data within them may be cloud-based, and therefore assuring data integrity and access throughout the retention period should take account of this.

The full set of data integrity controls that would be applied to primary GxP records are not required, as these tools do not maintain GxP regulated records. Most tools do support technical and transactional logging supporting integrity and investigations.

29.3.8 Approvals

For tools within the scope of this appendix, any approvals or acceptances associated with the tool are not subject to regulated electronic signature requirements. Where an approval or acceptance is required, there needs to be traceability to the person approving or accepting, and approval roles need to be defined.

29.3.9 Tools over Documentation

There may be a temptation, particularly where tools store test execution records, to export information into controlled GxP documentation when there is no quality benefit in doing so. This approach is not recommended — it is inefficient and there is the risk that documentation becomes out of step with the information/records within the tools. Tools should have sufficient controls to preserve the data/records.

There is the potential for regulatory inspections to request access to information in tools (e.g., system requirements, test results). Process owners need to be aware of what information relating to their computerized system life cycle activities is managed within tools. It may be possible to pre-configure reports to extract test results relating to areas of GxP functionality.

Tools and systems supporting life cycles, IT processes, and infrastructure (rather than directly supporting product life cycle processes) are not themselves GxP regulated systems and should not be subject to specific validation, but managed by routine company assessment and assurance practices and good IT practices.

D9 中文解析：軟體工具

關鍵問題：Excel macro需要驗證嗎？

這是CDMO環境中最常遇到的問題之一。答案取決於Excel的用途：

  • 用Excel執行GxP計算（例如OOS計算、環境監控趨勢分析）：Excel本身是工具（Category 1），但這個特定的macro/workbook是在執行GxP業務流程 → 需要CSV（Computerized System Validation）
  • 用Excel管理驗證測試的test scripts（不含GxP記錄）：這是開發工具用途 → 不需要validation，但需要基本risk assessment + change control
  • 用Excel自動生成validation protocol的模板：生命週期工具 → Category 1，不需要validation

關鍵判斷標準：工具輸出的記錄是不是直接支援product life cycle的GxP記錄？

GAMP Category 1：工具 vs 業務應用的分野

軟體類型GAMP分類是否需要validation
LIMS（管理GxP測試記錄）Category 4/5是
MES（製造執行系統）Category 4/5是
測試管理工具（如Jira用於tracking defects）Category 1否，但需risk assessment
程式碼儲存庫（GitHub/GitLab）Category 1否，但需risk assessment
自動化測試工具（如Selenium）Category 1否，但需adequacy assessment
效能監控工具（如Datadog）Category 1否，IT good practice即可
GxP記錄用的Excel macroCategory 4/5是

EU GMP Annex 11的工具要求

Annex 11明確要求：automated testing tools和test environments必須有documented adequacy assessment。這不等於要validation，但必須有書面評估說明這個工具夠不夠好、是否適合其用途。

實務上的最低要求：

  • 工具識別與用途描述
  • Adequacy assessment（SME判斷：工具是否適合intended use）
  • 使用者訓練記錄
  • 基本access control
  • 納入CMDB（配置管理資料庫）

工具風險評估的關鍵考量

GAMP 5提供了九個風險評估考量點。在CDMO環境，最重要的是：

  • 工具儲存的記錄性質：如果工具存有test results或system requirements，這些記錄雖非GxP records，但支援validated status → 需要integrity controls
  • 雲端工具的資料保留：如果工具是SaaS（例如雲端Jira、GitHub Enterprise），須確保記錄在retention period內可取用
  • 工具失效的影響：若工具當機，是否影響已上線的GxP系統？（例如監控工具失效可能影響環境監控的警報）
  • 資安風險：開源工具的下載來源是否可信？工具是否可能引入惡意軟體？

「工具記錄不要複製進GxP文件」的重要原則

很多驗證工程師習慣把Jira/TestRail的測試結果截圖後貼進Word文件再上傳到文件管理系統。GAMP 5說：這樣做沒有品質效益，而且有風險——工具裡的記錄和文件裡的截圖可能不同步（工具裡的defect已close，但文件還沒更新）。

更好的做法：在驗證報告中引用工具的report（例如：「詳細測試結果見TestRail Report #TR-2026-042」），並確保稽核前能展示工具的原始記錄。

稽核應對：檢查官要求看工具記錄

GAMP 5提醒：法規檢查官可能要求看工具裡的記錄（例如system requirements、test results）。CDMO需要事先準備：

  • 知道哪些工具存有哪些系統的life cycle記錄
  • 能夠快速從工具中產生特定系統的GxP功能測試結果報告
  • 如果工具是第三方SaaS，確認在audit期間能取得資料存取權
  • 工具的access log能顯示誰在何時存取了哪些記錄

不要等稽核當天才發現「那個tool的管理員已離職，帳號停用了」。

工具生命週期管理：被忽視的維護義務

工具需要有designated owner（不是IT全負責，也不是驗證團隊全負責，要有明確的single point of contact）。工具的退役計畫同樣重要：

  • 工具退役前，確認其中儲存的記錄已轉移或存檔
  • 確保記錄在regulatory retention period內（通常10年以上）仍可讀取
  • 版本升級需要change control + 確認不影響既有記錄

Cloud-based工具特別要注意：vendor若停止服務，你的test records在哪裡？

Section Summary — 本節總結

Appendices D6–D9 of GAMP 5 (2nd Edition) address four practical topics that bridge the gap between theoretical GxP compliance requirements and modern software engineering practice.

  • D6 System Descriptions — A regulatory-facing document required by EU GMP Annex 11 for critical systems. It serves as the "passport" of a computerized system, describing its purpose, architecture, interfaces, access controls, and electronic records in non-technical language. Must be subject to change control and periodic review; must be complete before system goes live.
  • D7 Data Migration — One of the most underestimated validation activities. GAMP 5 requires a formal data migration plan (including data mapping, staging architecture, verification strategy, rollback plan) and report approved by QA, process owner, and SMEs. Three-environment staging (source → staging → target) under configuration management is standard good practice. Source data reliability, audit trail continuity, and tool fitness for use are key risk areas.
  • D8 Agile Software Development — Agile (Scrum-based) development is fully compatible with GxP compliance when correctly applied. Evidence of compliance lives in tools (backlog, test management, code repository) rather than traditional document stacks. Key governance mechanisms: Definition of Done, sprint testing (including regression), sprint ceremonies, and INVEST-quality user stories. DevOps/CI/CD adds further automation and control. Quality is built in throughout the process, not bolted on at the end.
  • D9 Software Tools — Development tools (backlog managers, test runners, code repositories, monitoring tools) are GAMP Category 1 and do not require computerized system validation. However, they need risk assessment, adequacy evaluation (EU GMP Annex 11 requirement), designated owners, CMDB inventory, and appropriate controls for any records they hold. The key decision point: does the tool's output constitute a primary GxP record directly supporting the product life cycle? If yes → validation required. If no → risk-based IT good practice suffices.

核心思維：GxP合規不在於文件數量，而在於可追溯性、完整性、以及整個生命週期中維持受控狀態（state of control）。Agile和現代工具鏈恰恰能夠以更有效率的方式實現這些目標——前提是要有正確的mindset和適當的治理機制。

ISPE GAMP 5 Second Edition | Appendix D10 (p257–p268) & Appendix D11 (p269–p279)

Learning Objectives  |  學習目標

  1. Understand what blockchain (distributed ledger) technology is, its core properties, and why it is relevant to GxP pharmaceutical systems — including smart contracts, immutability, and access governance.
  2. Identify key pharma applications for blockchain: supply chain serialization (DSCSA), batch record integrity, material traceability, and cross-enterprise data sharing — and apply a risk-based validation approach for blockchain deployments.
  3. Distinguish between static and dynamic (continuously learning) AI/ML sub-systems, and articulate why each requires a different validation and change-management strategy in a regulated environment.
  4. Describe the AI/ML life cycle (Concept → Project → Operation) as defined in GAMP 5 and explain the critical role of data governance, dataset partitioning, and bias management in model development.
  5. Explain model drift and performance degradation, and describe the monitoring, trending, and periodic-review controls needed to maintain a validated AI/ML system in ongoing operation.
  6. Recognize the current regulatory landscape for AI/ML (FDA Good Machine Learning Practice guiding principles) and articulate the "human in the loop" requirement for GxP-critical decisions in pharma manufacturing.
Appendix D10 — Distributed Ledger Systems (Blockchain)  |  分散式帳本系統（區塊鏈）

30.1 What Is Blockchain? Core Technology Concepts

A distributed ledger (blockchain) is a shared, cryptographically secured record of transactions maintained simultaneously across many independent nodes. Each new block of records is cryptographically linked to the preceding block, creating a chain that is practically immutable: altering any historical record would require re-computing every subsequent block across the majority of the network.

The core properties that make blockchain relevant to GxP applications are:

  • Immutability: Once a transaction is written and confirmed, it cannot be changed without network-wide consensus — making fraudulent modification computationally improbable.
  • Attributability: Every transaction is signed by a cryptographic key (blockchain address/wallet), providing a clear record of who performed which action.
  • Transparency: All participants with access can audit the full transaction history.
  • Decentralization: When a network is sufficiently decentralized there are enough independent node operators to make it improbable that any single entity holds undue influence over the core protocol.

The Blockchain Technology Stack

A typical blockchain deployment in pharma involves multiple layers:

  • Layer 1 (Core Protocol): The underlying blockchain network (e.g., Ethereum, Hyperledger Fabric). Changes require majority node consensus.
  • Layer 2 / Off-chain systems: Ancillary systems (ERP, MES, LIMS) that feed data to the blockchain via APIs. GxP controls must be applied to these as well as the blockchain itself.
  • Smart Contracts: Self-executing code deployed on-chain that automates actions when defined conditions are met — analogous to PLC logic trees in manufacturing.
  • Off-chain data storage: Most data is stored off-chain (for cost and privacy); the on-chain record typically holds a cryptographic hash that links to and validates the off-chain data.

Governance of Public Networks

Core protocol updates require coordination of the majority of network operators. When a significant update is not universally adopted, the network may "fork" into two separate chains. Organizations must track these changes and assess the GxP impact of updating — or choosing not to update — their connected systems.

There is no preventive mechanism to stop an entity from posting inaccurate data. However, because blockchains are ecosystem-level systems, sustained falsification would require collusion across many independent parties — making it inherently more secure than a single centralized repository.

解說：什麼是區塊鏈？為何製藥業要關注？

一個簡單的比喻

把區塊鏈想像成一本由數百人同時持有的「共用分類帳」。每一筆交易都被寫入所有人的帳本，並且蓋上加密印章。要竄改其中一筆記錄，你必須同時修改全部持有者的帳本，這在計算上幾乎不可能。這就是「不可篡改性（Immutability）」的核心。

製藥供應鏈的實際意義：DSCSA 合規

美國 藥品供應鏈安全法（DSCSA, Drug Supply Chain Security Act） 要求製藥商對每一個銷售單元進行序列化追蹤。傳統做法是各自維護自己的資料庫，驗證時需要跨系統比對。

區塊鏈解決方案的優勢：整個供應鏈（製造商 → 批發商 → 藥局）共用同一個不可竄改的記錄，任何一方都可以即時驗證藥品真偽，無需信任單一中央機構。

Smart Contract（智能合約）在製藥中的應用

智能合約是部署在區塊鏈上的自動化程式碼，當預設條件觸發時自動執行。例如：

  • 當 GS1 序列號成功驗證後，自動發出放行記錄
  • 當監管機構發出召回訊號，自動標記相關批次庫存
  • 當原料到達指定溫度記錄超標，自動阻止該批次進入下一步

GAMP 5 要求：智能合約的程式邏輯必須納入整體系統的 SDLC，進行代碼審查（code review）與測試，就如同任何 GxP 關鍵軟體一樣。

GxP 重點提醒：區塊鏈不等於審計追蹤

常見誤解：區塊鏈的「不可篡改性」是否意味著它可以自動取代傳統的 GxP 審計追蹤（Audit Trail）？

答案：不完全是。區塊鏈確保「一旦寫入的記錄不被修改」，但它無法保證「一開始寫入的資料就是正確的」。如果一個操作員登入後輸入了錯誤數據，這個錯誤數據會被永久且不可撤銷地記錄下來。

因此，輸入控制（Input Controls）、人員認證、來源系統的資料品質仍然是驗證的核心。監管機構對於「區塊鏈紀錄是否符合 21 CFR Part 11 或 EU Annex 11」的立場目前仍在演進中。

30.2 Pharmaceutical Applications of Blockchain

Supply Chain Serialization and Traceability

Blockchain's most mature pharma application is cross-enterprise product traceability. A serialized medicine can be represented as a token on-chain with an associated hash of its data attributes (GTIN, lot number, expiry, serial number). Any supply chain participant can verify the token's integrity by re-hashing the off-chain metadata and comparing the result.

Illustrative Token Example (from GAMP 5)

Serialized product attributes:
  GTIN (01): 00855245005019
  EXP  (17): 112023
  LOT  (10): XYZ123
  S/N  (21): 447018182632

On-chain token ID (random, privacy-preserving):
  0x778gha0ca303305a92d8d028704d65e4942b7ccc9a999164cf

tokenURI hash (SHA-256 multihash):
  1220D5CC15B22D5606BF3DC255979552A4214E29054CD2E60A1446FE570F53F18C6B

Verification: Re-hash source attributes → compare to on-chain hash → if equal, data integrity confirmed.

Batch Record Integrity and Data Management

Blockchains are generally not the source of origin for manufacturing data (that remains in MES, LIMS, ERP). Rather, the blockchain serves as the source of truth — an immutable index that links records, timestamps, and transaction evidence across multiple enterprise systems.

Data-quality controls must be in place to keep blockchain records in sync with source systems. If off-chain data is corrected for a legitimate reason (error correction, lab OOS investigation), the on-chain hash reference may become invalid and must be updated accordingly.

GxP Controls Required for Blockchain Systems

Four control categories must be addressed in any blockchain GxP validation:

  • Input Controls: Integrity of data posted to the blockchain; events that trigger transactions; API transformation integrity
  • Output Controls: Accuracy of data extracted from the blockchain; completeness of queries; detectability of skipped transactions
  • Processing Controls: API monitoring; change control for protocol updates; failed transaction monitoring; network stability
  • Access Controls: Who controls which blockchain addresses; authentication before posting; private key custody; smart contract permission management

解說：製藥區塊鏈應用與 GxP 控制

為什麼要用哈希（Hash）？

哈希是一種「數位指紋」算法：相同的資料永遠產生相同的哈希值，但只要資料改變一個字母，哈希值就會完全不同。

在製藥應用中，當你把批次記錄的哈希值寫入區塊鏈，日後你可以重新計算文件的哈希值並與鏈上記錄比對——如果相符，就證明文件自寫入以來從未被修改。這是一種非常有力的數據完整性（Data Integrity）驗證機制。

CDMO 實際場景：原料可追溯性

作為 CDMO，我們同時接受多個客戶委託，每批原料都有自己的 CoA、供應商記錄、檢驗結果。傳統做法是紙本或各自的 ERP 記錄，客戶審計時要調閱大量文件。

區塊鏈解決方案：為每批關鍵原料建立鏈上記錄，含哈希化的 CoA、放行狀態、入庫時間戳。客戶可通過 API 即時查驗，不需要進廠審計——這對 EU GMP Annex 11 下的遠程審計尤其有價值。

四大控制類別的現實意義

輸入控制：最薄弱的環節。區塊鏈只能保護「已寫入的資料」，無法保護「寫入行為本身」。系統設計必須確保觸發寫入的來源系統（MES、LIMS）本身就是受控的。

輸出控制：查詢結果的完整性同樣重要。必須能夠偵測是否有交易記錄被跳過或遺漏——建立可重複執行的查詢機制是關鍵。

存取控制：區塊鏈地址（錢包）就是身份識別。私鑰（Private Key）的保管等同於電子簽章憑證的保管，必須有正式的金鑰管理程序（Key Management Procedure）。

Blockchain-as-a-Service（BaaS）的供應商評估

許多製藥公司不會自行維運區塊鏈節點，而是使用 Microsoft Azure、AWS、Oracle 等的 BaaS 服務。GAMP 5 要求依照 Appendix M2 進行供應商評估，並額外確認：

  • 節點的新增/移除流程是否受控？
  • BaaS 供應商是否同時提供鏈下存儲？其資料控制是否符合 ALCOA+？
  • 私鑰的所有權與保管責任如何界定？

30.3 Validation Life Cycle for Blockchain Systems

30.3.1 Concept Phase

Blockchains are ecosystem-level networks. From the start, external stakeholders must be involved. Business-process mapping during the concept phase should document:

  • The intended use of the blockchain solution and which use cases are GxP
  • Ancillary systems (ERP, MES, LIMS) that push and pull data to/from the blockchain
  • High-level risks to patient safety, product quality, and data integrity
  • Business logic within smart contracts (if applicable)
  • Data being managed across the network: on-chain, off-chain, metadata
  • Type of blockchain protocol and associated special considerations

Creating a swim-lane diagram across all integrated systems helps identify high-risk integration points and interface dependencies — particularly where APIs or smart contracts connect the blockchain to regulated systems.

30.3.2 Project Phase — Data and Process-Driven Approach

The blockchain is likely to serve as a backbone connecting multiple data sources and, in many cases, becoming the source of truth. However, the blockchain is generally not the source of origin for new data other than identifiers and timestamps.

Key project phase steps include:

  1. Map data from source of origin, source of truth, and ownership perspectives
  2. Identify the resulting controls (Input / Output / Processing / Access)
  3. Perform risk assessment of business-process logic and data flows
  4. Plan change management for the full GxP use case

30.3.2.5 Change Management

Change management must cover the entirety of the GxP use case. For public networks, core protocol changes are managed by the open-source community — the organization must track these and assess the GxP impact. Composable smart contracts (DApps) create a network of dependencies; each component must be assessed for its upgrade governance.

30.3.3 Retirement and Migration

Most blockchains are designed for high availability in perpetuity, but networks may become stagnant. Regulatory data-retention requirements must be met even if the network is abandoned. Strategies include:

  • Maintaining a full node of the retired network until data-retention period expires
  • Anchoring the final block hash in another secure location
  • Adopting a "cryptographic agility" approach to evolve with changing security standards

Migration to a new blockchain protocol presents unique challenges: historical transactions cannot be recreated with original ordering, and wallet addresses are protocol-specific and cannot be directly mapped across chains.

解說：區塊鏈系統的驗證生命週期

游泳道圖（Swim-Lane Diagram）的價值

想像一個製藥供應鏈區塊鏈專案：涉及 MES（批次記錄）、LIMS（檢驗結果）、WMS（倉庫管理）、ERP（採購訂單），以及客戶端的 SAP 系統。

如果只是逐一驗證每個系統，很容易遺漏「系統與系統之間的 API 介面」——而這些介面恰恰是資料錯誤最容易發生的地方。游泳道圖強制你把整個生態系統畫出來，確保沒有任何介面點被忽略。

「Source of Origin」vs「Source of Truth」的區別

這個區分在 GxP 驗證中非常重要：

  • Source of Origin（來源系統）：數據首次被創建的地方，例如天平打印秤重記錄、溫度計記錄的環境數據。GxP 要求在來源系統即進行控制（ALCOA+）。
  • Source of Truth（真相來源）：被各方認可為「當前正確狀態」的系統。區塊鏈的優勢在於它可以成為跨企業的共同 Source of Truth，無需信任任何單一方。

兩者必須保持同步——若 LIMS 中的 OOS 結果更新後，對應的鏈上哈希也需要更新。

退役（Retirement）的監管挑戰

製藥行業的記錄保存要求往往長達 10–30 年（取決於產品類型）。區塊鏈的記錄保存面臨特殊挑戰：

  • 加密算法可能在未來被破解（量子計算的威脅）——「加密敏捷性（Cryptographic Agility）」是指在設計時就保留切換算法的能力
  • 如果網絡停止運作，必須有方案確保記錄仍然可訪問和可驗證
  • 實際上，製藥區塊鏈的長期數據保存案例仍然不夠充足，GAMP 5 承認這是一個待解決的問題

公共區塊鏈的加密貨幣風險

使用以太坊等公共網絡時，每筆交易都需要支付「Gas 費用」（以加密貨幣計價）。這對 GxP 系統帶來獨特風險：

  • 若交易費用賬戶餘額不足，GxP 記錄可能無法被寫入
  • 加密貨幣的價值波動可能帶來財務和會計合規問題
  • Layer 2 解決方案可降低費用，但引入額外的技術複雜性，需獨立評估

這也是許多製藥公司傾向使用私有鏈（Hyperledger Fabric、Corda）的原因——沒有交易費用，同時具備更強的隱私控制。

30.4 Emerging Technology Considerations & Regulatory Status

30.4.1 Maturity Evaluation Criteria

When selecting a blockchain platform for GxP use, organizations should assess technology maturity across three dimensions:

Dimension Key Questions
Network Maturity Size of developer community? Length of operation? Number of prior forks?
Vendor Support Commercial support model available? Technology vendor landscape? Vendor QMS in place?
Pace of Change Mature change-governance process? Architectural changes well documented to users?

30.4.2 Cryptography as a Foundation of Trust

Blockchain security relies on two cryptographic principles:

  • Hash functions: Easy to compute forward, computationally intensive to reverse — linking blocks and providing data integrity verification
  • Asymmetric encryption: Private key creates signatures; public key verifies them — enabling attribution without revealing the private key
"From this perspective the validation strategy for the source system may be focused more on data quality than data integrity. While an in-depth understanding of the mathematics and cryptography may not be required, organizations should check that generally accepted or well-known algorithms are used."
— ISPE GAMP 5 Second Edition, Appendix D10, §30.4.2

30.4.3–30.4.4 Cryptocurrencies and Privacy

Public networks require transaction fees paid in cryptocurrency — creating financial and operational risks (account balance depletion, value volatility). Organizations should evaluate Layer-2 solutions carefully, as they inherit but do not fully replicate Layer-1 security.

Privacy on public blockchains remains a significant challenge: by design, all transactions are visible to network participants. Zero-knowledge proofs, optimistic roll-ups, and other privacy-preserving technologies are evolving rapidly but carry their own maturity and assessment requirements.

Current Regulatory Guidance Gap

Standards for GxP blockchain systems are still emerging, largely driven by industry practice rather than regulatory mandate at the time of publication. The regulatory position on whether blockchain records satisfy the requirements of 21 CFR Part 11 (FDA) or EU Annex 11 remains under active discussion. Organizations are advised to apply conservative, risk-based validation approaches while engaging with ISPE GAMP Communities of Practice for evolving guidance.

解說：技術成熟度評估與監管現狀

為什麼「成熟度評估」對 GxP 系統特別重要？

一般 IT 系統如果使用了不成熟的技術，最壞結果是系統崩潰、重新部署。但在 GxP 環境中，使用不成熟的區塊鏈平台的後果可能是：

  • 批次放行記錄無法被稽查機構接受
  • FDA 483 觀察事項或警告信
  • 批次記錄完整性受質疑，導致產品召回

因此，選平台的邏輯與選擇 MES 或 LIMS 供應商類似——要看 QMS、看用戶社群、看更新歷史。

「驗證焦點轉向資料品質」的含義

傳統 GxP 驗證的一大重點是「資料完整性（Data Integrity）」——確保記錄不被竄改。

區塊鏈的不可篡改性從底層技術上解決了這個問題，因此驗證重心可以轉移到「資料品質（Data Quality）」——確保一開始寫入的資料就是準確、完整、及時的。這是一個思維上的重要轉變。

實際應用：驗證測試可以減少對「修改偵測」的測試，增加對「來源系統準確性」和「介面傳輸完整性」的測試。

監管空白現狀（截至 GAMP 5 第二版出版）

目前沒有任何主要監管機構（FDA、EMA、PMDA）發布專門針對 GxP 區塊鏈系統的指南。

現行做法：

  • FDA 21 CFR Part 11 / EU Annex 11 仍是基準——但這些法規均寫於區塊鏈技術出現之前
  • ISPE GAMP Community of Practice 是目前最活躍的行業共識建立平台
  • 各公司採用保守的「超合規」驗證策略，同時等待監管明確

對 CDMO 的建議：在客戶合約中明確界定區塊鏈記錄的責任歸屬，並在 Quality Agreement 中規定雙方的記錄保存義務。

Appendix D11 — Artificial Intelligence and Machine Learning (AI/ML)  |  人工智慧與機器學習

31.1–31.2 Introduction and Scope

Artificial Intelligence (AI) and Machine Learning (ML) are transforming how the life sciences industry processes data and automates functions previously performed by humans. As datasets grow and computing power expands, AI becomes capable of making robust decisions in domains previously requiring expert human judgment.

This appendix applies specifically to the ML sub-system or component — typically embedded within a wider IT system or application — and provides a life cycle framework for its development, validation, and ongoing management within a GxP regulated environment. This is a new appendix in the GAMP 5 Second Edition (no equivalent in the First Edition).

The appendix addresses four themes:

  • A basic understanding of AI and static/dynamic ML sub-systems
  • A risk-based regulatory compliant AI/ML life cycle framework aligned with GAMP 5 phases
  • The importance of data integrity to AI/ML quality
  • The iterative nature of AI/ML development and its implications for validation

Types of AI/ML Models

Common model categories by function:

Model Type Function Example Pharma Application
Classification Categorize data into two or more classes Visual inspection: pass/fail for cosmetic defects
Clustering Recognize patterns by attribute for targeted action Environmental monitoring: group anomalous locations
Outlier Detection Identify anomalous data points Process monitoring: detect OOS precursors in real time
Forecasting Analyze patterns to predict future outcomes Predictive maintenance: forecast equipment failure timing

Static vs. Dynamic ML Systems

A critical GxP distinction is whether an AI/ML system is static or dynamic:

  • Static ML (offline learning): The model is trained once, frozen, and deployed. Changes require formal change management — treated similarly to traditional software changes.
  • Dynamic ML (online/continuous learning): The model continuously updates its parameters as new data arrives during operation. This creates a unique validation challenge: the model you validated at time T is no longer the same model at time T+6 months.

解說：AI/ML 的類型與 GxP 挑戰概覽

為什麼 AI/ML 的驗證比傳統軟體更難？

傳統軟體的邏輯是固定的：你給它 X，它永遠輸出 Y。驗證就是確認這個對應關係在所有條件下都正確。

AI/ML 模型的邏輯是從數據中「學習」出來的，而且某些模型（動態模型）會持續學習——意思是你今天驗證過的模型，明天可能已經不一樣了。這就是 GxP 驗證面臨的根本性挑戰。

四種模型類型的 CDMO 應用場景

  • 分類（Classification）：自動視覺檢查（AVI）系統——用於無菌充填的安瓿外觀檢查，AI 判斷是否有顆粒、破裂、填充量異常。這是目前製藥行業 AI 應用最成熟的領域之一。
  • 異常偵測（Outlier Detection）：環境監測異常偵測——在 ISO 5 潔淨室中，若 EM 數據的趨勢異常（雖未超標），AI 可以提前預警潛在污染風險。
  • 預測（Forecasting）：充填機預測性維護——分析灌裝機的震動、溫度、壓力歷史數據，預測關鍵零件（如蠕動泵、灌裝針）的更換時機，減少計畫外停機。
  • 聚類（Clustering）：製程參數分群——將歷史批次依據製程特徵分群，識別哪些批次組合對應最佳產品品質。

靜態 vs 動態：選擇的 GxP 含義

對於 GxP 關鍵決策（例如批次放行、異常判定），靜態模型通常是更可取的選擇：

  • 驗證狀態清楚：版本 1.0 經過正式驗證，變更後必須重新評估
  • 符合 FDA/EU 現有對「已驗證軟體」的預期

動態模型適用於非 GxP 關鍵的輔助分析，或有足夠強健的持續監控機制：

  • 必須定義可接受的性能參數範圍（容許限度）
  • 超出限度時必須自動觸發人工審查
  • 每次模型更新都應視為一次「受控變更」

31.3.1–31.3.2 Life Cycle: Concept Phase

The AI/ML life cycle follows the GAMP 5 framework of Concept → Project → Operation → Retirement, but with critical differences. Most importantly, data management must begin in the concept phase because data is the primary resource required for ML — unlike traditional software where data considerations can be deferred.

31.3.2 Concept Phase Activities

The concept phase must address five primary principles before any data collection begins:

  • Transparency: How will the model behave? Can its reasoning be explained?
  • Reproducibility: Can outcomes be reliably replicated under the same conditions?
  • Interpretability: What factors drive the model's outputs?
  • Applicability: How and where will the model be applied? What are the boundaries of use?
  • Liability: Who is ultimately accountable for model decisions?

31.3.2.2 Data Acquisition and Selection

Data can be acquired from internal sources (data warehouses, MES historians, LIMS) or external sources (open-source datasets, purchased datasets). Key selection considerations:

  • Source: Internal, external open-source, external purchase
  • Privacy and controls: Data classification, GDPR/PII compliance, use rights
  • Structure/format: Unstructured, semi-structured, or structured
  • Segmentation: Clustering, priority tiers, necessary vs. nice-to-have

Data must be partitioned into training, validation, and test sets during the concept phase — and this partitioning must be maintained throughout development to prevent data contamination that would compromise unbiased model evaluation.

31.3.2.3 Data Preprocessing and Classification

Data preparation includes: profiling and formatting, cleansing and transformation, anonymization (for GDPR compliance), and augmentation for diversity. The quality and integrity of data is critical — the quality of output is determined by the quality of input. Preparation must be documented and performed by data scientists with domain expertise.

"The quality and integrity of the data is critical (the quality of output is determined by the quality of input) and must be suitably classified and labeled. This is one of the most time-consuming efforts in the process."
— ISPE GAMP 5 Second Edition, Appendix D11, §31.3.2.3

解說：AI/ML 生命週期——概念階段

GIGO：垃圾進，垃圾出

這是 AI/ML 領域最重要的格言：Garbage In, Garbage Out（GIGO）。

你可以擁有世界上最先進的深度學習算法，但如果訓練數據本身有偏差或錯誤，模型輸出的結論同樣是錯誤的。更糟糕的是，模型會以高度「自信」的方式呈現這些錯誤結論。

在製藥 GxP 環境中，GIGO 的後果尤為嚴重：訓練數據如果系統性地遺漏了某種罕見的缺陷，視覺檢查 AI 就永遠不會識別這種缺陷——而整個生產團隊卻完全不知道這個盲點的存在。

五大設計原則的 GxP 意義

  • 可解釋性（Interpretability）：FDA 21 CFR Part 211 和 EU GMP 均要求能夠理解和解釋品質決策的依據。如果一個 AI 做出了拒絕批次的決定但無法解釋原因，在 GxP 環境中這是不可接受的。
  • 可重現性（Reproducibility）：對相同輸入，模型必須始終產生相同（或統計一致的）輸出。這與 GMP 的「一致性」原則直接對應。
  • 責任（Liability）：AI 做出了錯誤決定，誰負責？在 GxP 環境中，答案必須是明確的人——AI 是輔助工具，最終責任歸屬於被授權的人員。

數據集分割（Dataset Partitioning）的關鍵

為什麼要把數據分成三份（訓練、驗證、測試）？

  • 訓練集（Training Set）：模型從這部分數據中學習規律。可以多次使用。
  • 驗證集（Validation Set）：用於在訓練過程中調整超參數，評估模型是否過度擬合訓練數據。
  • 測試集（Test Set）：完全隔離，只在最後一次用於最終性能確認（相當於 UAT）。絕對不能用於任何訓練或調參活動。

如果測試集數據「洩漏」到訓練過程，模型會表現出虛假的高準確率——而在真實生產環境中表現糟糕。這是 AI 驗證中最常見的陷阱之一。

CDMO 數據挑戰：數據孤島問題

大多數製藥 CDMO 的歷史數據存在孤島問題：MES 的批次記錄、LIMS 的檢驗數據、設備 PLC 的製程數據、QA 系統的偏差記錄——各自存在不同系統，格式不一，難以整合。

在啟動 AI/ML 項目之前，必須先評估數據整合的可行性和成本，否則概念階段的假設在項目階段將面臨嚴重挑戰。

31.3.3 Life Cycle: Project Phase — Model Development

The project phase follows an iterative and incremental approach — not the linear waterfall model familiar from traditional computerized system validation. Each iteration cycles through: model design/selection → engineering → training → evaluation → hyperparameter tuning.

31.3.3.1 Model Requirements and Specifications

Initial requirements define the functionality and performance expectations of the ML sub-system. Performance metrics are a key component — they serve as the technical specifications for model acceptability and drive the iterative training-evaluation cycle. Nonfunctional requirements (deployment constraints, integration, security) must also be defined early to inform algorithm selection.

31.3.3.2 Model Design and Selection

A ML model is selected based on the question it is expected to answer. For a new system, it is unlikely that the algorithm choice is clear-cut from the start. Candidate algorithms should be evaluated against operational, performance, and regulatory requirements through a structured prototyping process.

31.3.3.3–31.3.3.4 Model Engineering and Training

Model engineering involves constructing architectures and surrounding infrastructure for training and hyperparameter tuning. During training:

  • The training dataset is supplied to the model; output is compared to ground truth to measure performance and update model parameters
  • The validation dataset evaluates training quality and assists in fine-tuning — it does NOT act as the final acceptance test
  • Hyperparameter optimization can be manual or automated (e.g., Bayesian optimization), but data scientists should not take a completely hands-off approach
  • Bias due to non-representative training data is a significant risk and must be actively managed

31.3.3.5 Model Evaluation and Testing

The best-performing models from training iterations are evaluated using performance scorecards. Visual qualitative evaluation of validation results — not just quantitative metrics — often yields better insights into failure modes. When target performance is achieved, models are selected as candidates for deployment.

31.3.3.6 Integration and Deployment

The ML sub-system is migrated from development code (optimized for fast prototyping) to deployment code (optimized for production maintenance). Key architectural principle: modularization — the inference module (forward pass from input to output) is isolated from training, evaluation, and parameter-update code.

31.3.3.7 Verification, Acceptance, and Release

The test dataset — excluded from all training and validation activities to date — is used as an independent dataset to confirm acceptable performance within the overarching application's UAT prior to deployment. At minimum, the verification process must be specified and documented, resulting in formal release of the first AI/ML sub-system version.

解說：模型開發的關鍵概念

超參數（Hyperparameters）是什麼？

機器學習中有兩類「數字」：

  • 模型參數（Parameters）：模型在訓練過程中自動學習的內部值（如神經網絡的權重）——你不直接設定，模型自己調整。
  • 超參數（Hyperparameters）：你在訓練前設定的「控制旋鈕」——如學習率、樹的深度、隱藏層數量。這些值決定了「模型如何學習」，而非「模型學到了什麼」。

超參數優化是 AI/ML 開發中最耗時的工作之一，需要反覆試驗不同的組合，找到使模型在驗證集上表現最佳的設定。

「模組化」設計與 GxP 的關係

GAMP 5 要求「推理模組（Inference Module）」必須與訓練代碼分離。為什麼這對 GxP 很重要？

類比：就像製藥製造中，我們把「生產配方」和「工藝開發記錄」分開管理。生產版本是固定且受控的；開發版本可以迭代修改。

在 AI 中，推理模組是「固定且受控的生產版本」；訓練代碼是「可以繼續優化的開發工具」。驗證只需覆蓋推理模組的確定性行為，而非整個訓練基礎設施。

UAT 中的 Test Set：類似於製藥的「製程確認批次」

Test Set 在 AI/ML 驗證中的角色，類似於製藥製程驗證中的 Process Performance Qualification（PPQ）批次：

  • 整個開發過程中完全封存，從不參與訓練或超參數調整
  • 只在最終確認階段使用一次，作為「在全新數據上的獨立性能驗證」
  • 如果 test set 性能不達標，不能只是「調整模型繼續試」——需要回到設計根本原因分析

視覺評估 vs 純數字指標

GAMP 5 特別強調：不要只依賴準確率、召回率等數字指標，視覺定性評估往往更有洞察力。

製藥 AI 場景舉例：一個視覺檢查 AI 整體準確率達到 99%，但對某種特定缺陷類型（例如微小氣泡）的漏檢率達到 40%——單看整體指標完全看不出這個問題。只有對錯誤案例進行逐一的視覺審查，才能發現這個系統性盲點。

31.3.4 Life Cycle: Operation Phase — Monitoring & Continuous Evaluation

The operation phase is where AI/ML systems diverge most significantly from traditional computerized systems. The performance of the AI/ML sub-system must be continuously monitored and maintained.

31.3.4.1 Monitoring for Static Systems

For static systems, changes must follow the organization's formal change-management process with risk-based evaluation of impact on current and future production data, and robust testing before deployment.

31.3.4.1 Monitoring for Dynamic Systems

For dynamic systems, appropriate KPIs and acceptable tolerance limits must be established to ensure the algorithm is still operating as intended. A systematic approach to integrating additional training data must be maintained:

  1. Acquire additional data of the needed sub-class
  2. Assign a portion to training set; exclude the remainder for testing
  3. Retrain model on augmented training dataset (expect possible performance drop due to increased challenge)
  4. Evaluate revised model against original model on augmented test dataset
  5. Confirm revised model achieves acceptable performance level before deployment

31.3.4.2 Performance Trending

In the operational phase, it is possible to integrate and prepare new data to further refine existing models, develop new predictive models, and establish performance monitoring to track ongoing effectiveness. Quality control standards and measures must exist to ensure acceptable performance throughout the model's usable life.

"In all cases, periodic review and monitoring of the model performance is needed to identify potential bias, overfitting, etc. The timing of reviews may be determined based on a defined interval and/or by activity such as the incorporation of new case data."
— ISPE GAMP 5 Second Edition, Appendix D11, §31.3.5.1

解說：運維階段——模型漂移與治理

模型漂移（Model Drift）：AI 最隱性的風險

模型漂移是指 AI 模型的預測性能隨時間逐漸下降的現象，通常發生在以下情況：

  • 數據漂移（Data Drift）：生產環境的輸入數據特性發生了變化（例如：換了一台新的充填機，其震動特徵與訓練數據不同）
  • 概念漂移（Concept Drift）：「正確答案」的定義發生了變化（例如：外觀可接受標準更新，但模型仍使用舊標準）
  • 過度擬合退化：模型過於適應歷史特定數據，在新數據上表現下降

危險之處在於漂移是緩慢的、難以察覺的。如果沒有持續的性能監控，你可能幾個月後才發現模型已經失效——而在此期間的所有決策都已基於一個不可靠的模型。

類比：製程驗證中的「持續製程確認（CPV）」

製藥製程驗證有三個階段：設計（PPD）、確認（PPQ）、持續確認（CPV）。CPV 的核心就是持續監控製程數據，確認製程狀態保持在驗證的範圍內。

AI/ML 模型的「持續性能監控」正是同樣的邏輯：驗證不是一次性活動，而是貫穿整個產品生命週期。每次監控觸發的模型更新都需要遵循變更控制程序，就像製程參數變更一樣。

定義「可接受性能參數（Tolerance Limits）」的挑戰

對靜態軟體，驗證標準是明確的（結果必須等於預期值）。對 AI/ML 模型，需要定義：

  • 哪些 KPI 用於監控？（準確率、精確率、召回率、F1 分數……）
  • 可接受的性能下限是多少？
  • 超出限度時的反應程序是什麼？（警告、自動切換為人工審查、強制重新訓練）
  • 多久進行一次定期審查？（基於時間間隔，還是基於數據量累積？）

這些標準必須在驗證方案中預先定義，而非事後設定——這是 GxP 合規的基本要求。

31.3.5 Supporting Processes: Risk Management, Data Governance & Change Management

31.3.5.1 Risk Management

Risk management drives the process and controls needed for AI/ML systems. The risk framework must address both the traditional risks of the original process AND the additional risks introduced by ML intervention. Key risk considerations include:

  • Use of external vendors and data suppliers
  • Retaining sufficient technical and scientific knowledge within the organization
  • Model maturity and extent of previous real-world use
  • Changes to production data and/or errant (corrupted) input data
  • System performance, downtime, and business continuity

For static ML sub-systems where all data acquisition and annotation are supervised and validated prior to inclusion, standard data validation and change-management processes are generally sufficient.

For dynamic ML sub-systems — including online learning with continuous model parameter updates — additional controls are required: continual and robust performance evaluation, defined acceptance criteria for ongoing model changes, and heightened monitoring.

In all cases, periodic review is needed to identify bias, overfitting, and performance degradation. Review frequency may be determined by time interval or by activity triggers such as incorporation of new case data.

31.3.5.2 Data Governance

Data governance is critical to the success of ML. Not all data is created equal. The governance strategy must address:

  • Data size, quality, and prevalence — what volume is sufficient for training?
  • Whether a separate data-acquisition project is needed before model development begins
  • Format specification, annotation tools, and cleanup processes
  • How ground-truth data is generated, validated, and maintained

For image-based tasks (e.g., visual inspection), ground truth is produced by expert labeling — a time-intensive process that requires people with both technical and domain expertise.

31.3.5.3 Change Management

Change management integrates data controls into system responses and processes to maintain ongoing control. Drivers of change in AI/ML systems include:

  • Performance Requirements: Changes to improve performance — may trigger model retraining on existing datasets
  • Additional Inputs: Changes to case data or algorithms to expand compatibility and increase generalization
  • Intended Use: Changes to the significance of information or the clinical/manufacturing context

User stories and system controls, along with human intervention as a check, are effective starting points for designing the change-management workflow. Visual process maps with scenarios and mitigations help identify weak points.

解說：支撐流程——數據治理、風險管理、變更控制

AI/ML 風險評估：比傳統系統多了哪些維度？

傳統 GAMP 5 風險評估問：「如果系統失效，對患者安全、產品品質、數據完整性的影響是什麼？」

AI/ML 必須額外問：

  • 訓練數據是否代表了所有重要的使用場景？（覆蓋率風險）
  • 模型是否對特定子群體（特定產品類型、特定設備）有系統性偏差？（偏差風險）
  • 模型的決策過程是否透明？稽查員能否理解某個決定的依據？（黑盒風險）
  • 如果模型在生產中突然失效，後備程序是什麼？（業務連續性風險）

數據治理：AI 的 GMP 原料管理

製藥生產有嚴格的原料管理：CoA 確認、供應商資格、入庫檢驗、儲存條件。每批原料的品質直接影響最終產品。

AI 訓練數據就是模型的「原料」。數據治理就是 AI 的「原料管理」：

  • 數據來源驗證（相當於供應商資格）
  • 數據品質確認（相當於入庫檢驗）
  • 數據版本控制（相當於批次記錄）
  • 標注品質管理（相當於製程控制）

沒有 GMP 原料管理的製藥廠是不合規的；沒有數據治理的 AI/ML 開發同樣無法通過 GxP 驗證。

「Human in the Loop（人在迴路中）」的 GxP 要求

這是 GxP AI/ML 部署中最重要的原則之一。對於 GxP 關鍵決策（批次放行、OOS 判定、偏差分類），AI 可以提供輔助分析和建議，但最終決策必須由具有資質的人員做出並簽署。

這不僅是現行監管立場的要求，更是一個深層的品質原則：

  • AI 模型可能有我們尚未發現的盲點
  • 異常情況可能超出模型的訓練邊界
  • 監管責任無法轉移給算法

CDMO 實踐建議：在 SOP 中明確界定「AI 輔助」與「AI 決策」的邊界，確保所有 GxP 決策都有有資質人員的電子簽章背書。

AI 變更管理的複雜性：什麼算「重大變更」？

傳統軟體變更管理相對清晰：代碼修改就觸發變更流程。但 AI/ML 的「變更」定義更複雜：

  • 加入新訓練數據後模型自動更新——算變更嗎？
  • 超參數微調後模型性能提升 0.5%——需要重新驗證嗎？
  • 輸入數據的分布發生了漂移——模型本身沒改變，但有效性已改變

GAMP 5 的建議：在驗證文件中預先定義「重大變更」的觸發條件（例如性能變化超過 X%），以及不同類型變更的審批路徑，避免事後爭議。

31.4 Regulatory Perspectives on AI/ML in Pharma Manufacturing

The regulatory framework for AI/ML in pharmaceutical manufacturing is actively evolving. GAMP 5 Appendix D11 references the Joint US FDA/Health Canada/UK MHRA Good Machine Learning Practice (GMLP) for Medical Device Development: Guiding Principles — currently the most comprehensive regulatory framework directly applicable to AI/ML in regulated environments.

Key FDA / MHRA GMLP Guiding Principles Referenced

Principle Focus Area
GP 1 & 2 Multi-disciplinary expertise; good software engineering and security practices
GP 6 Model selection fit for the intended purpose
GP 8 Performance demonstrated during model testing through scorecards
GP 9 Users are provided with clear, essential information — transparency of AI outputs
GP 10 Deployed models are monitored for performance and users can report problems

The "Continuous Learning" Validation Challenge

The FDA's action plan for AI/ML-based Software as a Medical Device (SaMD) acknowledges that traditional pre-market testing cannot fully address the unique nature of continuously learning AI systems. The regulatory challenge is that a model validated at time of approval may legitimately change over time through continued learning — raising questions about re-validation triggers.

Current industry consensus positions:

  • Any significant model change (performance shift beyond defined tolerance, change in intended use, change in training data scope) should trigger a formal change assessment
  • Pre-defined performance monitoring plans with explicit alert thresholds should be part of the validation package
  • Transparency reporting to regulators for significant post-deployment model changes is emerging as expected practice

Human Oversight Requirement

Current regulatory guidance universally maintains that for GxP-critical decisions, AI should assist human judgment, not replace it. Automated AI-driven decisions in GxP-critical processes (batch release, OOS investigation conclusions) remain a high regulatory risk without explicit guidance permitting them. Decisions must be attributable to qualified human reviewers who can evaluate and accept or override AI-generated recommendations.

解說：監管展望與 CDMO 戰略定位

FDA GMLP 指導原則：製藥製造的適用性

GAMP 5 引用的 FDA/Health Canada/MHRA 聯合 GMLP 指導原則原本是針對醫療設備軟體（SaMD）制定的，但其原則直接適用於製藥製造 AI：

  • 多學科團隊（數據科學家 + 製程工程師 + QA）
  • 良好的軟件工程實踐（版本控制、代碼審查、測試文件）
  • 透明的性能評估方法
  • 部署後持續監控和問題回報機制

對 CDMO QA 的實際意義：AI 系統的驗證主協議（VP）和驗證總結報告（VSR）中應明確引用 GMLP 相關原則作為指導框架。

「持續學習」的監管困境：一個思想實驗

假設你在 2026 年 1 月對一個視覺檢查 AI 完成了完整的驗證。到 2026 年 6 月，該模型已經從 50,000 個新的生產數據點中學習了——它的準確率從 97% 提升到了 99%。

問題：你需要重新驗證嗎？性能提升了，但模型的「DNA」已完全不同。

目前的監管立場傾向於：是的，需要觸發變更評估和重新驗證——即使性能改善了。原因是：沒有人能完全確定性能改善不是以犧牲某些邊緣情況的性能為代價。

白鴉（White Raven）案例：CDMO AI 競爭情報啟示

歐洲競爭對手 White Raven CDMO 已開始在其 SA25 充填機上部署 AI 解決方案。這代表行業前沿正在快速移動。

關鍵問題：他們如何解決 GxP 驗證問題？可能的路徑：

  • 使用靜態 AI 模型（定期訓練更新，每次作為受控變更）——監管風險最低
  • AI 作為「輔助建議系統」而非決策系統——人員仍然做最終決定
  • 先在非 GxP 關鍵應用（預測性維護）上積累驗證經驗

這也應該是我們 CDMO AI 路線圖的策略起點：從預測性維護和非 GxP 關鍵監測開始，逐步積累驗證能力，再擴展到 GxP 關鍵應用。

CDMO AI/ML 實施路線圖建議

Phase 1（現在可以開始）：非 GxP 關鍵應用

  • 充填機預測性維護（Predictive Maintenance）
  • 冷凍乾燥製程參數優化輔助工具
  • EM 趨勢分析異常偵測（警示，非決策）

Phase 2（12-18 個月後）：輔助性 GxP 應用

  • AI 輔助批次記錄審查（提高人工審查效率）
  • 偏差初步分類輔助

Phase 3（長期）：GxP 關鍵應用

  • 自動視覺檢查（需完整 GMLP 符合性驗證）
  • 即時製程分析技術（PAT）AI 模型

Section Summary  |  本章重點總結

Appendix D10 — Blockchain (區塊鏈) Key Takeaways

  • Blockchain provides cryptographic immutability for transaction records — but cannot guarantee the accuracy of data initially posted; input controls remain critical.
  • The blockchain is typically the source of truth, not the source of origin; all source systems (MES, LIMS) must maintain ALCOA+ compliance.
  • Four control categories are required: Input / Output / Processing / Access — with particular attention to API integrity and private key management.
  • Smart contracts must undergo code review and change management as GxP software components.
  • Regulatory guidance on whether blockchain records satisfy 21 CFR Part 11 / EU Annex 11 is still evolving — conservative validation approaches and industry engagement (ISPE GAMP CoP) are recommended.
  • Technology maturity evaluation (network age, developer community, change governance) is essential before selecting a blockchain platform for GxP use.

Appendix D11 — AI/ML Key Takeaways

  • AI/ML introduces a fundamentally different validation challenge: dynamic models change as they learn — validation must be ongoing, not a one-time activity.
  • Data is the primary asset in AI/ML: GIGO applies — data governance (classification, labeling, partitioning, provenance) is as important as algorithm selection.
  • Dataset partitioning into training / validation / test sets must be established and maintained from the concept phase — data contamination undermines all subsequent validation.
  • Model drift (gradual performance degradation) requires continuous KPI monitoring with pre-defined tolerance limits and periodic review triggers.
  • For GxP-critical decisions, AI must assist, not replace, qualified human judgment — "human in the loop" remains the regulatory baseline.
  • Start AI/ML programs with non-GxP-critical applications (predictive maintenance, EM trend analysis) to build validation competency before expanding to GxP-critical use cases.

Shared Theme: Risk-Based Validation in the Age of Emerging Technologies

Both blockchain and AI/ML represent cases where traditional SDLC and validation frameworks must be applied with adaptation. GAMP 5 2nd Edition's core message: the principles remain the same (risk-based, life-cycle approach, patient-centered), but their application must evolve with the technology.

For both technologies, the concept phase is disproportionately important — decisions made about governance, data architecture, and system boundaries at the start determine whether GxP compliance is achievable at all.

新興技術共同主題：概念階段的決定性作用

區塊鏈和 AI/ML 的共同教訓：概念階段的決策品質決定了整個系統的可驗證性。倉促進入開發的結果往往是：到了驗證階段才發現根本性的架構問題，代價極高。

核心心法：不要問「這個 AI/區塊鏈技術能做什麼」，而是問「這個技術能否以符合 GxP 的方式被驗證和維護」。技術可行性和法規可行性必須同時評估。

7

Section 7: App O1-O13: Operation Appendices (Handover, CAPA, Security, Archiving)

附錄O：運營附錄（移交、CAPA、安全管理、歸檔） | p281-p346

ISPE GAMP 5 Second Edition | Appendices O, O1–O5 | Doc p281–p302

Learning Objectives — 學習目標

  1. Understand the purpose and scope of GAMP 5 Operational Appendices and how they extend the lifecycle beyond go-live. / 了解 GAMP 5 運營附錄的目的與範圍，以及其如何將系統生命週期延伸至上線後階段。
  2. Define what constitutes a complete and compliant handover (App O1) from the project team to the operations/support organization. / 定義構成從專案團隊到運營/支援組織的完整合規移交（附錄 O1）的要素。
  3. Describe the structure and GxP-specific considerations for Service Level Agreements (SLAs) and support tiers. / 描述服務水平協議（SLA）的結構及針對 GxP 系統的特殊考量。
  4. Identify what system monitoring must cover in a GxP context beyond standard IT availability checks. / 識別 GxP 系統監控超越標準 IT 可用性檢查的範圍，包括稽核軌跡完整性與存取控制。
  5. Explain incident classification, the three-tier support model, and when a GxP deviation must be raised. / 解釋事件分類、三層支援模型，以及何時必須發起 GxP 偏差報告。
  6. Apply the CAPA process to computerized system failures, linking IT incident records to the quality management system. / 將 CAPA 流程應用於電腦化系統故障，將 IT 事件記錄連結至品質管理系統。
App O Appendix O — Introduction to Operation Appendices (p281–p282)

Appendix O — Introduction to Operation Appendices

Purpose and Scope

The Operational Appendices provide guidance on how to maintain GxP computerized systems in a compliant state after go-live. These appendices ensure that GxP computerized systems continue to maintain patient safety, product quality, and the integrity of GxP data and records.

The Operational Appendices may be used as a foundation for implementing policies, procedures, and/or work instructions within the QMS. The application of good IT practices such as described by ITIL [54], supported by IT service management tools and automation, is encouraged.

Scalability Principle

Scalability should be considered: controls can be implemented at a level of formality and complexity appropriate to the individual organization and across a wide range of systems. Organizations may have straightforward controls for simple systems and more sophisticated tools and procedures for systems with increased impact, size, and complexity.

Non-Prescriptive Approach

In view of the diversity of computerized systems and organizations, it is not considered appropriate to be prescriptive regarding how operational controls are implemented. To ensure compliance with regulatory expectations, regulated companies should be able to demonstrate that they have:

  • Considered and reviewed the maintenance and support needs for each system
  • Decided what procedures, processes, and records should be established and maintained

Operational Process Relationships

Figure 32.1 (source document) illustrates the relationships between operational processes. The key operational appendices — Handover (O1), Support Services (O2), System Monitoring (O3), Incident & Problem Management (O4), CAPA (O5), and Change & Configuration Management (O6) — form an interconnected lifecycle management framework.

中文解說 — 運營附錄導論

為什麼需要「運營附錄」？

GAMP 5 大部分內容聚焦於驗證（Validation）專案階段，但系統驗證通過只是生命週期的中點，而非終點。附錄 O 系列專門處理 go-live 之後 的持續合規維護。

核心概念：從「驗證過」到「維持驗證狀態」

監管機構（FDA、EMA）關注的不只是系統上線時是否符合規範，更要求企業能證明系統在整個使用期間（數年乃至數十年）持續維持在受控、合規的狀態。這就是 Operational Appendices 的核心存在意義。

ITIL 框架的引用意義

GAMP 5 明確引用 ITIL（IT Infrastructure Library）作為良好 IT 實踐的基礎。對 CDMO 而言，這代表：IT 部門不應自訂一套流程，而應採用業界成熟框架，並在其上疊加 GxP 要求層。

可擴展性（Scalability）的實務意義

對 CDMO 最重要的一點：GAMP 5 允許依照系統重要性調整控制嚴格程度。

  • Category 3 配方軟體（高 GxP 風險）→ 需要完整的 SLA、事件分類、CAPA 鏈接
  • 辦公室文書系統（低 GxP 風險）→ 標準 IT 維護即可

類比：工廠設備保養 vs 電腦系統維護

就像無菌充填設備需要持續校正、清潔驗證、預防保養計畫一樣，電腦化系統也需要對應的「IT 版」維護體系——這正是 O1-O6 所建立的框架。

App O1 Appendix O1 — Handover (p283–p286)

Appendix O1 — Handover

33.1 Introduction

Handover is the process of moving the computerized system from the project phase to the operational phase. This includes the transfer of responsibilities for:

  • Maintaining the computerized system in a validated state
  • Maintaining data integrity

These responsibilities transfer to the business process owner, data owner, and system owner.

33.2 Key Requirements

Regulated companies should be able to demonstrate the formal acceptance of computerized systems following the completion of validation activities and verification of the controlled transfer of the system into operational use.

33.4 Guidance

33.4.1 General Approach

The project management approach should include a process for handover from the project phase into the operational phase. Handover activities should ensure that the business and support organization are ready to receive the new or upgraded solution following confirmation of successful validation (e.g., approval of the validation report).

Key handover activities cover:

Confirmation of the Validated State: The validated state of the computerized system should be confirmed — including closure of change controls, approval of validation reports. System specifications should be in an "as built" state reflecting the configuration baseline of the validated system. SOPs should be updated to reflect changed roles; training provided in new or modified business processes.

Managed Handover of Open Items: Open items remaining at handover (defects, incomplete training, documents awaiting approval) must be transferred in a controlled manner in accordance with risk. Incident logs, change records, CAPAs, or deviations may be raised to ensure open items are appropriately assigned. Particular attention should be given to items that could negatively impact GxP or compromise compliance status.

Completion of Data Migration: Data migration/load has been successfully completed in accordance with a documented data migration plan and data migration report.

Update of Configuration Items: Updates to the CMDB/configuration items list for the system are complete. New system modules and infrastructure components have been registered.

Establishing Support Agreements and Controls: Establishment of appropriate SLAs, quality agreements, OLAs, or contracts defining support requirements. Creation/update of operational support procedures in accordance with the O Appendices. Service management tools used in the provision of support services have been established/updated.

Knowledge Transfer: Knowledge transfer to support organizations should be conducted. This includes transfer of system lifecycle documentation, business process and data flows, and risk assessments. Knowledge transfer is not only documentation — it also includes transfer of implicit knowledge and lessons learned by the project team.

"Knowledge transfer is not only the transfer of documentation and records; it also includes the transfer of knowledge and experiences of the project team, including implicit knowledge that cannot be easily articulated in documentation and records."

Hypercare and Monitoring of Business Readiness: Depending on complexity, a period of hypercare may be required — a phased transition from project team to support team following handover. Hypercare continues until defined criteria are met (e.g., post go-live incidents diminishing in quantity and severity; support organization has demonstrated adequate knowledge). A rollback strategy should be defined in the event of a significant problem.

33.4.2 Responsibilities

  • Project Manager: Prepares the system for handover
  • Process Owner, Data Owner, System Owner: Accepts the system into operational use

中文解說 — 系統移交

移交的本質：責任的正式轉移

移交（Handover）不只是「把系統交出去」，而是一次法律和品質責任的正式轉移。移交後，若系統出現數據完整性問題，責任主體從專案經理轉移到系統擁有者（System Owner）。

CDMO 實務警示：移交是最常被輕忽的步驟

許多 CDMO 在驗證通過後就急著上線，卻沒有完成正式移交文件。這在 FDA 483 觀察項目中屢見不鮮——稽查員會問：「誰在維護這個系統的驗證狀態？」若找不到正式移交記錄，等同於系統責任歸屬不明。

CDMO 移交查核清單（實務版）

以下是 CDMO 環境下移交前必須確認的事項，對應 GAMP 5 要求：

類別確認事項責任人
驗證狀態驗證報告已核准，所有 change control 已關閉Validation Engineer
文件SOP 已更新反映新流程，訓練記錄已完成QA
數據遷移數據遷移報告已核准，歷史數據可查詢IT + Data Owner
備份備份排程已設定並測試過還原IT
支援協議SLA 已簽署，IT helpdesk 已知悉此系統System Owner
開放項目所有開放缺陷已登記追蹤，GxP 影響已評估PM + QA
知識轉移IT 支援人員已完成系統訓練Project Team
回退計畫Rollback 程序已文件化並已演練IT + PM

Hypercare：不是可選的，是必要的

GAMP 5 第二版新增了 Hypercare 概念。對複雜系統（如 MES、LIMS），建議設定至少 4–8 週的 hypercare 期，在此期間：

  • 專案團隊仍保持隨時待命
  • 每日記錄事件數量與嚴重性
  • 只有在事件趨勢穩定下降後才正式結束 hypercare

Hypercare 期結束應有正式文件記錄，這是移交完成的最終確認。

「隱性知識」轉移的挑戰

GAMP 5 特別強調，知識轉移不只是交出文件，還要包含無法寫進文件的「經驗知識」。對 CDMO 而言，這意味著：

  • 舉辦工作坊讓 IT 支援人員「跟著用」
  • 記錄「已知問題及其臨時解決方案」
  • 專案團隊在 hypercare 期應主動 coaching，而非只提供文件
App O2 Appendix O2 — Establishing and Managing Support Services (p287–p290)

Appendix O2 — Establishing and Managing Support Services

34.1 Introduction

The process for establishing and managing support services ensures that support services (whether internal or external) are appropriately specified and managed. This is often governed by Service Level Agreements (SLAs).

34.2 Key Requirements

When external service providers are used, there should be a formal agreement that clearly states the services to be provided and the responsibilities of the service provider and the regulated company. This applies to both external third parties and internal support functions.

34.4 Guidance

Types of Agreements

Service Level Agreement (SLA): Describes the services to be provided and service level targets; specifies responsibilities of both parties. May be established separately for individual systems or cover groups of similar systems.

Operating Level Agreement (OLA): An agreement between a service provider and another part of the same organization. Example: agreement between the primary support organization and a storage management group regarding file restoration times.

Underpinning Contract (UC): A contract between a service provider and a third party that provides goods or services integral to overall support service delivery. Example: a contract with a telecommunications provider for WAN maintenance.

Additionally, a Quality Agreement may be required, defining the quality expectations of the regulated company to be achieved by the service provider.

34.4.4 SLA Content Requirements

SLAs should address:

  • Scope of computerized systems/support services to be provided
  • Service descriptions including:
    • Software releases, patch, maintenance, enhancement releases
    • IT infrastructure and platform services
    • IT security
    • Backup and restoration
    • Business continuity and disaster recovery
    • Information security and data privacy controls
    • Data archiving and retention
    • Record and asset disposal
    • System maintenance, administration, repair, housekeeping
    • Maintenance of separate development, testing, and operations environments
    • Routine testing and calibration
    • Training
  • System support tools (e.g., service desk, security monitoring, backup)
  • Roles and responsibilities
  • Reporting, prioritization, and processing times for support requests and faults
  • Key contact details
  • Escalation processes

34.4.5 Measurement, Reporting, and Review

Service performance monitoring should be defined in terms of:

  • Key performance metrics (system and data availability, downtime, unplanned outages, response times, incidents)
  • Reporting frequency
  • Periodic review meetings

34.4.6 Managing Contract Exit

Contract exit should be planned in advance. Agreements should address:

  • Knowledge transfer
  • Documentation/records transfer
  • Software code transfer
  • Data transfer

中文解說 — 支援服務管理

GxP 系統的 SLA：遠不只是「99.9% 可用性」

一般 IT 的 SLA 談的是系統可用性（uptime）。但 GxP 系統的 SLA 必須涵蓋更廣的內容，因為監管要求比商業 SLA 更嚴格。

CDMO 建議的 GxP SLA 關鍵指標

指標類型關鍵 GxP 系統建議值備注
系統可用性（Uptime）≥ 99.5%（計畫維護除外）批次記錄系統、LIMS 等
P1 事件響應時間15 分鐘內確認，2 小時內解決P1 = 生產停擺或數據完整性受損
P2 事件響應時間1 小時內確認，8 小時內解決P2 = 功能降級但可繼續生產
備份完成率每日備份成功率 100%備份失敗必須立即通報
備份還原測試每季至少一次DR 演練，測試還原時間 RTO
安全補丁部署關鍵補丁 30 天內，其餘 90 天內需走 change control 流程
稽查軌跡可用性隨時可查詢，保存期 ≥ 系統退役後 1 年21 CFR Part 11 要求

三種協議的區別（SLA / OLA / UC）

對 CDMO 來說，理解這三種協議的區別很重要，因為監管稽查時稽查員可能要求出示：

  • SLA（對外）：CDMO 與 SAP/Oracle 等系統供應商簽訂的服務協議
  • OLA（對內）：IT 部門與 QA 部門之間的內部服務協議（例如 IT 承諾在多少時間內恢復系統）
  • UC（供應鏈）：IT 供應商與其子供應商之間的合約（例如雲端服務商與數據中心的合約）

品質協議（Quality Agreement）的重要性

對外部雲端系統供應商（如 AWS、Veeva），除了 SLA 之外，還需要一份品質協議（Quality Agreement），明確：

  • 供應商的稽查軌跡保存責任
  • 稽查配合義務（允許監管機構到訪稽查）
  • 數據所有權歸屬
  • 服務終止時的數據交還/刪除程序

缺少品質協議是 FDA 警告信的常見原因之一。

合約退出計畫（Contract Exit）

GAMP 5 第二版新增了合約退出條款。對 CDMO 而言，這意味著在簽訂 SLA 時就要規劃：「如果我們要換供應商，如何確保數據和系統知識的完整轉移？」這是一個經常被忽略的風險點，尤其在雲端 SaaS 系統（如 Veeva Vault）合約到期時。

App O3 Appendix O3 — System Monitoring (p291–p293)

Appendix O3 — System Monitoring

35.1 Introduction

System monitoring can be used to monitor and report system failures, availability, performance, configuration baseline, and information security issues. Feedback from monitoring processes and tools can be used to anticipate and respond to potential computerized system incidents and to improve the overall controls environment.

35.2 Key Requirements

The need for, and extent of, monitoring activities should be based on business risk and risk to patient safety, product quality, and data integrity. The extent of monitoring shall also be relative to the type of system and its external exposure.

35.4 Guidance

35.4.1 General Approach

System monitoring may cover a specific system, group of systems, or an IT infrastructure environment. The extent of monitoring is dependent on system complexity, business impact, patient safety, product quality, data integrity impact, and external threats such as cybersecurity threats.

35.4.2 Responsibilities

System Owner:

  • Ensures system monitoring is in place based on risk
  • Works with system administrators and IT to ensure system monitoring is implemented
  • Participates in the incident and problem management process for detected incidents

Business Process Owner / Data Owner:

  • Agrees on scope of system monitoring
  • Participates in incident and problem management process

35.4.3 System Monitoring Considerations

System monitoring should consider the following:

  • System and data availability
  • System performance and resources (CPU utilization, storage capacities)
  • Network routing, load, and failures
  • Configuration status against configuration templates
  • Batch job failures including backups
  • System interface failures
  • Instrumentation communication failures
  • Software, operating system, and hardware failures
  • Printer queue failures
  • System and process alarms and events
  • Response times
  • Security vulnerabilities
  • Intrusion detection

35.4.4 System Monitoring Tools

System monitoring should leverage automated tools wherever possible. Such tools can detect and report potential system incidents and automatically alert support organizations. Some monitoring tools include self-rectification capabilities — resources such as processing and storage capacity can automatically adjust to address performance issues. Monitoring tools can also automatically reset configuration that does not meet the current configuration template.

35.4.5 Manual Monitoring

Manual monitoring activities can be defined in and scheduled from service management tools or defined in system administration plans or procedures. Monitoring tasks, roles, frequency, and reporting requirements should be clearly defined.

中文解說 — 系統監控

GxP 系統監控 ≠ 一般 IT 系統監控

IT 部門通常只監控「系統有沒有在跑」，但 GxP 合規要求的監控範圍遠超於此。對 CDMO 而言，以下三個維度缺一不可：

GxP 監控的三個維度

維度 1：IT 可用性監控（傳統 IT）

  • 系統是否在線、響應時間是否正常
  • CPU/儲存資源使用率
  • 備份是否成功執行

維度 2：GxP 數據完整性監控（GxP 特有）

  • 稽查軌跡（Audit Trail）是否完整，有無異常修改
  • 電子簽名是否有效
  • 系統時鐘是否與標準時間同步（時間戳造假的常見途徑）
  • 數據備份完整性定期驗證

維度 3：資訊安全與存取控制監控（合規要求）

  • 異常登入嘗試（非工作時間登入、帳號共用跡象）
  • 存取權限是否符合最新的使用者角色清單
  • 配置偏離（Configuration Drift）：系統設定是否偏離驗證基準

配置偏離（Configuration Drift）監控

GAMP 5 特別提到監控「配置狀態是否符合配置模板」。這是 GxP 系統的關鍵概念：系統驗證時確立了一個「基準配置」，任何未經授權的配置變更都可能使系統脫離驗證狀態。

實務案例：LIMS 配置偏離事件

某 CDMO 的 LIMS 系統，IT 人員在未開 change control 的情況下更改了計算公式參數。三個月後稽查發現，此配置偏離導致部分品管檢測結果計算誤差。若有配置監控工具，可在問題產生當下立即告警，而非三個月後才發現。

儀器通訊失敗的監控

GAMP 5 特別列出「儀器通訊失敗」（Instrumentation communication failures）作為監控項目。對無菌充填 CDMO 而言，這包括：

  • 環境監控系統（EMS）感測器通訊中斷
  • 秤重系統與 MES 的介面失敗
  • SCADA 系統與 DCS 的通訊中斷

這類失敗若未被即時發現，可能導致批次記錄中缺少關鍵數據，觸發數據完整性偏差。

App O4 Appendix O4 — Incident Management and Problem Management (p295–p297)

Appendix O4 — Incident Management and Problem Management

36.1 Introduction — Key Definitions

An incident relates to the effect of an unplanned interruption to a service, or reduction in service quality, typically linked to a breach of the SLA, user observation, or feedback from automated monitoring tools.

A problem relates to the root cause of one or more incidents. Problems can be raised in response to a single significant incident or multiple related incidents.

"Problems are the cause and incidents are the effect."

36.2 Key Requirements

Unplanned computerized system interruptions or reductions in service quality should be reported, investigated, and resolved by support teams in order to ensure incidents are effectively managed.

36.4.1 Incident Management — Three-Tier Support Model

Level 1 Support is usually provided by IT SMEs staffing the help desk. Level 1 gathers information describing the incident, conducts basic investigations and troubleshooting, and solves common problems such as access issues, solution understanding, setup issues, and service restoration.

Level 2 Support conducts a more in-depth assessment of the incident and identifies available solutions. Level 2 is generally provided by IT SMEs outside the help desk staff. If no available solutions exist, a problem is raised and handed to Level 3 support.

Level 3 Support is provided by SMEs such as developers, DevOps, architects, engineers, or external software/IT service suppliers. Level 3 investigates potential design and implementation issues. Technical solutions may be required.

Major Incidents: Relate to serious disruption to business operations and should be resolved with greater urgency. A major incident team comprising business, technical, and quality expertise may be assembled. Business continuity and disaster recovery plans may need to be invoked.

36.4.2 Problem Management

Problem management is the process by which the root cause of one or more incidents is determined and solutions are implemented to minimize the risk of similar incidents occurring in the future. Problem management processes are integrated with change management, configuration management, training, and disaster recovery.

Resolution of a problem may also involve GxP CAPA activities.

Communication is an essential part of the incident and problem management process to ensure business users and the quality unit are aware of any disruptions or restrictions of service.

36.4.3 Determining GxP Impact

Incidents are generally reported directly to technical functions who are not necessarily SMEs with respect to the impact on patient safety, product quality, and data integrity.

Configuration Management Databases (CMDB) or other tools should identify configuration items (hardware components, application modules, business processes, records) that impact GxP. Processes for GxP determination should be agreed by business process owners, data owners, and the quality unit.

The quality unit should be informed of incidents and problems potentially impacting product quality and patient safety. They may raise a quality deviation and initiate a CAPA process. IT, system owners, process owners, and the quality unit should cooperate in ensuring effective resolution.

36.4.4 Incident and Problem Records

Incident and problem records are typically managed in IT tools and capture: incident/problem information, impact assessments, root cause analyses, and actions taken to resolve the problem including any workarounds. If changes are required to system lifecycle documentation or configuration records, they should be updated and tested in line with any changes implemented.

中文解說 — 事件管理與問題管理

事件（Incident）vs 問題（Problem）：概念上的關鍵區別

這是 ITIL 框架的核心概念，在 GxP 環境中尤為重要：

  • 事件：使用者感受到的現象（系統變慢、功能無法使用）
  • 問題：造成事件的根本原因（資料庫索引損壞、記憶體洩漏）

同一個「問題」可能引發多個「事件」。問題管理的目標是永久消除根本原因，而不只是一次次解決個別事件。

何時需要發起 GxP 偏差報告（Deviation）？

這是 CDMO QA 人員最常被問到的問題。判斷標準：

情境是否需要偏差報告原因
系統速度變慢，使用者抱怨否（一般事件）不影響 GxP 數據完整性
LIMS 無法登入，1 小時後恢復視情況若批次在此期間記錄了數據，需評估影響
稽查軌跡記錄中斷 30 分鐘是數據完整性直接受損
批次生產數據未正確同步至 MES是GxP 記錄的完整性受損
存取控制失效，非授權人員可進入是21 CFR Part 11 / Annex 11 要求
系統時鐘偏移超過 ±1 分鐘是時間戳可靠性受損

判斷原則：任何可能影響數據完整性、患者安全、產品品質的事件，都需要發起偏差報告並啟動 CAPA 評估。

三層支援模型在 CDMO 的實踐

類比：醫療急救的分級制度

就像急診室依照病情嚴重程度分流（輕傷→診所，重傷→急診，危急→加護），IT 支援的三層模型也是一種「資源最佳化」的分流機制。

  • L1（Helpdesk）：「看診」——先問清楚問題，解決密碼重設等簡單問題
  • L2（系統管理員/應用支援）：「急診」——深入診斷，提供已知解決方案
  • L3（供應商/開發商）：「手術室」——需要修改程式碼或設計的根本性解決

CMDB：GxP 影響評估的基礎

GAMP 5 強調 CMDB（配置管理資料庫）應標記哪些配置項目屬於 GxP 範疇。這在實務上意味著：

  • IT 在建立 CMDB 時，需要 QA 的輸入來標記 GxP 相關性
  • 當事件被登入 helpdesk 系統時，系統應自動查詢 CMDB，顯示「此配置項目為 GxP 相關」的警告
  • 這樣 IT 人員即使不了解 GxP，也能知道「這個問題要通知 QA」

常見陷阱：IT 未通知 QA

稽查中最常見的問題：IT 處理了一個影響 GxP 系統的事件，但沒有通知 QA，沒有發起偏差報告，也沒有 CAPA。這通常源於 IT 和 QA 之間缺乏明確的「GxP 影響判定流程」。GAMP 5 要求這個流程必須書面化，並由 QA 批准。

App O5 Appendix O5 — Corrective and Preventive Action (CAPA) (p299–p302)

Appendix O5 — Corrective and Preventive Action (CAPA)

37.1 Introduction

CAPA is a process for investigating, understanding, and correcting deviations and nonconformities to address the immediate impact of the issue and to minimize the risk of recurrence. The scope and depth of CAPA plans should be developed relative to the risk of the associated deviation or nonconformity to patient safety, product quality, and data integrity.

37.2 Key Requirements

The CAPA process covers:

  • Assessment of the impact of the identified deviation or problem
  • Corrective action planning to address the impact
  • Root cause analysis to determine the cause
  • Preventive action to minimize the risk of recurrence
  • Monitoring of action completion
  • Effectiveness checks and trending analysis
