Section 8: App S1-S6 + G1-G2: Special Topics, References & Glossary

附錄S：特殊主題（電子批記錄、試算表、組織變革）+ 參考文獻與詞彙 | p347-p404

ISPE GAMP 5, 2nd Edition | Appendix S1–S6 | p347–p382

Learning Objectives — 學習目標

  1. Explain how GAMP 5 aligns with and differs from ASTM E2500, and determine when each framework is the appropriate tool. ／ 說明 GAMP 5 與 ASTM E2500 的共同原則與適用場景差異。
  2. Describe the structure and regulatory requirements of Electronic Production Records (EPR / eBR / eDHR) including audit trail obligations under 21 CFR Part 11 and EU Annex 11. ／ 描述電子生產記錄的架構、稽核軌跡要求，以及相關法規義務。
  3. Categorize end user applications (spreadsheets, databases, macros) by GAMP category and apply appropriate risk-based validation controls. ／ 依 GAMP 類別分類終端使用者應用程式，套用風險導向驗證控制措施。
  4. Apply a risk-based patch management framework that balances enterprise cybersecurity risk against GxP validated-state maintenance. ／ 建立平衡資安風險與 GxP 驗證狀態的補丁管理決策架構。
  5. Identify the compliance impacts of organizational change (M&A, outsourcing, supplier loss) on validated computerized systems. ／ 識別組織變更對已驗證電腦化系統的法規合規影響。
  6. Apply the stakeholder engagement and documentation update requirements for CSV programs undergoing organizational restructuring. ／ 在組織重組期間，執行 CSV 程式的利害關係人參與及文件更新要求。

Appendix S1 — Alignment with ASTM E2500 (p347–p351)

S1.1 Introduction & Background

GxP regulations require validation of computer and control systems that are critical to patient health and protection. Historically, regulated companies performed installation, commissioning, and validation as separate sequential exercises — producing duplicated documentation that added little value to demonstrating fitness for intended use.

Emerging standards, particularly ASTM E2500 (Standard Guide for Specification, Design, and Verification of Pharmaceutical and Biopharmaceutical Manufacturing Systems and Equipment), adopt a science- and risk-based philosophy focused on patient risk rather than prescriptive activity sequences. Combining Good Engineering Practice (GEP), science- and risk-based approaches, process understanding, and appropriate SME involvement creates a streamlined framework that meets all regulatory requirements.

S1.2 Focusing on Patient Risk

By focusing on risk to the patient and leveraging supplier expertise and SME knowledge through GEP, verification replaces the previously separate IQ and OQ activities as an integrated set of activities. Regulated company IQ/OQ activities may be omitted or limited to assessing supplier activities, closing gaps, and confirming fitness for intended use through Performance Qualification focused on critical-to-quality attributes.

This approach demonstrates that equipment or systems are performing satisfactorily for their intended purpose, the process is controlled, and patient risks are effectively managed — thereby satisfying regulatory validation requirements.

ASTM E2500: The Specification, Design, and Verification Process

ASTM E2500 structures equipment qualification around three integrated phases:

  • Specification — Define critical requirements tied to patient risk
  • Design — Apply GEP with appropriate SME review
  • Verification — Leverage supplier testing; confirm critical-to-quality requirements are met

A plan describing the approach and a report providing evidence supporting fitness for use remain appropriate regardless of terminology used.

S1.3 Different Types of Computerized Systems

For integrated manufacturing systems where a computer-based system is part of overall functionality, a separate computerized system validation may not be required. Where computer-controlled equipment is one component of a wider manufacturing or process control system, verification can be an integrated part of the overall process validation effort.

IT systems with no direct correlation to manufacturing (e.g., clinical trials data collection, adverse event management, product release systems) have no direct parallel to process validation. Acceptance depends on satisfactory functional testing equivalent to OQ prior to controlled cut-over into the live environment.

S1.4 Terminology

GAMP 5 recognizes that different organizations may use different terminology:

  • Some adopt "verification" for both computer and control systems
  • Others retain "qualification" language but apply ASTM E2500 principles
  • Still others use verification for controlled process equipment and qualification for computer systems

GAMP Guidance is neither mandatory nor prescriptive. Individual companies should decide what terms and precise approach they will use, provided the outcome demonstrates fitness for intended use with appropriate risk control.

中文解析：GAMP 5 vs. ASTM E2500

兩個框架的本質差異

ASTM E2500 的核心目標是製造設備與製程系統的規格、設計和驗證（specification, design, and verification）。它是工程導向的，強調把設備的 IQ/OQ 活動整合成一個以病人風險為中心的「verification」流程，大量借用供應商的測試文件。

GAMP 5 的範圍更廣：它涵蓋所有電腦化系統，包括製造執行系統、實驗室系統、ERP、臨床數據系統等，不只是製造設備。

互補關係：ASTM E2500 的思想直接影響了 GAMP 5 的演進——兩者的核心都是「科學+風險導向」，都反對重複且無價值的文件。

實際場景比較

使用 ASTM E2500 的情境：廠房新建時導入無菌灌裝機（aseptic filling machine）。設備製造商的工廠驗收測試（FAT）、現場驗收測試（SAT）可直接作為 verification 的一部分，不需要再另外跑完整的 IQ/OQ 文件套組。

使用 GAMP 5 的情境：同一條灌裝線上的 MES（Manufacturing Execution System）或 SCADA 系統的電腦化系統驗證，屬於 GAMP 5 的主要適用範疇。

重疊區域：整合控制系統（PLC/DCS）通常兩者都適用；此時依公司政策選擇術語即可，關鍵是文件證明 critical-to-quality requirements 已被驗證。

查廠重點

稽核員關注的不是你用哪個術語（IQ/OQ 或 verification），而是：

  • 你有沒有識別出對病人風險有影響的關鍵要求（critical-to-quality requirements）？
  • 你有沒有提供充分的文件證據說明這些要求已被驗證？
  • 你有沒有一份計畫（plan）說明你的驗證方法，以及一份報告（report）作為完成的證據？

CDMO 情境應用

在 CDMO 環境，同一台設備可能生產多個客戶的產品。建議在設備層級做一次完整的 GAMP/ASTM E2500 驗證，然後在產品層級的製程驗證（PV）中確認該設備在特定產品條件下的表現。這樣可以避免每換一個產品就重跑完整 IQ/OQ 的資源浪費。

Appendix S2 — Electronic Production Records (EPR / eBR) (p351–p361)

S2.1 Introduction

This appendix describes best practices for Electronic Production Records (EPRs) in GxP manufacturing environments. EPRs support modern manufacturing paradigms including Review by Exception (RBE), real-time disposition, cloud technology, and blockchain technology.

The ISA-88 standard provides the basis for establishing electronic system terminology equivalent to paper-based batch records. Key terminology mappings:

Paper SystemElectronic EquivalentDescription
Master Batch Record (MBR)Master RecipeProduct name, formulas, equipment requirements, sequence of activities, BoM
Production Batch RecordControl RecipeMBR dispatched for execution with schedule, specific quantities, batch instance data
Electronic Production RecordEPRData and information created or entered during Control Recipe execution; may span multiple systems/databases
Batch (Production) ReportData ReportHuman-readable output for review, disposition, investigation, audit, and analysis

S2.2 GxP-Relevant Data Considerations

Systems must be capable of reconstruction of GxP-relevant data in appropriate formats. Key data elements to define include production record data requirements, data audit trails, security and user rights, master data and metadata, and time zone/timestamp reconciliation methods.

Audit Trail Terminology

Data audit trails — as required by various regulations — record operator actions that create, modify, or delete GMP records during normal operations, and must be clearly distinguished from system technical logs and other event logs. The data audit trail provides electronic equivalency to striking out data on paper: recording the original and new values, the user, the timestamp, and in some cases, the reason for the change.

Audit Trail Review

"Audit trail review is similar to assessing cross-outs on paper when reviewing data. Personnel responsible for record review under CGMP should review the audit trails that capture changes to data associated with the record as they review the rest of the record." — FDA Guidance on Data Integrity

Key FDA/MHRA guidance principles:

  • Review frequency for audit trails should match review frequency for the underlying data
  • Risk assessment should determine review frequency where regulations do not specify
  • Review need not include every system activity (log-on/off, keystrokes)
  • Exception reporting (a validated search tool identifying abnormal data or actions) is an acceptable approach
  • Reviewers must have sufficient knowledge and system access to review relevant audit trails, raw data, and metadata

S2.3 EPR Data Types and ALCOA+

ALCOA+ principles (Attributable, Legible, Contemporaneous, Original, Accurate, plus Complete, Consistent, Enduring, Available) must be applied to EPR data. Only records and data required by applicable regulations are considered GxP electronic records within an EPR.

Systems across the manufacturing domain that may generate or hold EPR data include: Document Management Systems, Supply Chain Management, MES, Data Historians, ERP, Process Control Systems (SCADA/DCS), and LIMS.

S2.4 Data Capturing, Processing, and Output

Data Input: Master recipes are created from multiple data sources; transformation from paper to electronic form requires verification of equivalency. ALCOA+ principles apply.

Data Processing: Key factors include verified rounding rules, calculation definitions, alerts, alarms, and specific events that may automatically create data or initiate actions. Audit trails and data review procedures are essential.

Data Output: Verified methods must generate reports from EPRs presenting all required information accurately in timely, human-readable form. Interface design, development, and verification requires specific attention; early involvement of interface partners is recommended.

S2.5 Review by Exception (RBE)

RBE screens manufacturing data through verified system functionality to create focused review reports that include all critical process exceptions while reducing the need to review in-tolerance data. RBE:

  • Does not eliminate or change data in EPRs
  • Is a verified extension of existing report-generation functionality
  • Filters EPR data presented to personnel, including all critical exceptions or deviations
  • Is applied to well-understood processes with operational experience
  • Requires that even when no exceptions occur, a report is always generated and examined by approvers

S2.6 Technology Considerations

Cloud Computing: Edge cloud (physically closer service provider) can mitigate risks of real-time process automation interruption. The end user is always ultimately responsible for determining and maintaining the validated state of cloud-based systems, regardless of cloud configuration.

Blockchain: Blockchain's distributed, immutable ledger characteristics make it a candidate for audit trail implementations. Every node verifies each data entry; transaction data is not centrally stored but distributed across designated nodes. This effectively creates a write-once, read-only data storage implementation.

中文解析：電子批次記錄 (eBR)

eBR vs. 傳統紙本批次記錄

電子批次記錄（eBR / Electronic Batch Record）是 EPR 的輸出報告形式。GAMP 5 的 ISA-88 術語體系幫助我們理解這個架構：

  • Master Recipe = 你的配方/製程指令（相當於 MBR）
  • Control Recipe = 針對特定批次的 MBR 實例（相當於 Production Batch Record 的指令部分）
  • EPR = 執行過程中產生的所有數據（分散在多個系統中）
  • Batch Report = 彙整給 QA 審查/放行的人類可讀文件（就是我們說的 eBR 或 eDHR）

重要區分：EPR 是數據的儲存，Batch Report 是審查用的呈現形式。兩者之間的轉換（report generation）本身需要被驗證。

CDMO 導入 eBR 的關鍵挑戰

當 CDMO 為客戶產品導入電子批次記錄時，稽核員特別關注以下問題：

  • 數據所有權：批次數據最終歸客戶還是 CDMO？數據遷移或合約終止時如何處理？
  • Master Recipe 控管：客戶提供的配方如何安全地匯入 MES？版本控制如何確保？
  • 跨系統完整性：當 ERP、MES、LIMS 各自保存一部分 EPR 數據時，如何確保整份 eBR 的完整性（completeness）？
  • 稽核軌跡範圍：所有 GMP 相關操作（修改、刪除、電子簽名）都必須被記錄，且與系統技術日誌明確區分。

21 CFR Part 11 / EU Annex 11 的核心要求

兩個法規的共同要求核心：

  • 稽核軌跡（Audit Trail）：必須記錄誰、何時、修改了什麼（原值 vs. 新值）
  • 電子簽名（Electronic Signature）：與手寫簽名法律效力相同；必須包含姓名、日期時間、簽名意義（例如：審查/批准）
  • 記錄保護：記錄必須防止未經授權的修改（access control + audit trail 雙重保護）
  • 可讀性與可存取性：在保存期間內必須保持可存取且人類可讀

稽核員的 483 觀察重點：「Audit trail is not reviewed as part of batch record review.」— 這是最常見的 eBR 系統缺失。

Review by Exception (RBE) — 實際意義

傳統做法：QA 人員審閱整份批次記錄，包括所有在允差內的製程數據。

RBE 做法：系統自動篩選，只把超出規格、需要人工判斷的例外項目呈現給 QA 審查。正常的數據不需要人眼逐一確認。

好處：大幅提高審查效率；風險：RBE 篩選邏輯本身必須經過嚴格驗證，否則可能遺漏真正的問題。

查廠重點：即使批次完全沒有例外，RBE 報告也必須被產生並由授權人員審核（不能「沒有例外 = 不需要簽名」）。

Cloud EPR 驗證狀態維護責任

GAMP 5 明確聲明：即使系統部署在雲端，終端使用者（即藥廠）仍對驗證狀態負最終責任。這對使用 SaaS MES 的公司影響深遠：

  • 供應商的軟體更新需要評估對驗證狀態的衝擊
  • 必須在供應商合約中明確服務水準協議（SLA）和資料完整性責任
  • 需要建立監控機制，確保雲端系統的可用性符合生產需求

Appendix S3 — End User Applications Including Spreadsheets (p361–p370)

S3.1 Introduction

End user applications — spreadsheets, small databases, statistical applications, and other small applications — present particular compliance challenges in GxP environments. Spreadsheets tend to be the most under-documented systems because:

  • Users regard them as part of the desktop environment
  • Users may not understand or be aware of quality procedures
  • The ease with which applications can be built without formal training
  • The significant data processing power they can have

The level and rigor of specification and verification applied to end user applications should be based on risk, complexity, novelty, and intended use.

S3.2 Application Types

Disposable Spreadsheets

Used in the same way as a hand calculator — results are calculated and the electronic copy is not retained. The calculation result must be printed, labeled, and signed (or saved to a static format with an external electronic signature). The arithmetic manipulation performed must be clearly documented. Calculations used to process GxP data should be verified — this means confirming the formulas are correct, not testing native spreadsheet functions.

Spreadsheets Retained as Documents

When used to both record GxP data and manipulate it, spreadsheets should be managed as documents. Calculations should be verified and fully explained. Control options include: internal security options (password-protecting cells), storing in a secure directory, or managing in an EDMS. If adequate control cannot be achieved, a static version (secure PDF or hardcopy) should be the primary record.

Spreadsheets as Databases

Using spreadsheets as GxP databases presents significant risk because:

  • Limited or no capability to restrict user data editing
  • No native audit trail support
  • Every save creates an entirely new database copy — code changes may go unnoticed

Where audit trails are required, use of spreadsheets is inadvisable as a general rule. A proper database application is a far better alternative.

Template Applications

Template solutions where data is subjected to standard manipulation require careful consideration of:

  • Verified calculations
  • Version control and effective change management
  • Access control (ideally, all cells except data entry fields should be locked)
  • Macro management (macros are custom software — even keystroke-captured macros contain VBA code)
  • Integration testing for multi-module sheets with cell links between worksheets
  • Electronic record controls for retained output files

S3.3 GAMP Category Assignment

The underlying spreadsheet tool (e.g., Excel) is Category 1. Spreadsheets themselves span a continuum of Categories 3, 4, and 5:

  • Category 3 — Simple native function calculations (e.g., calculating mean and SD using built-in functions)
  • Category 4 — Moderate complexity with configuration elements, e.g., simple Boolean logic (IF branches based on user input)
  • Category 5 — Custom macros, sophisticated nested logic, or lookup functions

Note: For end user applications, Category 4 focuses on complexity rather than configurability (the standard GAMP definition).

S3.4 Risk-Based Controls

Four control dimensions apply:

  • Degree of Verification — Complexity determines rigor; macros require functional testing; logical branches require multiple logic path testing
  • Security Control — Combination of infrastructure controls (restricted directory access) and application-level controls (cell password protection). GxP data should be saved to a secure, backed-up drive.
  • Change Control — All GxP end user applications must be subject to change control; EDMS or code library tools support version management
  • Infrastructure Control — The spreadsheet environment (e.g., Excel installation) is Category 1 software; IT manages its verification and compatibility with the standard desktop build

S3.5 Examples of Typical Approaches

ExampleImpact / ComplexityRecommended Approach
Content uniformity calculation templateHigh / LowRS + third-party verification of calculations + security + change control
Training attendance spreadsheetLow / LowStandard electronic document controls only
Desktop database for toxicology studyHigh / MediumFull Category 4: Validation Plan, RS, FS/DS, traceability, testing, report
Clinical study statistics with VBA macrosHigh / HighFull Category 5: All above + rigorous macro and branch testing
SPC spreadsheet with complex logic/lookupsLow / HighThird-party verification of calculations + change control + security
Label disposition tracking databaseMedium / MediumAbbreviated Category 4: Combined RS/FS/DS + testing + report + change control

中文解析：試算表驗證

FDA 483 最常見觀察項目：未驗證的 Excel 試算表

這是製藥界最普遍的合規問題之一。常見的 483 觀察文字是：

"Laboratory controls do not include the validation of test methods and associated computerized systems. Specifically, the spreadsheet used to calculate [product X assay results] was not validated."

問題的根源在於：試算表被視為「日常辦公工具」而非「電腦化系統」，因此沒有納入 CSV 程式管控。

GxP 試算表最低文件要求（實務清單）

根據 GAMP 5 S3 附錄，以下是風險導向的最低文件要求：

  • 需求規格（RS）：說明試算表的用途、輸入數據類型、計算目的、輸出格式（通常一頁即可）
  • 公式驗證記錄：列出所有儲存格公式（可列印公式視圖），由第三方確認公式邏輯正確
  • 測試案例：至少包括正常值、邊界值、已知結果的樣本計算
  • 版本控制：版本號、修改日期、修改者、審核者，儲存於安全目錄
  • 存取控制：非輸入欄位應鎖定，防止意外修改
  • 變更控制程序：任何修改都需要重新驗證並記錄影響評估

Macro（巨集）的特殊風險

許多使用者認為「錄製巨集」只是記錄按鍵動作，不是真正的程式設計。但 GAMP 5 明確指出：即使是錄製的巨集，背後也是 VBA 程式碼。

這意味著：

  • 含有巨集的試算表必須視為 Category 5 軟體
  • 所有邏輯分支（IF 判斷）都需要測試
  • 巨集碼需要版本控制（不能只控制試算表本身）
  • 如果 VBA 碼使用了外部引用或 API，還需要整合測試

建議做法：如果業務需求需要複雜巨集，評估是否應直接使用正式驗證過的系統（例如 LIMS、MES）會更安全。

試算表作為資料庫：為何危險

GAMP 5 非常明確地說：需要稽核軌跡的 GxP 資料，不應使用試算表儲存。原因：

  • Excel 沒有原生稽核軌跡（Track Changes 功能不符合 GxP 要求）
  • 每次儲存都會覆蓋整個檔案，無法追蹤誰改了哪一個儲存格
  • 存取控制薄弱，無法有效防止未授權修改

如果目前有用 Excel 管理 GxP 資料（例如穩定性數據表、OOS 追蹤表），建議納入風險評估，優先考慮遷移到有原生稽核軌跡的系統。

CDMO 情境：QC 計算試算表驗證策略

在 CDMO 環境，實驗室經常使用 Excel 計算含量均一度、效價、降解物等。建議策略：

  1. 建立試算表盤點清單（Inventory），依 GxP 影響分類
  2. 高影響（產品放行決策相關）→ 正式 RS + 驗證 + 版本控制
  3. 低影響（研究用輔助計算）→ 文件化說明計算目的即可
  4. 考慮使用 EDMS 管控所有高影響試算表，確保版本完整性
  5. 定期（例如每年）審查盤點清單，確認沒有未管控的新增試算表

Appendix S4 — Patch and Update Management (p371–p373)

S4.1 Introduction

Software patches, hot fixes, and service pack upgrades are a frequent operational reality due to:

  • Security vulnerabilities in widely integrated/connected applications (theft of personal data or IP; theft of computing power for malicious software agents)
  • Defects in complex software requiring supplier-issued fixes for critical processes
  • Periodic supplier software updates

Appropriate patch management is particularly important to maintain compliance and fitness for intended use of GxP regulated computerized systems.

S4.2 Approach to Patch and Update Management

Regulated companies should develop a patch and upgrade management approach that:

  • Provides criteria for determining enterprise threat levels and urgency for applying patches
  • Allows flexibility considering both enterprise risk and compliance risk to regulated systems
  • Generates configuration records showing version and patch level at any point in the system life cycle
  • Generates change records describing what testing was done (may include enterprise-level and/or application-specific testing)

The Core Tension: Security vs. GxP Compliance

Many patches address urgent security vulnerabilities where exploits may already be known or imminent. The time required to evaluate and test all affected GxP regulated computerized systems prior to implementation may increase risk to data integrity if a threat is actively being exploited.

Regulated companies must develop a risk-management approach that considers both regulatory compliance (validated state) and the level of threat to the system and wider computing environment.

Quality Unit Role

The quality unit should approve the process for risk evaluation of all patches but is generally not involved in individual patch assessments. If the QU is involved in an assessment, they should not have final say in how the patch is managed. Enterprise risk typically has to be given precedence over GxP risk. If a patch must be applied that carries undesirable GxP risk, business process owners and the quality unit should work together to mitigate through verification activities, temporary business process changes, or other approaches.

Patch Strategies (Figure 49.1)

StrategyApproachEnterprise RiskGxP Risk
Strategy 1 (Most Aggressive)Apply immediately enterprise-wide; perform post-implementation testingLowestHighest (limited pre-testing)
Strategy 2Apply to non-GxP systems immediately; apply to GxP systems after abbreviated testingLow-MediumMedium
Strategy 3Apply to all systems after normal change management testing cycleMedium-HighLower
Strategy 4 (Most Conservative)Apply only after full application-specific impact assessment and testingHighestLowest

The process should define criteria and required approvals for selecting each strategy, and include notification to affected parties (including the help desk) after patch application.

S4.3 Configuration Management

Accurate configuration management records support patch management by enabling:

  • Planning — Patches often must be applied sequentially; knowing the current patch level is prerequisite
  • Interoperability — Systems running at multiple sites or interfacing with external applications may require matching patch levels
  • Troubleshooting — Thorough knowledge of configuration is critical to understanding incidents
  • Data Integrity — Demonstrating security gaps have been closed and when this was achieved

Configuration records should be sufficient to show the current as-built state and when patches or upgrades have been applied.

中文解析：補丁管理的兩難困境

核心衝突：立即打補丁 vs. 先測試

這是許多製藥廠 IT/品保部門的日常矛盾：

  • IT 資安立場：Windows/Linux 發布高危漏洞補丁 → 應在 24-48 小時內部署，否則系統暴露在攻擊風險中
  • GxP 合規立場：任何對已驗證系統的變更都需要影響評估和測試，怎麼可能 48 小時內完成？

GAMP 5 的答案是：企業資安風險通常優先於 GxP 法規風險。關鍵是要有一個被 QA 批准的程序，規定在不同威脅等級下採取不同策略，並且記錄決策依據。

實務補丁策略設計

建議將補丁分為三類來管理：

  1. 緊急安全補丁（Critical Security）：CVSS 評分 ≥ 9.0 或已有主動攻擊 → 採用 Strategy 1/2，事後補齊測試記錄；通知幫服台和使用者；QA 記錄風險決策
  2. 一般安全補丁（High/Medium）：計畫到下個維護窗口，在非 GxP 環境先測試 1-2 週後推送 GxP 系統 → 採用 Strategy 2/3
  3. 功能更新 / Service Pack：完整的影響評估 + 回歸測試 + 變更控制 → 採用 Strategy 3/4

查廠重點：補丁管理 SOP 的必備要素

稽核員在檢查補丁管理時會尋找：

  • 是否有 QA 批准的補丁管理 SOP，且涵蓋 GxP 系統
  • 每個補丁是否有影響評估記錄（即使決定「不測試」也要記錄理由）
  • 配置管理記錄是否能顯示「某系統在某日期的補丁水準」
  • 緊急補丁後是否有「補後測試」記錄（retrospective testing documentation）
  • 跨站點系統是否維持相同補丁水準（interoperability 問題）

組態管理記錄的實際重要性

當生產系統發生資料異常或系統故障時，調查的第一步通常是查詢「事件發生時系統的確切版本和補丁水準」。如果組態管理記錄不完整，就無法確定是否因為某個補丁引入了問題，也無法向稽核員證明系統在事件前後的配置狀態。

建議工具：使用 CMDB（Configuration Management Database）或在變更控制系統中強制記錄每次補丁後的版本快照。

OT/IT 融合環境（SCADA、DCS）的特殊挑戰

生產環境的控制系統（例如無菌灌裝線的 PLC/SCADA）往往有更長的補丁延遲，因為：

  • 設備供應商（如 Rockwell、Siemens）需要先測試補丁對控制邏輯的影響再發布認可版本
  • 生產設備通常 24/7 運行，難以安排停機維護窗口
  • 某些老舊設備的作業系統（如 Windows XP embedded）已停止更新

對策：針對 OT 環境建立補償控制措施（compensating controls），例如網路隔離（air gap / DMZ）、入侵偵測系統，並在補丁管理 SOP 中明確 OT 環境的特殊處理規則。

Appendix S5 — Retired (p375)

Appendix S5 — Managing Quality within an Outsourced IS/IT Environment (Retired)

Appendix S5 of GAMP 5, 1st Edition covered the management of quality within an outsourced IT/IS environment. In the 2nd Edition, this content has been withdrawn and substantially revised. The updated material has been renamed and relocated to Appendix M11, which provides current guidance on managing outsourced IT/IS environments in the context of GxP computerized systems.

This appendix entry is retained as a placeholder to maintain the numbered appendix sequence (S1 through S6) and to direct readers to the current guidance location.

附錄 S5 — 已撤銷（Retired）

GAMP 5 第一版的 S5 附錄涵蓋「外包 IS/IT 環境中的品質管理」。在第二版中，此內容已被撤銷並重新修訂，改名為 Appendix M11。

如需查閱 IT 外包的 GxP 合規管理指引，請參閱 Appendix M11。S5 的空缺是刻意保留，以維持附錄編號序列（S1–S6）的連貫性。

Appendix S6 — Organizational Change (p377–p381)

S6.1 Introduction

There has been a global trend within the life sciences sector toward organizational consolidation and outsourcing of services. Additional challenges from the COVID-19 pandemic and digital transformation have further stimulated agile ways of working. This appendix considers the impact of organizational change on GxP regulated computerized systems and provides guidance for ensuring continued compliance and system availability.

S6.2 Initiators for Change

  • Internal reorganization
  • Being acquired by another company
  • Divesting part of an organization to a third party (including offshoring and outsourcing)
  • Supplier or service provider ceasing to trade

S6.3 Scope and Impact of Change

Organizational change may apply to any aspect of the system supply chain — regulated companies, system integrators, base product and infrastructure suppliers. Change can occur during any stage of a computerized system's life cycle. Aspects to consider include:

  • Changes in the business process the computerized system supports
  • Changes in how an existing system is used
  • Moving systems from one location to another
  • New or different regulatory and compliance requirements
  • Impact on regulated records and associated signatures
  • Changes in how security (physical and logical access control) is handled
  • Clarification of where primary data is located and who the system/process owners are
  • Timing and need to audit a reorganized supplier
  • Impact on service level agreements
  • Maintaining expertise on systems (with both supplier and regulated company)
  • Impact on support contracts and system implementation projects
  • Changes in personnel and/or individual responsibilities

S6.4 Organizational Challenges

  • Maintaining multiple/parallel systems for the same business process
  • Developing interfaces between multiple/parallel systems
  • Migrating data or subsets of data from one system to another
  • Maintaining data sets for third parties for extended periods (format, conversion, discarding decisions)
  • Systems likely to be retired
  • Location of life cycle records and inspection support on an ongoing basis
  • Maintaining multiple/parallel compliance practices and documentation
  • Harmonizing compliance practices and training in new practices
  • Changes in regulatory expectations and subsequent impact on life cycle activities
  • Change management and configuration management across changed organizations
  • Increased focus on incident monitoring during the transition period

S6.5 Outsourcing Considerations

Where organizational change involves outsourcing, additionally consider:

  • Whether the regulated company continues to own the equipment or whether this transfers to the outsource company
  • Whether the outsource organization QMS is used or the regulated company QMS
  • Need to both initially and periodically audit the outsource organization (scope: both compliance and financial)

See Appendix M11 for further details on managing outsourced IT/IS environments.

S6.6 Loss of a Supplier

Where a supplier ceases to trade, consider:

  • Ensuring business continuity plans are established and accurate for related systems
  • Invoking any escrow agreements to gain access to application source code
  • Record and system migration options
  • Retrieval of regulated company owned components (hardware, software, records, documentation)

S6.7 Risk Assessment and Project Status Scenarios

Project StatusCompany AcquisitionCompany MergerSupplier Insolvency
Not StartedOn hold pending management reviewOn hold pending management reviewCancelled
In Progress — Early in Life CycleOn hold pending management reviewOn hold pending management reviewCancelled
In Progress — Late in Life CycleOn hold pending management reviewContinuedOn hold pending management review
Approaching Go-LiveOn hold pending management review (priority decision)ContinuedOn hold pending management review

S6.8 Affected Stakeholders

Agreement must be reached between all affected organizations. Representatives typically involved include:

  • Business process owners
  • Compliance / Quality / Regulatory
  • Legal
  • IT and Engineering
  • Purchasing groups and in some cases Finance

Key documentation update tasks for stakeholders:

  • Business process documentation
  • Policies, procedures, work instructions, test methods
  • Training materials and user manuals
  • Batch records (if applicable)
  • Archived records/data
  • Contracts, system interfaces, validation/qualification records
  • Record retention schedules

Training requirements must be evaluated against all changes made to QMS, ways of working, or documentation — at both organizational and system levels.

中文解析：CSV 程式的組織變更管理

為什麼組織變更對 CSV 是高風險事件

已驗證的電腦化系統存在於特定的組織環境中：有特定的系統負責人、SOP 持有人、IT 支援人員、供應商關係管理者。當組織發生重大變更時，這些角色可能在同一時間全部改變，而系統本身（硬體、軟體、配置）可能完全不變——但它的「驗證狀態維護」所依賴的所有人和程序都斷裂了。

IT 部門重組 / 外包的真實挑戰

想像一個製藥廠決定把 IT 基礎設施外包給第三方 IT 服務商：

  • 原本的內部 IT 團隊（知道 MES 系統的所有歷史決策）離職了
  • 新的外包供應商不了解 GxP 要求，只按照一般 IT SLA 操作
  • 系統的補丁管理、備份驗證、存取控制管理現在由不熟悉 GxP 的人執行

這種情況會導致：驗證狀態的逐漸侵蝕（validated state drift）——系統還在跑，但沒有人確保它還在「驗證狀態」下運行。

CDMO 在 M&A 情境下的特殊風險

當 CDMO 被大型藥廠收購，或自己收購其他 CDMO 時，常見的 GxP 風險包括：

  • 系統整合壓力：IT 急著整合系統（例如統一 ERP），但整合本身就是對已驗證系統的重大變更，需要重新驗證
  • SOP 衝突：兩個組織各自有不同的 CSV SOP，需要決定遵循哪一套，並訓練所有人員
  • 供應商審計重新啟動：收購後，新的母公司可能有不同的供應商審計要求，需要重新審計所有關鍵系統供應商
  • 記錄保留責任轉移：客戶的批次記錄、驗證文件的保留責任在合約轉移後如何確保連續性？

供應商倒閉的緊急應對

這是最難預先準備但後果最嚴重的情境。關鍵行動清單：

  1. 立即啟動業務連續性計畫（如果有的話）
  2. 執行軟體源碼托管（Escrow）協議：如果合約中有 source code escrow 條款，立即申請釋出
  3. 下載所有支援文件：技術手冊、驗證文件、系統配置記錄——供應商的伺服器可能隨時關閉
  4. 評估現有維護合約：年度維護費已付但供應商倒閉，這是法律問題也是合規問題
  5. 決定替換或維持策略：如果系統還要繼續使用，需要找有能力維護該系統的第三方廠商

組織變更的 CSV 影響評估框架

建議在任何重大組織變更發生時，執行以下 CSV 影響評估：

  1. 盤點清單：列出所有受影響的 GxP 電腦化系統，標記其 GxP 影響等級
  2. 角色責任重新對應：系統負責人、SOP 持有人、IT 聯絡人在新組織結構下由誰負責？
  3. 程序文件審查：涉及組織架構、人員職責的 SOP 是否需要更新？
  4. 訓練需求評估：新的負責人員是否已接受系統特定訓練？
  5. 合約審查：系統支援合約、許可協議在組織變更後是否仍有效？
  6. 過渡期監控強化：在組織過渡期間，提高事件監控頻率，設立快速升級機制

Section Summary — 章節總結：附錄 S1–S6 核心要點

  • S1 — ASTM E2500: GAMP 5 and ASTM E2500 share the same science- and risk-based philosophy. ASTM E2500 focuses on manufacturing equipment; GAMP 5 covers all computerized systems. "Verification" replaces separate IQ/OQ as an integrated activity; the key requirement is evidence that critical-to-quality requirements have been met. ／ 兩者核心一致：以病人風險為中心、借用供應商測試、減少重複活動。術語可以不同，但文件證據必須充分。
  • S2 — Electronic Production Records: EPR ≠ Batch Report — EPR is distributed data; the batch report is the human-readable output. Data audit trails are mandatory; they must be reviewed as part of the batch review process. The end user is always ultimately responsible for validated state, even for cloud-hosted systems. ／ 稽核軌跡必須作為批次記錄審查的一部分；RBE 是合規的，但篩選邏輯本身需要被驗證。
  • S3 — Spreadsheets: Unvalidated GxP spreadsheets are a top FDA 483 observation. Minimum requirements: formula verification, version control, access control, change control. Macros = Category 5 software. Spreadsheets with audit trail requirements should be replaced with proper database systems. ／ Excel 不是 GxP 的安全選項，除非有完整的驗證和控制措施。含巨集的試算表等同 Category 5 軟體。
  • S4 — Patch Management: Enterprise security risk generally takes precedence over GxP risk. Quality unit approves the patch management process but not individual patch decisions. A documented risk-based decision for each patch — including the choice of strategy and testing scope — is required. Configuration records must show patch levels at any point in time. ／ 有「QA 批准程序 + 風險記錄」才能合規地快速打補丁。
  • S5 — Retired: Content from GAMP 5 1st Edition S5 (Managing Quality within an Outsourced IS/IT Environment) has been moved to Appendix M11 in the 2nd Edition. ／ 相關內容已移至 Appendix M11。
  • S6 — Organizational Change: M&A, outsourcing, and supplier loss all threaten validated state. A CSV-specific organizational change impact assessment is essential. Training requirements must be re-evaluated. Stakeholders from Business, QA, Legal, IT, and Finance must all be engaged. ／ 組織變更不只是 HR 的事——它直接威脅已驗證系統的合規狀態，需要 QA 主動介入管理。
ISPE GAMP 5, 2nd Edition | p383–p404 | Section 08b

Learning Objectives — 學習目標

  1. Identify the key regulatory references cited in GAMP 5 (FDA 21 CFR Part 11, EU Annex 11, ICH Q9/Q10) and understand why each is foundational to computerized system validation. / 識別 GAMP 5 引用的核心法規文件，理解各自在電腦化系統驗證中的基礎地位。
  2. Distinguish between "validation," "qualification," and "verification" as defined in the GAMP 5 glossary, and apply the correct term in validation documentation. / 區辨 GAMP 5 詞彙表中「驗證」、「確效」與「查核」三個術語的精確定義，並在驗證文件中正確使用。
  3. Explain the roles of "regulated company," "supplier," "system owner," and "process owner," and describe how responsibilities differ. / 說明受管制公司、供應商、系統擁有者及流程擁有者的角色分工與責任差異。
  4. Use the GAMP 5 glossary and reference list to correctly cite standards and define key terms during regulatory inspections or validation document preparation. / 在法規查核或驗證文件撰寫時，能正確引用 GAMP 5 標準並定義關鍵術語。

中文解說 — 參考文獻導讀

核心法規文件解析 — 為什麼要引用這些標準？

GAMP 5 第二版的附錄 G1 列出超過 100 份引用文件。對 CDMO 實務工作者來說，最重要的是以下三個法規核心：

21 CFR Part 11（美國 FDA）
管轄範圍：電子記錄 (Electronic Records) 與電子簽章 (Electronic Signatures)。核心要求：電子記錄必須可信、可靠、等同於紙本記錄，且電子簽章具法律效力。
常見誤解：Part 11 不是要求「所有系統必須有電子簽章」，而是當你選擇使用電子記錄時，必須符合這些要求。

EU GMP Annex 11（歐盟）
管轄範圍：GMP 範圍內的電腦化系統。與 21 CFR Part 11 的關鍵差異：Annex 11 涵蓋更廣的系統生命週期概念，包括供應商評估、驗收測試、定期回顧 (Periodic Review)，以及資料完整性要求。
重點：Annex 11 在某些方面比 21 CFR Part 11 要求更嚴格，例如明確要求供應商稽核。

ICH Q9（品質風險管理）
GAMP 5 風險導向方法的科學基礎。ICH Q9 提供了「危害」、「風險」、「嚴重性」、「可偵測性」等詞彙的官方定義，GAMP 5 詞彙表直接引用這些定義。
重要性：當你在驗證文件中進行風險評估時，你的方法論必須能對應到 ICH Q9 的框架。

21 CFR Part 11 vs. EU Annex 11 — 相同但不相同

比較項目21 CFR Part 11EU Annex 11
主管機關美國 FDA歐盟 EMA ／ 成員國監管機構
適用範圍電子記錄與電子簽章GMP 電腦化系統（全生命週期）
供應商稽核未明確要求明確要求評估
定期回顧未明文規定明確要求 Periodic Review
資料備份間接要求明確規定備份與還原測試
審計軌跡要求稽核軌跡要求稽核軌跡（更詳細）

同時銷售 FDA 和 EU 市場的 CDMO，必須同時符合兩套要求，取較嚴格者為準。

ICH Q10 — 製藥品質系統的整體框架

ICH Q10（製藥品質系統）與 ICH Q9 相輔相成，Q10 描述了在整個產品生命週期中維持品質系統的要求，GAMP 5 的 CSV 工作必須在 Q10 框架下運作。

ASTM E2500-20 同樣重要：它提供了「Verification（查核）」作為 CSV 替代路徑的標準依據，是 ISPE Vol. 5 C&Q 指南的重要基礎。

GAMP 5 引用文件的使用原則

  • 當文件引用「ICH Q9 [14]」這樣的格式時，方括號內的數字就是 G1 附錄中的編號。
  • 在您自己的驗證文件中引用 GAMP 5 時，正確格式為：「ISPE GAMP 5 Second Edition, 2022, www.ispe.org」
  • 稽核員可能要求您證明您了解所引用文件的具體要求，不只是列在參考文獻中而已。
  • PIC/S PI 011-3（電腦化系統指南）適用於歐盟 GMP 稽核，是 GAMP 5 之外的重要補充。

CDMO 實務應用 — 在驗證文件中正確引用法規

驗證主計畫 (VMP) 中的法規依據章節：

  • 列出適用的所有法規：21 CFR Part 11, EU GMP Annex 11, ICH Q9, ICH Q10
  • 說明各法規的適用市場（美國、歐盟、日本等）
  • 引用 GAMP 5 作為方法論指導依據

風險評估文件中：

  • 明確聲明風險評估方法依據 ICH Q9 原則
  • 定義使用的術語（Harm, Hazard, Risk, Severity, Detectability）

常見稽核問題：
「您的 CSV 方法是基於哪個指南？」— 回答：GAMP 5 2nd Edition (2022), supported by EU GMP Annex 11 and 21 CFR Part 11.

稽核員常問的縮寫問題

在 FDA 或 EU 稽查時，稽核員可能會隨機詢問縮寫含義，以確認您的 CSV 知識基礎：

  • "What is COTS software under GAMP 5?" — 商業現成軟體，已有廣泛商業用戶驗證其適用性，可簡化驗證策略。
  • "What is the difference between URS and FS?" — URS 描述使用者業務需求；FS 描述系統如何實現這些需求。
  • "What does GxP cover?" — GMP, GLP, GCP, GDP, GVP 等所有適用法規規範的總稱。
  • "What is ALCOA+?" — 資料完整性的九項原則：可歸屬、易讀、同步、原始、準確、完整、一致、持久、可取用。

CSA vs. CSV — 新舊方法的關鍵差異

FDA 在 2022 年推出 CSA（Computer Software Assurance）指南草案，作為傳統 CSV 的補充方向：

  • CSV：重視文件完整性，IQ/OQ/PQ 三階段，測試腳本詳盡
  • CSA：強調「關鍵思維」(critical thinking)，風險導向決定測試範圍，減少不必要文件
  • GAMP 5 2nd Edition 同時支援兩種方法，讓受管制公司依風險選擇適合的方式。

Appendix G2, Section 53.2 — Definitions / 名詞定義

G2 — Definitions (A–M)

Acceptance Criteria
Source: ASTM E2500 [8]
The criteria that a system, component must satisfy in order to be accepted by a user, customer or other authorized entity.
Acceptance Test
Source: IEEE [96]
Testing conducted to determine whether or not a system satisfies its acceptance criteria and to enable the customer to determine whether or not to accept the system.
Application Software
Source: ISO/IEC 13066 [97]
Software or a program that is specific to the solution of an application problem.
Audit
Source: ISO 9000 [1]
Systematic, independent, and documented process for obtaining audit evidence and evaluating it objectively to determine the extent to which agreed criteria are fulfilled.
Batch Record
Source: GAMP 5
The set of records of all relevant process information in any physical or electronic format.
Blockchain
Source: Merriam-Webster [98]
A digital database containing information (such as records of financial transactions) that can be simultaneously used and shared within a large decentralized, publicly accessible network.
Business Continuity Planning
Source: ISO/IEC 27031:2011 [99]
Documented procedures that guide organizations to respond, recover, resume, and restore to a pre-defined level of operation following disruption.
Calibration
Source: ICH Q7 [100]
The demonstration that a particular instrument or device produces results within specified limits by comparison with those produced by a reference or traceable standard over an appropriate range of measurements.
Change Management
Source: ICH Q10 [21]
A systematic approach to proposing, evaluating, approving, implementing and reviewing changes.
Commercial Off-the-Shelf Software (COTS)
Source: IEEE [96]
Software defined by a market-driven need, commercially available, and whose fitness for use has been demonstrated by a broad spectrum of commercial users. Also known as COTS.
Computer System
Source: IEEE [96]
A system containing one or more computers and associated software.
Computerized System
Source: GAMP 5
A broad range of systems including, but not limited to, automated manufacturing equipment, automated laboratory equipment, process control and process analytical, manufacturing execution, laboratory information management, manufacturing resource planning, clinical trials data management, vigilance and document management systems. The computerized system consists of the hardware, software, and network components, together with the controlled functions and associated documentation.
Computerized System Validation
Source: GAMP 5
Achieving and maintaining compliance with applicable GxP regulations and fitness for intended use by:
  • The adoption of principles, approaches, and life cycle activities within the framework of validation plans and reports
  • The application of appropriate operational controls throughout the life of the system
Critical Process Parameter (CPP)
Source: ICH Q8 [84]
A process parameter whose variability has an impact on a critical quality attribute and therefore should be monitored or controlled to ensure the process produces the desired quality.
Critical Quality Attribute (CQA)
Source: ICH Q8 [84]
A physical, chemical, biological or microbiological property or characteristic that should be within an appropriate limit, range, or distribution to ensure the desired product quality.
Detectability
Source: ICH Q9 [14]
The ability to discover or determine the existence, presence, or fact of a hazard.
Factory Acceptance Test (FAT)
Source: IEEE [96]
An Acceptance Test in the Supplier's factory, usually involving the Customer. See also Acceptance Test. Contrast to Site Acceptance Test.
GxP Compliance
Source: GAMP 5
Meeting all applicable pharmaceutical and associated life-science regulatory requirements.
GxP Regulated Computerized System
Source: GAMP 5
Computerized systems that are subject to GxP regulations. The regulated company must ensure that such systems comply with the appropriate regulations.
GxP Regulation
Source: GAMP 5
The underlying international pharmaceutical requirements, such as those set forth in the US FD&C Act, US PHS Act, FDA regulations, EU Directives, Japanese regulations, or other applicable national legislation or regulations under which a company operates. These include but are not limited to:
  • Good Manufacturing Practice (GMP) — pharmaceutical, including API, veterinary, and blood
  • Good Clinical Practice (GCP)
  • Good Laboratory Practice (GLP)
  • Good Distribution Practice (GDP)
  • Good Quality Practice (GQP)
  • Good Pharmacovigilance Practice (GVP)
  • Medical Device Regulations
  • Prescription Drug Marketing Act (PDMA)
Harm
Source: ICH Q9 [14]
Damage to health, including the damage that can occur from loss of product quality or availability.
Hazard
Source: ICH Q9 [14]
The potential source of harm (ISO/IEC Guide 51).
Incident
Source: GAMP 5
Operational event which is not part of standard operation.
Middleware
Source: GAMP 5
Software that provides common services such as communication and data management to software applications beyond those available from the operating system.

中文解說 — 重要定義精析（上半段）

三個最容易混淆的術語辨析

Validation（驗證）vs. Qualification（確效）vs. Verification（查核）

這三個詞在日常中文習慣上常被混用，但在 GAMP 5 中有精確的層次關係：

  • Verification（查核）：ASTM E2500 使用的上位概念，「確認製造系統適合預定用途的系統性方法」，是一個包含所有確認方式的傘狀術語。
  • Validation（驗證）：GAMP 5 對 Computerized System Validation 的定義，強調「達成並維持 GxP 合規及適合預定用途」，涵蓋生命週期全程。
  • Qualification（確效）：特指 IQ/OQ/PQ 等設備或系統的逐階確認活動，是 Validation 的組成部分之一。

簡言之：Verification ⊇ Validation ⊇ Qualification（範圍由大到小）

Computerized System 的正式定義 — 比你想的更廣

GAMP 5 明確定義電腦化系統包括：硬體 + 軟體 + 網路元件 + 受控功能 + 相關文件。

這意味著一台簡單的 PLC 控制器（含其程序邏輯）也算是電腦化系統，需要適當的驗證方法。CDMO 常見的電腦化系統包括：MES、LIMS、EDMS、ERP、DCS/PLC、稱量系統等。

GxP 涵蓋的法規範圍 — 一圖讀懂

縮寫全稱主要適用場域
GMPGood Manufacturing Practice生產製造
GLPGood Laboratory Practice非臨床研究
GCPGood Clinical Practice臨床試驗
GDPGood Distribution Practice配送流通
GVPGood Pharmacovigilance Practice藥物安全監視
GQPGood Quality Practice品質管理

CDMO 主要適用 GMP，但若有承接臨床試驗用藥生產，需同時考慮 GCP 對資料完整性的要求。

ICH Q9 來源術語 — 稽核員最喜歡問的

GAMP 5 詞彙表中有大量術語直接引用 ICH Q9。稽核員常問：

  • Harm（危害）：對健康的損害，包括產品品質或供應可用性損失所造成的損害。
  • Hazard（危險源）：傷害的潛在來源（不等同於 Harm）。
  • Risk = Probability × Severity：發生危害的機率乘以嚴重程度的組合。
  • Detectability（可偵測性）：辨識危險源存在的能力（有助於降低整體風險評分）。

COTS 軟體 — 用超市食品打比方

COTS（商業現成軟體）就像超市販售的現成食品：製造商（供應商）已經大規模生產並通過市場驗證，你（受管制公司）不需要從零建立，但你需要確認它適合你的具體需求（URS），並在你的環境中正確組態。

相反地，自定義開發軟體（Category 5）就像自己從頭烹調，需要完整的開發生命週期管控。

G2 — Definitions (N–Z)

Network
Source: FDA [101]
A system [transmission channels and supporting hardware and software] that connects several remotely located computers via telecommunications.
Periodic Review
Source: GAMP 5
A documented assessment of the documentation, procedures, records, and performance of a computer system to determine whether it is still in a validated state and what actions, if any, are necessary to restore its validated state. The frequency of review is dependent upon the systems complexity, criticality, and rate of change.
Pharmacovigilance
Source: EMA [103]
Science and activities relating to the detection, assessment, understanding and prevention of adverse effects or any other medicine-related problem.
Process
Source: ISO 9000 [1]
Set of interrelated or interacting activities that use inputs to deliver an intended result.
Process Analytical Technology (PAT)
Source: ICH Q8 [84]
A system for designing, analyzing, and controlling manufacturing through timely measurements (i.e., during processing) of critical quality and performance attributes of raw and in-process materials and processes with the goal of ensuring final product quality.
Process Owner
Source: GAMP 5
This is the owner of the business process or processes being managed. The process owner is ultimately responsible for ensuring that the computerized system and its operation is in compliance and fit for intended use in accordance with applicable company Standard Operating Procedures (SOPs). The process owner may also be the system owner. The process owner may be the de facto owner of the data residing on the system (data owner) and therefore, ultimately responsible for the integrity of the data. Process owners are typically the head of the functional unit using the system. (cf. System Owner)
Process Validation
Source: FDA [104]
The collection and evaluation of data, from the process design stage through commercial production, which establishes scientific evidence that a process is capable of consistently delivering quality products.
Product Lifecycle
Source: ICH Q9 [14]
All phases in the life of the product from the initial development through marketing until the product's discontinuation.
Quality (ICH Q9)
Source: ICH Q9 [14]
The degree to which a set of inherent properties of a product, system or process fulfills requirements.
Quality by Design (QbD)
Source: ICH Q8 [84]
A systematic approach to development that begins with predefined objectives and emphasizes product and process understanding and process control, based on sound science and quality risk management.
Quality Management System (QMS)
Source: ISO 9000 [1]
Part of a management system with regard to quality. (A management system is a set of interrelated or interacting elements of an organization to establish policies and objectives, and processes to achieve those objectives.)
Quality Risk Management (QRM)
Source: ICH Q9 [14]
A systematic process for the assessment, control, communication and review of risks to the quality of the drug (medicinal) product across the product lifecycle.
Risk
Source: ICH Q9 [14]
The combination of the probability of occurrence of harm and the severity of that harm (ISO/IEC Guide 51).
Risk Assessment
Source: ICH Q9 [14]
A systematic process of organizing information to support a risk decision to be made within a risk management process. It consists of the identification of hazards and the analysis and evaluation of risks associated with exposure to those hazards.
Risk Management
Source: ICH Q9 [14]
The systematic application of quality management policies, procedures, and practices to the tasks of assessing, controlling, communicating and reviewing risk.
Severity
Source: ICH Q9 [14]
A measure of the possible consequences of a hazard.
Site Acceptance Test (SAT)
Source: IEEE [96]
An Acceptance Test at the Customer's site, usually involving the Customer. See also Acceptance Test, contrast to Factory Acceptance Test.
Software Life Cycle
Source: NIST [81]
Period of time beginning when a software product is conceived and ending when the product is no longer available for use. The software life cycle is typically broken into phases denoting activities such as requirements, design, programming, testing, installation, and operation and maintenance.
Subject Matter Expert (SME)
Source: ASTM E2500 [8]
Those individuals with specific expertise in a particular area or field. Subject Matter Experts should take the lead role in the verification of computerized systems. Subject Matter Expert responsibilities include planning and defining verification strategies, defining acceptance criteria, selection of appropriate test methods, execution of verification tests, and reviewing results.
Supplier
Source: GAMP 5
An organization or individual internal or external to the user associated with the supply and/or support of products or services at any phase throughout a systems life cycle.
System Owner
Source: GAMP 5
The system owner is responsible for the availability, and support and maintenance, of a system, and for the security of the data residing on that system. The system owner is responsible for ensuring that the computerized system is supported and maintained in accordance with applicable company SOPs. The system owner also may be the process owner (e.g., for IT infrastructure systems or systems not directly supporting GxP). For systems supporting regulated processes and maintaining regulated data and records, the ownership of the data resides with the GxP-process owner, not the system owner. (cf. Process Owner)
Testing, Functional
Source: IEEE [96]
Testing that ignores the internal mechanism or structure of a system or component and focuses on the outputs generated in response to selected inputs and execution conditions. Also called black-box testing or input/output driven testing. Contrast with testing, structural.
Testing, Structural
Source: IEEE [96]
Testing that takes into account the internal mechanism [structure] of a system or component. Types include branch testing, path testing, statement testing. Also called white-box testing, glass-box testing, logic driven testing. Contrast with functional testing.
User
Source: GAMP 5
The pharmaceutical customer or user organization contracting a supplier to provide a product. In the context of this document it is not intended to apply only to individuals who use the system, and is synonymous with customer.
Verification
Source: ISO 9000 [1]; ASTM E2500 [8]
(1) Confirmation, through the provision of objective evidence that specified requirements have been fulfilled. (2) A systematic approach to verify that manufacturing systems, acting singly or in combination, are fit for intended use, have been properly installed, and are operating correctly. This is an umbrella term that encompasses all types of approaches to assuring systems are fit for use such as qualification, commissioning and qualification, verification, system validation, or other.

中文解說 — 重要定義精析（下半段）

System Owner vs. Process Owner — 責任分界清單

責任System Owner（系統擁有者）Process Owner（流程擁有者）
主要背景通常來自 IT 或工程部門通常是使用部門主管（QA/生產/實驗室）
核心責任系統可用性、維護、安全業務流程合規與適合預定用途
資料所有權不擁有 GxP 資料擁有受管制資料（Data Owner）
SOP 符合性確保系統維護符合公司 SOP確保系統操作符合 GxP SOP
驗證責任提供技術支援最終驗證核准簽署人

CDMO 實務：一個 LIMS 系統，IT 部門是 System Owner，QC 主管是 Process Owner。資料完整性的責任在 QC 主管，而非 IT。

Periodic Review（定期回顧）— 常被忽略的要求

EU GMP Annex 11 明確要求對電腦化系統進行定期回顧，GAMP 5 詞彙表也提供了正式定義：

  • 評估文件、程序、記錄和系統效能
  • 確認系統仍處於「已驗證狀態」(validated state)
  • 回顧頻率依系統的複雜性、關鍵性和變更頻率而定

實務建議：建立 Periodic Review SOP，每 1-3 年執行一次，並記錄結果。稽核時若無此記錄，EU 查核員會開立缺失。

如何在查核中引用詞彙表 — 實戰技巧

當稽核員要求定義術語時，標準回應策略：

  • 第一層：引用 GAMP 5 或其引用來源（如 ICH Q9）的官方定義
  • 第二層：解釋該定義如何應用於你的系統或流程
  • 第三層：提供你的 SOP 或驗證文件中如何體現該定義

例如被問到「什麼是 GxP Compliance？」：
「依據 GAMP 5 定義，GxP Compliance 是指符合所有適用的藥品及生命科學法規要求。對我們公司而言，主要適用的法規包括 FDA 21 CFR Parts 211 和 11，以及 EU GMP Annex 11，我們的 VMP 中有詳細說明。」

CDMO 應用提示 — 角色責任的實務安排

典型 CDMO 電腦化系統責任矩陣：

  • MES / ERP：System Owner = IT Director；Process Owner = VP Operations
  • LIMS：System Owner = IT；Process Owner = QC Manager
  • EDMS (文件管理系統)：System Owner = IT；Process Owner = QA Manager
  • 環境監控系統 (EMS)：System Owner = Engineering；Process Owner = QA Manager
  • DCS / PLC：System Owner = Engineering；Process Owner = Manufacturing Manager

建立此矩陣並記錄在 VMP 或系統清單中，是 EU Annex 11 稽核的基本要求。Process Owner 必須實際理解系統功能，而非僅掛名簽署。

Section Summary — 本節重點總結

Appendix G1 — References

  • Over 106 cited documents spanning ISO standards, ICH guidelines, FDA regulations, EU directives, ISPE/GAMP guides, PIC/S, WHO, and ASTM standards.
  • The three pillars of GAMP 5's regulatory framework: 21 CFR Part 11 (US electronic records), EU GMP Annex 11 (EU computerized systems), and ICH Q9 (quality risk management).
  • 21 CFR Part 11 and EU Annex 11 have overlapping but not identical requirements; companies supplying both markets must satisfy the stricter of the two.
  • ICH Q9 provides the scientific foundation for GAMP 5's risk-based approach and defines core risk terminology.
  • When citing GAMP 5 in validation documents, use the full citation: ISPE GAMP 5, Second Edition, 2022, www.ispe.org.

Appendix G2 — Glossary

  • 96 acronyms defined, from AI to XaaS, covering all major GxP and IT terms used in GAMP 5.
  • Key distinction: Verification (ASTM umbrella term) ≥ Validation (life cycle compliance) ≥ Qualification (IQ/OQ/PQ phases).
  • Process Owner owns data integrity; System Owner owns system availability — these are distinct roles with different accountability.
  • Periodic Review is a formal GAMP 5-defined requirement, not optional — it confirms the system remains in a validated state.
  • COTS software has fitness demonstrated by broad commercial use; custom code requires full development life cycle controls.
  • GxP Regulation extends beyond GMP to include GLP, GCP, GDP, GVP, and medical device regulations depending on the business context.

附錄 G1 的 106 份引用文件構成了 GAMP 5 知識體系的法規地基；附錄 G2 的詞彙表則確保所有利害關係人（受管制公司、供應商、稽核員）對相同術語有一致的理解。對 CDMO 而言，精通這些定義是通過 FDA 和 EU 稽查的必要基礎，也是在驗證文件中正確使用專業術語的前提。
